嘉兴 (出生地)

-----end



-----title
衢州
-----detail

-----title
无锡
-----detail
<div class='label1' id='7e699eada3fe40c889be413ef7e41729_label'><a href='javascript: DetailSwitch("7e699eada3fe40c889be413ef7e41729");'><span id='7e699eada3fe40c889be413ef7e41729_link' class='switch'>—</span></a><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1138&endYear=1141')">1138-1141年</a>，16-19岁</div><div id='7e699eada3fe40c889be413ef7e41729' class='detail'><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1138&endYear=1138')">1138年</a>　奉母丧来无锡。在无锡，与僧明有交游。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1139&endYear=1139')">1139年</a>　是年，在无锡，守母丧，与适、遵二兄同习词科课于无锡。外家坟庵巨松结二毬，为二兄登科之祥。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1139&endYear=1139')">1139年</a>　尝与钱伸仲往还，借书问学。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1140&endYear=1141')">1140-1141年</a><br /></div>
-----end



-----title
景德镇
-----detail
<div class='label1' id='20d0cf12dea145798b15aa4fa28248ce_label'><a href='javascript: DetailSwitch("20d0cf12dea145798b15aa4fa28248ce");'><span id='20d0cf12dea145798b15aa4fa28248ce_link' class='switch'>—</span></a><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1142&endYear=1144')">1142-1144年</a>，20-22岁</div><div id='20d0cf12dea145798b15aa4fa28248ce' class='detail'><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1142&endYear=1142')">1142年2月5日</a>　梁竑夫通判江州，迈有送序。作品：送梁竑夫通判江州序。<div id='poem_1256752' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1256752' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1256752?labeling=true' target='_blank'>送梁竑夫通判江州序</a><span class='authorDate'>（1142年2月5日）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 南宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(28601, "南宋", "洪迈", "poem_title_1256752")'>洪迈</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1256752_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1256752'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1256752'>东平梁竑夫六世而下嗣以文鸣，为大龙甲。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1256752_comment'></div>五世祖庄肃公相永昭陵，驯至高曾大父，身荣若庙告，咸都帝师，胙巨邦，信史景钟，垂徽迈烈。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1256752_comment'></div>故竑夫以邃清学士子，年未壮，彻籍中朝，天子以监浔阳郡事。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1256752_comment'></div>所凭厚矣，而窃窃然不得愿，今三十二年。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1256752_comment'></div>诵诗读书，掇拾骚人剩残，自《两京》、《三都》、唐昌黎、河东先生以降，眼之而不置，手之而不释。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1256752_comment'></div>既久且有得，则又设格诸子百氏，扬子云所摈不读者，兼而有之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1256752_comment'></div>厚积以富藏，饫览而腴中，务与瓮牖桑枢者牟，向所固然槩不录，视诡涂并辔，追尾儒先，不暇顾也，而予特幸友之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1256752_comment'></div>一日踵门告曰：「吾父母在是，吾朋从在是，吾愿朝夕焉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1256752_comment'></div>官之长迟吾来，厮舆之卒且至，吾不得留，今别子，子何以幸教」？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1256752_comment'></div>予矍而语曰：今人之称士大夫者，子知之矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1256752_comment'></div>道先王者传经谊，扳儒术，其蔽文而腐；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1256752_comment'></div>业吏道者，熟法制，商功利，其蔽暴而刻。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1256752_comment'></div>自游、夏之文学，圣人不以政事两之，而问宰于莒父，鸣弦于武城，虽有明者不能善其后，古君子大过人者职此。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1256752_comment'></div>今之士起家一官，主簿、尉于某，令、丞于某，地计里以百，民数户以万，欣悴恬愉系焉，乃曰我以文进，此俗吏职耳。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1256752_comment'></div>治中于某，守于某，地之侈，民之夥，视县且十，亦曰我以文进，此俗吏职耳。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1256752_comment'></div>立县若郡者举不自效，数闻有以法制功利自予者，则圜拱而笑之，至使民重足引领，曰某郡有良二千石，某邑有贤大夫，胡不使我幸生此土也！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1256752_comment'></div>由是学者敝民倍蓰于俗吏，不幸而相参会其祸，斯人也不少矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1256752_comment'></div>竑夫侠于文，方将戛青冥，凌阆风，与瀛洲玉堂人曹游，愿先致志于所蔽。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1256752_comment'></div>江干饶山之椒，可以望会，乃日申引导而丁可税也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1256752_comment'></div>举措之必闻，犹鸣鸡吠犬，然尚毋忘今日意。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_19_1256752_comment'></div>竑夫颔此言，则叙而送之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_20_1256752_comment'></div>绍兴十二年二月五日序。</div><div id='poem_sentence_21_1256752_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1142&endYear=1142')">1142年2月</a>　寓南山净慈寺，与伯兄适、仲兄遵同待词科试。迈落选。作品：代枢密使谢赐玉带表、克敌弓铭。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1143&endYear=1143')">1143年8月</a>　父皓归国到阙，命迈作谢赐物劄子。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1143&endYear=1143')">1143年9月</a>　代父作《知饶州谢上表》。作品：有怀大兄正字。<div id='poem_179633' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_179633' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/179633?labeling=true' target='_blank'>有怀大兄正字</a><span class='authorDate'>（1143年9月）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 南宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(28601, "南宋", "洪迈", "poem_title_179633")'>洪迈</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'>五言律诗</div></div><div id='poem_title_179633_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_179633'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_179633'>今日思兄弟，江东望浙东。<div id='poem_sentence_0_179633_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_179633'>别离无奈久，书札且频通。<div id='poem_sentence_1_179633_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_179633'>雨湿芭蕉碧，风乾薜荔红。<div id='poem_sentence_2_179633_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_3_179633'>何时尊酒共，夜语小窗中<span class='inlineComment2'>（宋林表民《天台续集别编》卷五）</span>。<div id='poem_sentence_3_179633_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_4_179633'></div><div id='poem_sentence_4_179633_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1144&endYear=1144')">1144年</a>　作《谢高宗绍兴十四年历日表》<div id='poem_1256691' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1256691' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1256691?labeling=true' target='_blank'>谢绍兴十四年历日表</a><span class='authorDate'>（1144年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 南宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(28601, "南宋", "洪迈", "poem_title_1256691")'>洪迈</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1256691_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1256691'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1256691'>清台课密，上元新甲子之符；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1256691_comment'></div>支郡颁常，正月谨王春之政。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1256691_comment'></div>拜恩喜幸，开卷遵行<span class='inlineComment2'>（中谢。）</span>。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1256691_comment'></div>切以观乎天文，有寒暑杀生之候；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1256691_comment'></div>考之人事，戒析因夷隩之期。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1256691_comment'></div>既水火金木土谷惟修，故度量权衡历算逌出。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1256691_comment'></div>居阳而治，振古如斯。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1256691_comment'></div>洪惟有道之朝，高视无前之迹。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1256691_comment'></div>南司北正，稽颛帝以建官；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1256691_comment'></div>东作西成，宪唐尧之分命。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1256691_comment'></div>爰暨照临之内，举由辅相之宜。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1256691_comment'></div>恭惟皇帝陛下与日并明，参天施教。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1256691_comment'></div>执玉帛者万国，罔不率从；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1256691_comment'></div>班正朔于八荒，无有远迩。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1256691_comment'></div>永念承流而宣化，宜思利用以厚生。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1256691_comment'></div>畀兹一卷之书，俾成四时之吏。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1256691_comment'></div>臣敢不审其作辍，奉以周旋？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1256691_comment'></div>夜寝夙兴，虽莫知于帝力；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1256691_comment'></div>春耕秋歛，誓勉相于农功。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1256691_comment'></div></div><div id='poem_sentence_19_1256691_comment'></div></div></div><br /></div><div class='label1' id='0db8264d9c8b4e85b7ddadd365b8def5_label'><a href='javascript: DetailSwitch("0db8264d9c8b4e85b7ddadd365b8def5");'><span id='0db8264d9c8b4e85b7ddadd365b8def5_link' href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1145&endYear=1145')">1145年11月</a>　回鄱阳乡里，旋又随父南行。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1145&endYear=1145')">1145年11月</a>　有《绍兴府钱清盐场厅壁记》<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1146&endYear=1146')">1146年</a>　侍父乡里。作品：寄题分绣阁。<div id='poem_179682' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_179682' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/179682?labeling=true' target='_blank'>寄题分绣阁</a><span class='authorDate'>（1146年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 南宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(28601, "南宋", "洪迈", "poem_title_179682")'>洪迈</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_179682_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_179682'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_179682'>新阁何隆隆，经营自兹岁。<div id='poem_sentence_0_179682_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_179682'>其前山送青，其下竹交翠。<div id='poem_sentence_1_179682_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_179682'>景物日夕佳，登临春秋异。<div id='poem_sentence_2_179682_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_3_179682'>治中公事暇，领客共留憩。<div id='poem_sentence_3_179682_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_4_179682'>四座欢相酬，寿主珍重意。<div id='poem_sentence_4_179682_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_5_179682'>向来蓬瀛上，视此毋乃愧。<div id='poem_sentence_5_179682_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_6_179682'>主称客意好，是事幸且置。<div id='poem_sentence_6_179682_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_7_179682'>拄颊饱看山，朝来殊爽致<span class='inlineComment2'>（宋陈耆卿《嘉定赤城志》卷五）</span>。<div id='poem_sentence_7_179682_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_8_179682'></div><div id='poem_sentence_8_179682_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1146&endYear=1146')">1146年</a>　有《寄题兄景伯清閟堂》诗。作品：寄题兄景伯清閟堂（昔闻王子猷）<div id='poem_179686' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_179686' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/179686?labeling=true' target='_blank'>清閟堂</a><span class='authorDate'>（1146年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 南宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(28601, "南宋", "洪迈", "poem_title_179686")'>洪迈</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_179686_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_179686'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_179686'>昔闻王子猷，借宅亦种竹。<div id='poem_sentence_0_179686_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_179686'>此君固可喜，人亦清不俗。<div id='poem_sentence_1_179686_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_179686'>伯氏贫而癯，一饭不饱肉。<div id='poem_sentence_2_179686_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_3_179686'>堂前自经始，护此无尽绿。<div id='poem_sentence_3_179686_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_4_179686'>一官岁强半，馀日如转烛。<div id='poem_sentence_4_179686_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_5_179686'>待其长稚子，而已牵归毂。<div id='poem_sentence_5_179686_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_6_179686'>何由享嘉荫，偿我志愿足。<div id='poem_sentence_6_179686_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_7_179686'>应烦彼邦人，日报平安幅<span class='inlineComment2'>（《嘉定赤城志》卷五）</span>。<div id='poem_sentence_7_179686_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1156&endYear=1156')">1156年11月</a>　葬父。<br /></div><div class='label1' id='97369c513017465081345a4cb57e7691_label'><a href='javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1162&endYear=1162')">1162年</a>　是岁秋后，退居乡里。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1162&endYear=1162')">1162年</a>　作《贺加太上尊号表》<br /><a showDetail'><a href='/Writing/179597?labeling=true' target='_blank'>王龟龄王嘉叟木蕴之同过小园用郡圃植花韵</a><span class='authorDate'>（1165年2月）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 南宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(28601, "南宋", "洪迈", "poem_title_179597")'>洪迈</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'>七言律诗</div></div><div id='poem_title_179597_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_179597'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_179597'>节到中和暖尚赊，东风随处起芳华。<div id='poem_sentence_0_179597_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_179597'>自惭翳翳松三径，相对萧萧马五花。<div id='poem_sentence_1_179597_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_179597'>老去醉乡为日月，年来痼疾在烟霞。<div id='poem_sentence_2_179597_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_3_179597'>午桥别墅归公手，早定淮西取白麻<span class='inlineComment2'>（元方回《瀛奎律髓》卷八）</span>。<div id='poem_sentence_3_179597_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_4_179597'></div><div id='poem_sentence_4_179597_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1165&endYear=1165')">1165年</a>　春夏间，与王十朋、陈阜卿、王秬、何麒等结楚东诗社唱和，结集为《楚东唱酬诗》。迈有序。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1165&endYear=1165')">1165年2月25日</a>　和王十朋长篇，十朋用韵以谢。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1165&endYear=1165')">1165年5月25日</a>　与王十朋、王宗丞等饯张孝祥于鄱阳荐福寺。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1165&endYear=1165')">1165年7月9日</a>　友人王十朋自饶州移夔州任，有诗贻迈。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1165&endYear=1165')">1165年</a>　作《扬州重建平山堂记》。<div id='poem_1256825' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1256825' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1256825?labeling=true' target='_blank'>扬州重建平山堂记</a><span class='authorDate'>（1165年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 南宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(28601, "南宋", "洪迈", "poem_title_1256825")'>洪迈</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1256825_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1256825'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1256825'>扬为州最古，南傅海，北犍淮，井而方之盖万里。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1256825_comment'></div>后世乖离鈲析，殆且百郡，独广陵得鼎其名，故常称巨镇，为刺史治所，为总管府，为大都督府，为淮南节度使。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1256825_comment'></div>方唐盛时，全蜀尚列其下，至有「扬一益二」之语。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1256825_comment'></div>入本朝，事权继衰，而太守犹带一道钤辖、安抚使。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1256825_comment'></div>品其域望，他方莫与京也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1256825_comment'></div>迷楼九曲，珠帘十里，二十四桥风月，登临气槩，政已突兀今古。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1256825_comment'></div>兹堂最后出，前志谓江南诸峰植立，檐户肩摩领接，若可拔取。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1256825_comment'></div>山川既佳，而又欧阳公寔张之，故声压宇宙，如揭日月。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1256825_comment'></div>搢绅之东西，以不得到为永恨，意层城、阆风、中天之台抑末耳，其重如此。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1256825_comment'></div>然百馀年间，屡盛屡歇，瓦老木腐，因之以倾陊，荐之以兵革，而遗址离离，无复一存，荒烟白露，苍莽灭没，使人意象萎然，诵「山色有无」之句，付之三叹而已。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1256825_comment'></div>吴兴周侯淙开藩之二年，北边输平，民俗安定，思所以壮隆一邦，作新穷檐。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1256825_comment'></div>乃致志于所谓平山堂者，稽工伐材，费省工倍，四旬而落其成。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1256825_comment'></div>遗民憧憧后先，策老抱幼，目荡魂怡，不自意太平官府之见，至或感以泣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1256825_comment'></div>有客从北来为予言，相与心嘉之，而侯踵书来请记。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1256825_comment'></div>扬为州虽大，然非昔比矣，无有崇台累榭之胜，瑰观佚览之乐，为官者视荫即去，无所寄适，非真有嫪慕不轻得留也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1256825_comment'></div>侯独居之安，居之安则其于事也勇而立。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1256825_comment'></div>一堂之就，似无讳以劳者。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1256825_comment'></div>曩侯为盱眙，予廷劳使客出其间弥两月留。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1256825_comment'></div>留益久，得侯之用心。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1256825_comment'></div>捬摩饥荒中，虽履屐间亦尽善。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_19_1256825_comment'></div>今日典大府，为方伯，休其心于护边乘障之馀，以抗思埃风之外，追昔人而与居，岂不益可嘉？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_20_1256825_comment'></div>则一堂之就，宜有足夸者。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_21_1256825_comment'></div>故为显书之，使淮人时节来游，笙箫舞歌，彷徉乎其上，拂石而镵之，以无忘贤侯之德。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_22_1256825_comment'></div>侯方以功力，奋从是为，羽仪天朝，可卜不疑。</div><div id='poem_sentence_23_1256825_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1166&endYear=1166')">1166年</a>　是年前期，当在鄱阳。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1166&endYear=1166')">1166年5月</a>　序陈确《名臣奏议》。<br /></div><div class='label1' id='41b2ff21020f494385c2f904bbcf061d_label'><a href='javascript: DetailSwitch("41b2ff21020f494385c2f904bbcf061d");'><span id='41b2ff21020f494385c2f904bbcf061d_link' class='switch'>—</span></a><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1169&endYear=1169')">1169年</a>，47岁</div><div id='41b2ff21020f494385c2f904bbcf061d' class='detail'><span style='margin: 0 0.5em; color: gray;'>▪</span>是春，治圃于乡里，与兄适酬唱酣咏于林壑，甚适。<br /><span style='margin: 0 0.5em; color: gray;'>▪</span>为友人向巨源作《临湖阁记》。<div id='poem_1256810' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1256810' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1256810?labeling=true' target='_blank'>临湖阁记</a><span class='authorDate'>（乾道五年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 南宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(28601, "南宋", "洪迈", "poem_title_1256810")'>洪迈</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1256810_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1256810'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1256810'>烛于远者遗于近，廛市之居江与山，燕、越如也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1256810_comment'></div>岂地势则然？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1256810_comment'></div>天实啬之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1256810_comment'></div>予家番城，面澹津三湖，有胜矣，而山不副。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1256810_comment'></div>买小圃撰楼以为高，平林四出，山意如骛，而澄江之境政堕灭没蔽亏中，非霜清木落不见也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1256810_comment'></div>二者不得兼，其难如此。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1256810_comment'></div>吾友向巨源独以书来曰：「自吾卜居南昌，擅东湖之阳，人行湖边，頫大明镜，荷华十里，照影彻目。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1256810_comment'></div>晨霏夕霭，开阖而摩荡，属玉交青，浮游而后先。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1256810_comment'></div>西山横陈，蜿蟺旁薄，空翠长烟，舒惨异状，常若洪崖浮丘翁挹袂拍肩其间。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1256810_comment'></div>凡湖山赋我以佳赏，撩我以瑰观，谓不能俯而有也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1256810_comment'></div>今吾临之以桀阁，崇而为丈者四，去一以为从，益一以为横。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1256810_comment'></div>既成而日登焉，湖之所以为湖，山之所以为山，次且自失，不能嘉遁。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1256810_comment'></div>相与收精会神，俎豆于吾轩楹之间。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1256810_comment'></div>东则十亩之园，池台竹花，输幽呈茂。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1256810_comment'></div>有草堂在湖堤北，其北与西折旋皆山，淡然如修眉，横远可玩而不可狎。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1256810_comment'></div>物色位置，大略似辋川临湖亭，故即而名之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1256810_comment'></div>吾夷犹其上，非更衣就枕不释也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1256810_comment'></div>吾困阨与世不谐偶，一旦独得此，吾心乐焉，愿子为我记」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1256810_comment'></div>予发书疑不信者罙日，私自策曰：巨源诗人也，其词夸。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1256810_comment'></div>是其孑孑来南，仅得边一障，财为郎亟去之，酸寒却扫，于是四年矣，未闻有朽贯腐粟可以汰。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_19_1256810_comment'></div>予从土木之事久，颇解商工费，斯阁也，度不满百万不可止，巨源安有是哉！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_20_1256810_comment'></div>彼特文其滑稽，饷我一笑耳。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_21_1256810_comment'></div>巨源诗人也，其词夸，记未可作。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_22_1256810_comment'></div>会有客从南昌来，为予笑曰：「巨源再为人谀墓，郑重答谢，通得百万钱，妻子睥睨咨晓，规作求田计。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_23_1256810_comment'></div>巨源左遮右绐，如护头目，举以付工师，不留一钱，故其就斯阁也勇之甚。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_24_1256810_comment'></div>书生定可笑，君无庸疑」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_25_1256810_comment'></div>予曰：「诚然。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_26_1256810_comment'></div>又有说于此，有阁如是，将不得以瓦器饮，以一豆饴客，以老无齿婢佐酒。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_27_1256810_comment'></div>巨源其铸黄金之杯，行白玉之柈，唤俦命侣，巽风介月，哀丝豪竹，光妓侍绕，熊蹯豹胎，饫及童骑，倾骇山川之神，日夜鼓舞之，于是为至，敢问策安出」？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_28_1256810_comment'></div>客怃然，予曰：「为我谢巨源，笔尚在足矣」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_29_1256810_comment'></div>乾道五年月日记。</div><div id='poem_sentence_30_1256810_comment'></div></div></div><br /><span style='margin: 0 0.5em; color: gray;'>▪</span>有《西山记》。<div id='poem_1256821' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1256821' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1256821?labeling=true' target='_blank'>西山记</a><span class='authorDate'>（1169年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 南宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(28601, "南宋", "洪迈", "poem_title_1256821")'>洪迈</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1256821_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1256821'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1256821'>天地发育万物，揫成于西，故名山川多西。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1256821_comment'></div>今夫所谓瑶池、昆崙、阆风、县圃，日月之所避隐，神仙之所窟宅，正在流沙、弱水外，中州指为西。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1256821_comment'></div>故其扶舆英淑之气，涣而它之，虽一岩壑、一观台，地无中边，亦莫不尔。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1256821_comment'></div>杭、汉、汝阴之西湖，洪、蜀、永之西山，嘉之蛾眉，巴陵岳阳之楼，黄之临皋，金陵之赏心、白鹭，扬之平山，吴之苏台、茂苑，荆楚之云梦，郢之白雪，滁之琅琊，九江之庾楼，皆延庚挹辛，宾夕阳而导初月，校奇品胜，于登临最宜。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1256821_comment'></div>彼东、北、南岂不或然，仅逮数一二也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1256821_comment'></div>吾邦东有督军湖，南有大江，北有芝山，而重渊复泽，吞包太虚无尽，复举集西偏。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1256821_comment'></div>槃洲、野处之所擅，危当之矣，非有以大表振之，不能以雄夸。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1256821_comment'></div>李阳冰书《山南西道军》额篆笔径二尺，高三十五寸，窃取其两字揭为西山，立亭于道上，出滨洲门者引首即见，当竦然改观也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1256821_comment'></div>起「琼楼」，讫「江月」，巨细二十二扁，皆伯兄丞相隶古所作。</div><div id='poem_sentence_8_1256821_comment'></div></div></div><br /><span style='margin: 0 0.5em; color: gray;'>▪</span>有《欸乃斋记》。<div id='poem_1256834' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1256834' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1256834?labeling=true' target='_blank'>款乃斋记</a><span class='authorDate'>（1169年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 南宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(28601, "南宋", "洪迈", "poem_title_1256834")'>洪迈</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1256834_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1256834'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1256834'>筠坞西限以小关，曰锁松。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1256834_comment'></div>其外地十亩，由郭门至此为最高。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1256834_comment'></div>彭子叔旸得之，转畀予。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1256834_comment'></div>予作小斋，规模广深，与崇桃正等，独于前增一楹以迎雨日。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1256834_comment'></div>正坐所见，已如媚川楼上，信其为最高不疑。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1256834_comment'></div>渔舟常百数，灭没渊泽，棹歌桡音，与波下上，非宫非商，意韵自远，故扁曰「欸乃斋」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1256834_comment'></div>二字本书为「欸乃」，见元次山、柳子厚集中，其音如袄霭。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1256834_comment'></div>涪翁始以欸为欸，虽字异，音则同元、柳。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1256834_comment'></div>相去久远，流传或讹，翁当有所据。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1256834_comment'></div>予尝三游三湘，习闻此歌，至今故髣髴在耳，惜无「一声山水渌」之句，孤负棹船郎。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1256834_comment'></div>柳别本或并二字为𥜊音，又别出一霭字，非也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1256834_comment'></div>斋后两室，窈而深，可受六七客，通曰「桂隐」。</div><div id='poem_sentence_11_1256834_comment'></div></div></div><br /><span style='margin: 0 0.5em; color: gray;'>▪</span>抄《节孝语录》一卷，许及之刊于郡庠。<br /><span style='margin: 0 0.5em; color: gray;'>▪</span>园池题咏，有《琼野录》。<br /><span style='margin: 0 0.5em; color: gray;'>▪</span>有《朝天菊》、《野处亭》诗。作品：朝天菊、野处亭。<div id='poem_179596' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_179596' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/179596?labeling=true' target='_blank'>朝天菊</a><span class='authorDate'>（1169年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 南宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(28601, "南宋", "洪迈", "poem_title_179596")'>洪迈</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'>七言绝句</div></div><div id='poem_title_179596_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_179596'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_179596'>但见荼蘼能上架，那知甘菊解朝天。<div id='poem_sentence_0_179596_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_179596'>亭亭秀出风烟上，冷落东篱却可怜<span class='inlineComment2'>（宋史铸《百菊集谱》卷四）</span>。<div id='poem_sentence_1_179596_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_179596'></div><div id='poem_sentence_2_179596_comment'></div></div></div><div id='poem_179608' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_179608' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/179608?labeling=true' target='_blank'>野处亭</a><span class='authorDate'>（1169年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 南宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(28601, "南宋", "洪迈", "poem_title_179608")'>洪迈</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'>七言律诗</div></div><div id='poem_title_179608_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_179608'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_179608'>莫厌攻台万杵声，芝亭入望得双声。<div id='poem_sentence_0_179608_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_179608'>快邀明月无馀地，俯瞰澄江不碍城。<div id='poem_sentence_1_179608_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_179608'>花雨著人迷杖屦，松风呼梦绕厢荣。<div id='poem_sentence_2_179608_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_3_179608'>弟兄丘壑平生事，付与鸣琴一再行。<div id='poem_sentence_3_179608_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_4_179608'></div><div id='poem_sentence_4_179608_comment'></div></div></div><br /><span style='margin: 0 0.5em; color: gray;'>▪</span>月台成，有诗，兄适、遵有和作。<br /><span style='margin: 0 0.5em; color: gray;'>▪</span>迈是时尚有《喜得安州牡丹》等诗二十余首，皆佚。<br /></div><div class='label1' id='dd75e156d99f42bb9535820293f77b6e_label'><a href='javascript: DetailSwitch("dd75e156d99f42bb9535820293f77b6e");'><span id='dd75e156d99f42bb9535820293f77b6e_link' class='switch'>—</span></a><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1174&endYear=1177')">1174-1177年</a>，52-55岁</div><div id='dd75e156d99f42bb9535820293f77b6e' class='detail'><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1174&endYear=1174')">1174年7月16日</a>　《洪氏世系谱》成，迈序之。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1174&endYear=1174')">1174年11月</a>　仲兄洪遵卒，年五十有五。迈作《行状》。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1175&endYear=1175')">1175年</a>　跋《皇族登科题名》。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1176&endYear=1176')">1176年</a>　是年，在鄱阳。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1176&endYear=1176')">1176年4月</a>　王巨济营修江淮诸道都大提点司成，迈为作记。作品：江淮诸道都大提点司兴造记。<div id='poem_1256813' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1256813' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1256813?labeling=true' target='_blank'>江淮诸道都大提点司兴造记</a><span class='authorDate'>（淳熙三年四月）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 南宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(28601, "南宋", "洪迈", "poem_title_1256813")'>洪迈</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1256813_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1256813'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1256813'>铸钱置使，治所在番阳，不颛职刺举，视若易然。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1256813_comment'></div>然北距淮，南傅海，西接巫、三巴，东际吴闽之会，部郡邑四五百所，分提封半，临制莫盛。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1256813_comment'></div>莞山泽之臧，媪神实主张，是或闲，弗我与。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1256813_comment'></div>引水溉铁，可多为善铜。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1256813_comment'></div>春罙月晴，场人狼顾，至得不补亡，幸而金锡不窳败，薪炭如书，采于山者党不继，辄赤立无册有一千，彼势足落吾事。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1256813_comment'></div>故居位鲜自称，唱为至难，而张官建台亦不常宁，咸尽废而弃他使。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1256813_comment'></div>或民部自领，或出使发运以临之，或分为两，率绵蕝不孰，未少时已复罢，文书益眊渫，大健吏不能观厥终。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1256813_comment'></div>去年春，始复合为一，还都大二名冠其官，著位举吏悉与曩别。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1256813_comment'></div>而上饶君王巨济周因任锡命，弭节于番，再贴四箱毖直，权尊事颛，风采自过，朝夕职其思，间寝食不暂舍。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1256813_comment'></div>亦类有天相，地不靳宝，曲江铅山胆泉至下流成渠，撰分铢小钱，肉好精洁，通数十年来所未有。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1256813_comment'></div>铸尚方刀二万，不调大农一毫费，更籍其赢储上诸，顾瞻后前，殆绝伦配。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1256813_comment'></div>乃言曰：吾为公家毕力当尔，今视吾居以及他，陋之甚，陋之甚，宜将一新之，掌固毋讳以劳。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1256813_comment'></div>我既葺永平之监楼官舍矣，台治巽维，元有堂可燕坐，顾剪为冗屋，敞饰之，扁曰「燕超」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1256813_comment'></div>有两民庐偪垣后，会其来儥，又包以为堂，复文正范公故迹，扁曰「秋香」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1256813_comment'></div>大门正西向侪于闾阎，于仪观弗韪，登以腆直予民。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1256813_comment'></div>买中出之，涂数十丈，作南门复门，端显伉赫，与事体称。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1256813_comment'></div>左立诏书亭，内列掾曹之听，府吏之次，卒徒之区，位置矩度，无小不惬。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1256813_comment'></div>适外间耳闻，俄以告备，迅捷如素，疑于神明。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1256813_comment'></div>于是钟官之故格格无馀韫。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1256813_comment'></div>皆兆于上冬十月，未涉春以成。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_19_1256813_comment'></div>主人大合客，命酒落之，而属予为记。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_20_1256813_comment'></div>予谓天下之事莫时于可为，莫勇于敢为，莫坏于不屑为。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_21_1256813_comment'></div>且官府宫室，蝉联付授，非我嫌欲擅而有之者。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_22_1256813_comment'></div>失今不治，后日之力必倍，尚欲置勿为，渠可得？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_23_1256813_comment'></div>巨济独从容谈笑，不动声气，力半而功倍蓰，直若不足为，人之赋才相万里不疑明甚。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_24_1256813_comment'></div>予既著其事，且推本其所以难之故，使后人可考。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_25_1256813_comment'></div>巨济受知圣天子，行身都剧，寄为国力，讫于大有为而后止，其将不一书。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_26_1256813_comment'></div>予羞，非文章家，然记事多矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_27_1256813_comment'></div>淳熙三年夏四月十六日记。</div><div id='poem_sentence_28_1256813_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1176&endYear=1176')">1176年11月</a>　张子颜刻《元和郡县志》，迈序之。作品：元和郡县志序。<span class='inlineComment2'>（《夷坚丁志》二十卷盖成于是年。）</span><div id='poem_1256770' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1256770' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1256770?labeling=true' target='_blank'>元和郡县志后序</a><span class='authorDate'>（淳熙三年十一月）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 南宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(28601, "南宋", "洪迈", "poem_title_1256770")'>洪迈</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1256770_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1256770'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1256770'>右，《元和郡县志》四十卷，目录二卷，唐元和八年丞相李赵公吉甫所上也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1256770_comment'></div>后三百六十有三年，今京西牧待制张公几仲始刻版于襄阳幕府。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1256770_comment'></div>按《新唐书·艺文志》著录，是书为五十四卷，《会要》析而两之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1256770_comment'></div>一曰《州县郡国图》三十卷，一曰《郡国图》，其卷与《新志》同，皆冠以元和。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1256770_comment'></div>三者了不相似，以今所刻證之皆非也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1256770_comment'></div>地理之最，莫切于图书，《周官》职方氏掌天下之图，要周知其利害。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1256770_comment'></div>沛公入关，萧何收秦丞相府图籍，具知阨塞户口多少强弱处，基汉为雄。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1256770_comment'></div>光武与邓禹论天下郡国，亦披舆地图乃克见。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1256770_comment'></div>则不出户庭而九州万里在吾目中，如策马并辔，援衣挈领，舍此谁则！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1256770_comment'></div>然方赵公为相，强藩悍帅狃贞元馀习，擅地自予，朝廷莫敢诃，而能以期年间易三十六镇。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1256770_comment'></div>魏田季安病，公请以滑任薛平，戍重兵邢洺，因图上河北险要。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1256770_comment'></div>宪宗张于浴堂门壁，每叹曰：「朕日按图，信如卿料」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1256770_comment'></div>则其所著书盖已见之行事矣，岂直区区纸上语而已哉！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1256770_comment'></div>几仲先忠烈王勋在彝鼎，为中兴社稷臣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1256770_comment'></div>几仲济美称家，文史声猷，有晋宋胜流风度。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1256770_comment'></div>方守国西门，雍容缓带，蹑叔子、元凯故迹。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1256770_comment'></div>一旦天子读此书，悼河山之独西，想燕冀而忼慨，眷焉北顾，思有所出，赵营平不必驰至金城，图上方略，马伏波不必聚米为山，指画形势。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1256770_comment'></div>几仲知之矣，予愿拭目焉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1256770_comment'></div>本作书之旨，则赵公之叙固在，今揭于篇首。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1256770_comment'></div>淳熙三年十一月，番阳洪迈书。</div><div id='poem_sentence_19_1256770_comment'></div></div><div class='poemNote' id='poem_note_1256770'><span class='label'>按：</span>《元和郡县志》卷首，文渊阁四库全书本。<br /></div><div id='poem_note_1256770_comment'></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1177&endYear=1177')">1177年7月6日</a>　跋《睢阳五老图》。作品：睢阳五老图卷跋。<div id='poem_1256791' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1256791' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1256791?labeling=true' target='_blank'>跋睢阳五老图</a><span class='authorDate'>（淳熙四年七月）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 南宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(28601, "南宋", "洪迈", "poem_title_1256791")'>洪迈</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1256791_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1256791'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1256791'>仁义之人，其言蔼如；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1256791_comment'></div>道德之人，其言穆如。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1256791_comment'></div>观此图像，诵此赓章，虽至细人，宁有不肃拜敛衽者！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1256791_comment'></div>大司农卿寿至九十有四，又于五公为最高，而希文克承先德，宗尚其事，真毕司农孙矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1256791_comment'></div>淳熙四年七月六日，鄱阳洪迈敬书。</div><div id='poem_sentence_4_1256791_comment'></div></div></div><br /></div><div class='label1' id='db72132d4de248529463cfea1a641876_label'><a href='javascript: DetailSwitch("db72132d4de248529463cfea1a641876");'><span id='db72132d4de248529463cfea1a641876_link' class='switch'>—</span></a><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1197&endYear=1202')">1197-1202年</a>，75-80岁</div><div id='db72132d4de248529463cfea1a641876' class='detail'><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1197&endYear=1197')">1197年4月9日</a>　序朱翌《猗觉寮杂记》。作品：猗觉寮杂记序。<div id='poem_1256782' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1256782' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1256782?labeling=true' target='_blank'>猗觉寮杂记序<span class='inlineComment2'>（庆元三年四月）</span></a><span class='authorDate'>（1197年4月9日）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 南宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(28601, "南宋", "洪迈", "poem_title_1256782")'>洪迈</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1256782_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1256782'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1256782'>右，上下两卷，凡四百三十五则，故紫微舍人桐乡朱先生公所记也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1256782_comment'></div>先生嗜学如渴之须饮，饥之须食，所谓以图史文章为园囿鼓吹者，盖无时不论著。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1256782_comment'></div>在曲江五闰久，闭关谢客。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1256782_comment'></div>正流落谪徙，力不能多载书，人家又非一瓻可借，素手无挟，栖迟僧房，独伥伥穷经考古，砭刮疵病，校量草木虫鱼，上掸骚雅，旁弋史传，證引竺乾龙汉诸章，下及琐录稗说，左掇右𠠒，悉为吾用，识测意见，超阅众甫，每一转语就，学者争先快睹。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1256782_comment'></div>方惕若避谤，不肯轻为人言，惟诸郎过庭，时得剽听。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1256782_comment'></div>善恶天定，然后始收拾汇次，绪成一编。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1256782_comment'></div>迈与文惠、文安两兄时省觐真阳，岁必过韶，踵门内谒，先生视如通家子弟，引而馆之，赐之诗，有曰：「彭蠡春生万顷湖，光明相映棣华柎。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1256782_comment'></div>鹓雏鷟鸑俱为凤，乳酪醍醐总是酥」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1256782_comment'></div>忽忽五十年，仲子軧通守赣，刊此书，使为之序。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1256782_comment'></div>泰山毫芒，昔者窃闻之矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1256782_comment'></div>文惠丐发明《隶释》，答之云：「尝作一书，如诗话之类，辨證古今数百事，目之《猗觉寮记》，他日求数字冠篇首，使信于人，托以传永」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1256782_comment'></div>呜呼，孰知不及为而顾以见属？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1256782_comment'></div>悲夫！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1256782_comment'></div>庆元三年四月九日，焕章阁学士、宣奉大夫、魏郡公番阳洪迈序。</div><div id='poem_sentence_13_1256782_comment'></div></div><div class='poemNote' id='poem_note_1256782'><span class='label'>按：</span>《猗觉寮杂记》卷首，文渊阁四库全书本。<br /></div><div id='poem_note_1256782_comment'></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1197&endYear=1197')">1197年5月14日</a>　《夷坚支癸》成，序之。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1197&endYear=1197')">1197年</a>　尝得双雁于衢人郑伯膺，置之云壑。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1197&endYear=1197')">1197年9月24日</a>　《容斋四笔》成，序之。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1197&endYear=1197')">1197年</a>　为甘叔怀作《碧崖修造疏》。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1197&endYear=1197')">1197年12月1日</a>　序娄机《汉隶字原》。作品：汉隶字原序。<div id='poem_1256783' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1256783' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1256783?labeling=true' target='_blank'>汉隶字源序<span class='inlineComment2'>（庆元三年十二月）</span></a><span class='authorDate'>（1197年12月1日）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 南宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(28601, "南宋", "洪迈", "poem_title_1256783")'>洪迈</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1256783_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1256783'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1256783'>《汉隶字源》六帙，槜李娄君彦发所辑也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1256783_comment'></div>其书甚清，其抒意甚勇，其考赜甚精，其立说甚当，其沾丐后学甚笃。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1256783_comment'></div>凡见诸石刻，若壶鼎刀镜盆槃洗甓，著录者三百有九。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1256783_comment'></div>起东京建武，讫鸿都建安，殆二百年。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1256783_comment'></div>滥觞于魏者仅卅而一，光和骨立，开元赑屃。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1256783_comment'></div>点画之炉锤，法度之宎奥，假借之同而异，发纵之简而古，合蔡中郎诸人笔力通神之妙，皆聚此编。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1256783_comment'></div>忆吾兄文惠公自壮至老，耽癖弗懈，尝区别为五种书，曰释、曰缵、曰韵、曰图、曰续。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1256783_comment'></div>四者备矣，唯韵书不成。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1256783_comment'></div>以为蠹竭目力，于摹写至难觱，旦旦而求之，字字而仿之，虽众史堵廧，孙甥鱼贯，不堪替一笔也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1256783_comment'></div>功之弗就，使获睹是书，且悉循其《隶释》次第，志之所底，不谒而同，正应𢥠然起立，兴不得并时之叹。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1256783_comment'></div>彦发曩岁有《班马字类》，突过诸家汉史之学，予尝序之矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1256783_comment'></div>今此帙刊于高明台，方通守吾州，朱墨鲜暇。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1256783_comment'></div>趣了官事竟，辄萧然一室中。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1256783_comment'></div>厮舆侧睨，但见其放策欠伸，搔头揩眼，而用心独苦之状，固所不克知。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1256783_comment'></div>彦发溯学有原委，工词章，身端行治，名最三吴，而诸公贵人不解收拾，使周鼎斡弃，与康瓠等。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1256783_comment'></div>予顷备侍从，承清问于燕閒，宣昭声光宜不辞费，顾亦不能一出诸口，心焉负愧，聊复再畅叙以自释云。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1256783_comment'></div>庆元三年十二月朔旦，野处洪景卢序。</div><div id='poem_sentence_16_1256783_comment'></div></div><div class='poemNote' id='poem_note_1256783'><span class='label'>按：</span>《汉隶字源》卷首，影印文渊阁四库全书本。<br /></div><div id='poem_note_1256783_comment'></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1197&endYear=1197')">1197年</a>　是年，《夷坚支辛》、《支壬》、《支癸》、《三甲》、《三乙》、《三景》、《三丁》诸志成。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1197&endYear=1197')">1197年</a>　鄱阳芝山寺僧欲建华严阁，请迈作《华严阁劝缘疏》。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1197&endYear=1197')">1197年</a>　有《赘稿》三十八卷。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1198&endYear=1198')">1198年</a>　初春一日，黄裳折红梅相示。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1198&endYear=1198')">1198年</a>　《夷坚三戊》成。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1198&endYear=1198')">1198年4月1日</a>　《夷坚三己》成，序之。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1198&endYear=1198')">1198年</a>　《夷坚三庚》成。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1198&endYear=1198')">1198年6月8日</a>　《夷坚三辛》成，序之。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1198&endYear=1198')">1198年9月6日</a>　《夷坚三壬》成，序之。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1198&endYear=1198')">1198年</a>　《夷坚三癸》成。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1198&endYear=1198')">1198年</a>　再上章告老，进龙图阁学士。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1198&endYear=1198')">1198年</a>　作《怡斋记》。作品：怡斋记。<span class='inlineComment2'>（未知马遂良三十七岁为何年，姑系之于其卒年。）</span><div id='poem_1256824' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1256824' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1256824?labeling=true' target='_blank'>怡斋记</a><span class='authorDate'>（1198年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 南宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(28601, "南宋", "洪迈", "poem_title_1256824")'>洪迈</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1256824_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1256824'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1256824'>马子遂良馆予宇下六百日，宿庐直客斋不能十步，语出口辄入予耳，故寓客无敢不公言。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1256824_comment'></div>今日余方写《楚词》，倦困枕肱卧，闻遂良与客对，始哫訾呫嗫不可听，已则放声棘谈，往复甚苦。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1256824_comment'></div>予蹑履蔽隐候伺，则遂良正东向拈篆笔，自作「怡斋」字。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1256824_comment'></div>何人长髯广额，秀眉箕口，倨坐其西，诘所以曰：「自而之去亲戚，远坟墓，行游四方有年矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1256824_comment'></div>谨岁时归休觐父母，再拜寒温罢，入室剌剌与妻子语，劳苦平生，百未一厌，复别去，上马恝然，无一分乐易色。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1256824_comment'></div>行年三十七，拄腹五千卷书，未能合有司度程，掇取一第。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1256824_comment'></div>耿耿栖栖，不自聊赖。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1256824_comment'></div>顾方以怡自满，傲睨容膝之室，得微大欺我欤？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1256824_comment'></div>敢问吾子所以怡者何事，而谓斋者果安在哉」？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1256824_comment'></div>遂良且笑且怒，瞪对之曰：「子貌则士也，夫何言之陋？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1256824_comment'></div>方吾家居，入怡颜以事父母，出怡色以与兄弟处，暇时读书以怡吾心。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1256824_comment'></div>食与口怡，寝与体怡，吾穷到骨矣，而其怡常自若也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1256824_comment'></div>旦吾游越则越为吾庐，暮吾游燕则燕为吾庐。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1256824_comment'></div>在吾室为吾斋固也，出而见子，坐子之舍，亦吾斋也，孰宾孰主哉？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1256824_comment'></div>何言之陋」！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1256824_comment'></div>语未既，予立听不暇久，疾出揖二子曰：「客则失矣，而主人亦未为得也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1256824_comment'></div>今人在贫贱而不失怡于布衣，在富贵而万钟不能怡也，亦几矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1256824_comment'></div>虽然，之二者于道由九牛一毛也，尚何足论？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1256824_comment'></div>天地大蘧庐也，曾不足以隘我，尚何燕越之间与？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1256824_comment'></div>闭口亟休，勿复言之」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_19_1256824_comment'></div>客舌举不得下，惝恍自失，意若欲遁而足不可引。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_20_1256824_comment'></div>予笑曰：「予亦多言耳，子何为而去」？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_21_1256824_comment'></div>顾侍奴取酒引满，径醉就睡。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_22_1256824_comment'></div>有顷，醒视之，独予、遂良在，客去矣。</div><div id='poem_sentence_23_1256824_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1198&endYear=1198')">1198年</a>　作《大死庵记》。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1199&endYear=1199')">1199年</a>　春，有人建议用洪迈与陆游修史，但为当路所沮，事遂寝。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1199&endYear=1199')">1199年</a>　《夷坚四甲》、《四乙》成。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1199&endYear=1199')">1199年</a>　《容斋五笔》成。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1199&endYear=1199')">1199年</a>　友人徐梦莘儒荣堂成，洪迈有诗相贺。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1200&endYear=1200')">1200年</a>　余镛刻唐王贞白《灵溪集》，请迈作《序》。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1200&endYear=1200')">1200年</a>　徐国润卒，迈为作墓志。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1201&endYear=1201')">1201年</a>　为余镛作《松风阁记》。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1202&endYear=1202')">1202年</a>　以端明殿学士致仕，未几卒。赠光禄大夫，谥文敏。<br /></div>
-----end

id='poem_sentence_14_179663_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_15_179663'>郫筒无惜醉，岷芋且加餐。<div id='poem_sentence_15_179663_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_16_179663'>乡曲沾投分，蓬莱忝备官。<div id='poem_sentence_16_179663_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_17_179663'>丹心空自喜，青眼独相看。<div id='poem_sentence_17_179663_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_18_179663'>此地从公别，何时话夜阑。<div id='poem_sentence_18_179663_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_19_179663'>归来消息近，鹏背一朝抟<span class='inlineComment2'>（同上书卷一一）</span>。<div id='poem_sentence_19_179663_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_20_179663'></div><div id='poem_sentence_20_179663_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1159&endYear=1159')">1159年2月25日</a>　奏减斥堠。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1159&endYear=1159')">1159年4月6日</a>　以秘书省校书郎兼国史院编修官。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1159&endYear=1159')">1159年6月15日</a>　史浩为秘書郎兼普安恩平郡王府教授，辞谢劄子曾举洪迈充代。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1159&endYear=1159')">1159年闰6月26日</a>　草任质言子恩泽诏。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1159&endYear=1159')">1159年7月</a>　敕令所删定官闻人滋请岁于改官员中差减员数，迈等言此法有弊，乃止。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1159&endYear=1159')">1159年8月</a>　除吏部员外郎。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1159&endYear=1159')">1159年12月5日</a>　召对，论本朝尤重告老之制。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1159&endYear=1159')">1159年</a>　奏请自今凡天下凶盗及杂犯杀人罪应至死而赦之者，量地里逺近，分配大军。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1160&endYear=1160')">1160年</a>　年初，有《追和玉版诗》、《四白诗》、《五白诗》等，王十朋有和诗。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1160&endYear=1160')">1160年1月</a>　充省试参详官，主司委出词科题。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1160&endYear=1160')">1160年1月14日</a>　鲍彪告老，迈与有司陈情旌表。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1160&endYear=1160')">1160年3月7日</a>　移礼部员外郎。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1160&endYear=1160')">1160年5月</a>　王龟龄自著作丞外补，迈有诗相送。作品：送王龟龄自著作丞外补。<div id='poem_179603' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_179603' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/179603?labeling=true' target='_blank'>送王龟龄自著作丞外补</a><span class='authorDate'>（1160年5月）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 南宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(28601, "南宋", "洪迈", "poem_title_179603")'>洪迈</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'>七言律诗</div></div><div id='poem_title_179603_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_179603'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_179603'>不奈诸公厌石渠，年年送客意何如。<div id='poem_sentence_0_179603_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_179603'>直言饱诵刘蕡策，大意争传贾谊书。<div id='poem_sentence_1_179603_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_179603'>今日朝廷唯主圣，异时风俗要人锄。<div id='poem_sentence_2_179603_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_3_179603'>须君早晚归遗补，莫恋王门久曳裾<sup class='reference inlineComment2'>⑴</sup>。<div id='poem_sentence_3_179603_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_4_179603'></div><div id='poem_sentence_4_179603_comment'></div></div><div class='poemNote' id='poem_note_179603'><div class='inline1'><div id='poem_sentence_3_179603_0'>⑴ 元富大用《古今事文类聚新集》卷三○</div></div></div><div id='poem_note_179603_comment'></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1160&endYear=1160')">1160年7月6日</a>　以礼部员外郎再兼国史院编修官。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1160&endYear=1160')">1160年</a>　撰《礼部郎官厅壁记》。<div id='poem_1256807' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1256807' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1256807?labeling=true' target='_blank'>礼部郎官厅壁记<span class='inlineComment2'>（绍兴三十年七月）</span></a><span class='authorDate'>（1160年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 南宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(28601, "南宋", "洪迈", "poem_title_1256807")'>洪迈</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1256807_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1256807'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1256807'>钧之为郎，然二十四司，冷热剧易不得同日语。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1256807_comment'></div>中兴时，捐不急之官，省郎员七，以主客合于礼部，号为两曹，而所掌犹不过笺削印瑞郊庙礼文与士子科举事，日所程判，其多不能以百。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1256807_comment'></div>天明省门开，繇大丞相以下毕入听治。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1256807_comment'></div>吾同舍郎南典选，北理财，文书鳞午，吏四绕不少置，独仪曹之廷可设翳罔。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1256807_comment'></div>予方理蠹简，呻呫毕，作书生事业。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1256807_comment'></div>倦则偃一榻上，迟食时矍起，摩睡眼以出，卒食，舒舒而行，伺丞相上马已即去，至无毫毛可用以为勤，以白长官者。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1256807_comment'></div>其官同，禄之入又同，而佚劳相绝顾如此，颜之不厚难矣哉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1256807_comment'></div>厅壁当有记，以谨岁月，识名氏，今亡有也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1256807_comment'></div>问诸掌故，掌故不知，盖其官閒，其吏缓，閒与缓相遭，茍且颓靡，非一日实然。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1256807_comment'></div>予访老吏，质太史，越数月而后颇得其梗槩。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1256807_comment'></div>乃探建炎以来至于今日，自祖秀实始并书，其幸甚云。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1256807_comment'></div>绍兴三十年七月八日记。</div><div id='poem_sentence_11_1256807_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1160&endYear=1160')">1160年9月21日</a>　撰《礼部尚书题名记》。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1160&endYear=1160')">1160年9月19日</a>　显仁皇后小祥，迈为礼部作请吉服奏。高宗居显仁皇后丧，当孟享，礼官不知所从，迈请遣宰相分祭，奏可。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1160&endYear=1160')">1160年10月2日</a>　序伯兄适《砚说》。作品：砚说序。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1160&endYear=1160')">1160年11月</a>　兼枢密院检详文字。每有建言，枢密重之。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1160&endYear=1160')">1160年</a>　在史馆，尝作《省中红梅》诗，王十朋、周必大等有和诗。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1161&endYear=1161')">1161年1月</a>　作《贺谢完颜亮表》。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1161&endYear=1161')">1161年2月4日</a>　与馆阁诸公饯别胡宪。诸公赋诗，迈序之。作品：馆阁送胡正字诗序。<div id='poem_1256754' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1256754' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1256754?labeling=true' target='_blank'>馆阁送胡正字诗序<span class='inlineComment2'>（绍兴三十一年二月）</span></a><span class='authorDate'>（1161年2月4日）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 南宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(28601, "南宋", "洪迈", "poem_title_1256754")'>洪迈</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1256754_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1256754'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1256754'>前二年，诏起胡先生于建安以司直廷尉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1256754_comment'></div>先生辞曰：「臣宪老矣，春秋七十有四，居山林堇堇自足。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1256754_comment'></div>官于朝非壮有力而材者不可，臣老矣，谊不得奉诏」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1256754_comment'></div>天子揽其章，换以中秘书官，使无累职事，益自养。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1256754_comment'></div>先生不得辞，来。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1256754_comment'></div>来数月，又请曰：「臣不能使老复少，今形容旅力又不逮在前时，而陛下留臣无为也」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1256754_comment'></div>于是宰相言胡宪半世为官，进不能以寸，愿加宠秩之，益广圣世贵老养贤之义。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1256754_comment'></div>即日拜八品京官，予祠禄使归。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1256754_comment'></div>归有日，馆阁之士八人举故事，载酒殽祖之于国东门之外，相属赋诗。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1256754_comment'></div>番阳洪迈独拱手言曰：先生之去美，而其所以去则不可。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1256754_comment'></div>夫翘关负乘，击剑驰马，加一日之老亦惫耳，况过七十者乎？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1256754_comment'></div>至于雍容在廷，标榜后进，坐乎安车蒲轮之上，惧不能老而已。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1256754_comment'></div>而先生去之，是使黄发皤皤之士终不一朝居也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1256754_comment'></div>且陛下择官以处，奉钱廪粟。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1256754_comment'></div>岁时诸恩泽甚厚，非所谓无人子思之侧者；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1256754_comment'></div>满朝贤大夫注意高仰，无公孙子侧目辕固之嫌；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1256754_comment'></div>儒生文士执弟子礼，恐不得一解颜笑，无有骊驹狗曲之诮。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1256754_comment'></div>而先生居之若不释然者，往来屑屑，不惮烦于道路。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1256754_comment'></div>吾党之士未有所闻于先生，若之何？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1256754_comment'></div>同舍生唶曰：「畴昔之岁，先生且对延英，以病告，上书公车，卓卓然五千言，今皆略施行。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_19_1256754_comment'></div>其有补于朝廷多矣，子之云云柰何」？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_20_1256754_comment'></div>迈竦然曰：迈有罪。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_21_1256754_comment'></div>酒阑以往，诸公诗且成，迈醉不遮，愧不暇诗，独序其所以然者。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_22_1256754_comment'></div>绍兴三十一年二月四日序。</div><div id='poem_sentence_23_1256754_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1161&endYear=1161')">1161年3月7日</a>　为枢密检详，多所建言。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1161&endYear=1161')">1161年3月9日</a>　为尚书郎。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1161&endYear=1161')">1161年4月23日</a>　奏车驾行幸劄子。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1161&endYear=1161')">1161年5月9日</a>　作《梧州府学记》。<div id='poem_1256833' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1256833' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1256833?labeling=true' target='_blank'>重建梧州府学记</a><span class='authorDate'>（1161年5月9日）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 南宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(28601, "南宋", "洪迈", "poem_title_1256833")'>洪迈</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1256833_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1256833'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1256833'>服岭而南，以千里名州者三十七，缭以大海。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1256833_comment'></div>其山则罗浮、桂林、阳朔、韶石诸峰，皆扶舆崭秀，有仙者窟宅；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1256833_comment'></div>水则昭潭、武溪、浔滩、真湟，沦涟清泻，可鉴毛发。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1256833_comment'></div>至于光灵纡馀，发为草木之祥，如水沉都梁，素馨之葩，芗气郁烈。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1256833_comment'></div>象犀玳瑁珠琲之凑，穷天下之产不足以掩之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1256833_comment'></div>都会盖如此，独人物效奇，闇然弗章。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1256833_comment'></div>由唐至今五六百年之间，卓然于时者，曲江张文献公、余襄公、日南姜公而已尔。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1256833_comment'></div>是岂山川炳灵精采，荡于异物，使魁奇伟丽之气不淑诸人耶，何其略无而仅有也！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1256833_comment'></div>余尝游南方，私为其人太息。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1256833_comment'></div>盖闽、蜀与粤，是三者均所谓斗绝不毛之区，而蜀移于文翁，闽变于常衮，今言多士者指二部为甲乙。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1256833_comment'></div>惟粤独不幸，无良二千石心乎教化者尸盟之，至环地万里而漠然自外于上国。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1256833_comment'></div>苍梧自汉为郡，入本朝有陈公恭、梁庄肃为之守，其风声气俗直出他郡。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1256833_comment'></div>顾学校褊陋，不常厥居，于山之巅，于冰井，于鳄鱼池。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1256833_comment'></div>其后逼于县舍科诏取士，又不于其乡而于浔于容，最后葺于僧房。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1256833_comment'></div>白袍纷纷，移徙之不暇，奚暇诵诗读书，以倡其心！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1256833_comment'></div>今任侯为州，独齐鲁其民，顾瞻校宫，以为当迁。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1256833_comment'></div>为诸生相攸宜而得神霄宫之旧址，高明有亢，龟食其墨，礼殿斋庐，闳严静深，厢庑门庖，秩秩井井，又作议道堂以待三岁角材之地，并之为八十一楹。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1256833_comment'></div>经始于旧年之仲冬，断手于今兹之仲春。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1256833_comment'></div>木出于山，贾人不知；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1256833_comment'></div>费出于公而乐助者四十一乡，民不知；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_19_1256833_comment'></div>工出于邻邦，州兵不知。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_20_1256833_comment'></div>规模奕然，粤中无足与比。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_21_1256833_comment'></div>既成，侯作书请记。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_22_1256833_comment'></div>余谓士者自修于穷闾之间，而待举于朝廷之上，虽羹藜饭糗，颛颛于寂寞之滨，固有穷乏其身而安之者，此其志岂一朝一夕之为哉！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_23_1256833_comment'></div>有屋以居，有粟而食，用其藏修游息之暇，以求夫存心养性之道，圣贤阃奥，直阶而升尔，一第常也，何足以慁我为哉！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_24_1256833_comment'></div>诸士子其勉之，必有不期然者。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_25_1256833_comment'></div>侯名诏，眉山人，尝令豫章之进贤。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_26_1256833_comment'></div>余行其涂，得歌谣于田里间，又尝过侯清江之居而为之赋凌风阁者，然则记学之成，所不得辞也。</div><div id='poem_sentence_27_1256833_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1161&endYear=1161')">1161年10月1日</a>　高宗亲征，迈草诏。作品：辛巳亲征诏。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1161&endYear=1161')">1161年10月8日</a>　南宋檄四夷诸国及河北等路，迈草檄文。作品：淮南浙西江东西制置使告契丹诸国及中原檄。<div id='poem_1256740' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1256740' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1256740?labeling=true' target='_blank'>刘锜等檄契丹西夏高丽渤海鞑靼诸国及河北河东等路书<span class='inlineComment2'>（绍兴三十一年十月）</span></a><span class='authorDate'>（1161年10月8日）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 南宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(28601, "南宋", "洪迈", "poem_title_1256740")'>洪迈</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1256740_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1256740'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1256740'>太尉、威武军节度使、淮南浙西江东制置使刘锜，庆远军节度使、神龙卫四厢都指挥使、京湖制置使成闵，少保、奉国军节度使、四川宣抚使吴璘，檄告契丹、西夏、高丽、渤海、鞑靼诸国及我河北、河东、陕西、京东、河朔等道官吏军民等：盖闻惟天无亲，作不善者神弗赦；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1256740_comment'></div>得道多助，仗大义者众必归。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1256740_comment'></div>敢摅一切之诚，用谂万方之听。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1256740_comment'></div>我国家功高上古，泽润中区。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1256740_comment'></div>列圣重光，方启升平之运；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1256740_comment'></div>斯民不幸，适丁板荡之灾。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1256740_comment'></div>蠢兹女真之微，首覆契丹之祀，怙其新造，间我不虞，妖氛既陷于神都，虐焰殆弥于宇县。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1256740_comment'></div>两宫北狩，讫罹胡地之烟尘；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1256740_comment'></div>大驾南巡，未正汉京之日月。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1256740_comment'></div>凡居率土，谊不戴天。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1256740_comment'></div>主上绍开中兴，宏济大业，望山河而陨涕，瞻陵庙以伤心。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1256740_comment'></div>盖卧薪尝胆之是图，宁拯溺救焚之敢缓？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1256740_comment'></div>然以人命至重，嘉兵不祥，靡辞屈己以事雠，姑欲安民而和众。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1256740_comment'></div>岂彼冥顽之虏，狃于篡逆之资，以至不仁，行大不道！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1256740_comment'></div>驱我中原之老稚，剪为异类之囚俘。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1256740_comment'></div>乃轻弃于穴巢，辄坐张于畿甸。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1256740_comment'></div>自谓富彊之莫敌，公然反覆以见欺。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1256740_comment'></div>指挥而取将相之臣，谈笑以求汉淮之地。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1256740_comment'></div>九州四海，闻之怒发以冲冠；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1256740_comment'></div>百将三军，谁不搴旗而抵掌？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_19_1256740_comment'></div>幕府滥膺齐钺，尽护戎旃，冀凭宗社之威灵，一洗穹庐之秽孽，待时而动，历岁于兹。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_20_1256740_comment'></div>天亡此胡，使之委身而送死；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_21_1256740_comment'></div>人自为战，誓不与贼以俱生。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_22_1256740_comment'></div>帝座一临，士气百倍。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_23_1256740_comment'></div>刘制置悉南徐之甲，成马军兴侍卫之师。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_24_1256740_comment'></div>李四厢虎视于青、徐，王太尉鹰扬于颍、寿。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_25_1256740_comment'></div>骑师捣殽函之险，步军冲伊洛之郊。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_26_1256740_comment'></div>兵多坚锋，勇有馀愤。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_27_1256740_comment'></div>以此制敌，何敌不摧？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_28_1256740_comment'></div>以此攻城，何城不克？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_29_1256740_comment'></div>惟彼诸蕃之大国，久为钜宋之欢邻。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_30_1256740_comment'></div>玉帛交驰，尚忆百年之信誓；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_31_1256740_comment'></div>封疆迥隔，顿违两地之邮音。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_32_1256740_comment'></div>愿敦继好之规，共作侮亡之举。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_33_1256740_comment'></div>至于秦晋奇士，齐赵隽材，抱节义之良谟，志功名之嘉会。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_34_1256740_comment'></div>为刘氏左袒，饱闻思汉之忠；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_35_1256740_comment'></div>徯汤后东征，必慰戴商之望。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_36_1256740_comment'></div>抗旌云合，投袂风从。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_37_1256740_comment'></div>或据郡以迎锋，或聚徒而特起，乘兹破竹之势，立尔剪茅之勋。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_38_1256740_comment'></div>侯王宁有种乎，人皆可致；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_39_1256740_comment'></div>富贵是所欲也，时不再来。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_40_1256740_comment'></div>更期父老之诲言，深念祖宗之德化，勿忘旧主，重建丕基。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_41_1256740_comment'></div>檄到如前，书不尽意。</div><div id='poem_sentence_42_1256740_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1161&endYear=1161')">1161年10月19日</a>　知枢密院事叶义问督视江淮荆襄军马，洪迈主管机宜文字，参议军事。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1161&endYear=1161')">1161年</a>　《夷坚甲志》二十卷，盖成于是年。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1162&endYear=1162')">1162年1月9日</a>　守尚书左司员外郎，兼权行在检详。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1162&endYear=1162')">1162年1月15日</a>　与史浩、马德骏、薛季益、冯圆中、汪中嘉等游蒋山，唱酬甚乐。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1162&endYear=1162')">1162年1月22日</a>　金遣使来告登位。洪迈充接伴使。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1162&endYear=1162')">1162年1月24日</a>　接伴到扬州，有奏。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1162&endYear=1162')">1162年1月25日</a>　洪迈入对，高宗谓土地为上，名分次之。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1162&endYear=1162')">1162年1月28日</a>　接伴使洪迈、张抡辞行。高宗赞曰：“洪皓三子，其才皆可用。”<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1162&endYear=1162')">1162年2月23日</a>　接伴过北界。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1162&endYear=1162')">1162年2月</a>　刘錡卒，迈作神道碑。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1162&endYear=1162')">1162年闰2月</a>　金使责臣礼及求新复四郡，迈移书折之。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1162&endYear=1162')">1162年3月6日</a>　洪迈、张抡奏言接伴变更旧例事件。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1162&endYear=1162')">1162年3月11日</a>　洪迈接伴北使还，入见。奏北使游观似不必禁。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1162&endYear=1162')">1162年3月14日</a>　因接伴，转一官。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1162&endYear=1162')">1162年3月21日</a>　时议遣使报金国聘，洪迈慨然请行，充贺大金登宝位国信使，欲令金称兄弟敌国而归河南地。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1162&endYear=1162')">1162年4月</a>　以右史午对。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1162&endYear=1162')">1162年4月22日</a>　洪迈等辞行，国书用敌国礼。知閤门事张抡为副使，弟景孙辅行。周必大、范成大有诗送行。<br /></div><div class='label1' id='a997c8a168924f4bb69a4e69b2c2969c_label'><a
