ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1166&endYear=1168')">1166-1168年</a>，44-46岁</div><div id='a997c8a168924f4bb69a4e69b2c2969c' class='detail'><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1166&endYear=1166')">1166年</a>　入对。除起居舍人。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1166&endYear=1166')">1166年</a>　上《国史院进三朝正史帝纪表》。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1166&endYear=1166')">1166年10月9日</a>　乞蠲减鄱阳岁贡诞节金。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1166&endYear=1166')">1166年10月</a>　兼权直学士院，作《辞免直学士院状》。<div id='poem_1256703' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1256703' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1256703?labeling=true' target='_blank'>辞免直学士院状</a><span class='authorDate'>（1166年10月）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 南宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(28601, "南宋", "洪迈", "poem_title_1256703")'>洪迈</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1256703_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1256703'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1256703'>宠数荐降，兼官愈优，受恩已多，拊己难称。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1256703_comment'></div>窃以代言之任，最切于翰林；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1256703_comment'></div>直院之名，实邻于学士。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1256703_comment'></div>臣之孤陋，众所鄙夷。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1256703_comment'></div>未至预荣，方幸摄官而承乏；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1256703_comment'></div>序升过分，未能满岁以为真。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1256703_comment'></div>曾是叨尘，若何启处！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1256703_comment'></div>愿寝已行之命，少须试可之长。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1256703_comment'></div>庶使微踪，获安旧署。</div><div id='poem_sentence_8_1256703_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1166&endYear=1166')">1166年11月13日</a>　洪迈奏请谨录圣语为《祥曦殿记注》，诏从之。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1166&endYear=1166')">1166年11月</a>　薛季益使金，迈等共饯之于吏部尚书厅。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1166&endYear=1166')">1166年12月9日</a>　叶颙自资政殿学士除枢密院事，迈作《赐叶资政辞召命诏》。<div id='poem_1256644' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1256644' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1256644?labeling=true' target='_blank'>赐叶资政辞召命诏</a><span class='authorDate'>（1166年12月9日）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 南宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(28601, "南宋", "洪迈", "poem_title_1256644")'>洪迈</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1256644_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1256644'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1256644'>见晛曰消，顾何伤于日月；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1256644_comment'></div>得时则驾，宜亟会于风云。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1256644_comment'></div></div><div id='poem_sentence_2_1256644_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1166&endYear=1166')">1166年</a><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1166&endYear=1166')">1166年12月14日</a>　洪迈等言《钦宗日历》可发付国史院，依例修纂《实录》，并申请修史条例。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1166&endYear=1166')">1166年12月15日</a>　叶颙、魏杞拜左、右相，迈草制。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1166&endYear=1166')">1166年12月18日</a>　《夷坚乙志》成。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1166&endYear=1166')">1166年12月28日</a>　请诏枢密院，凡已被旨文书，门下依三省画黄书读。诏从之。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1166&endYear=1166')">1166年12月</a>　兼同修国史。有《辞免同修国史奏状》。<div id='poem_1256702' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1256702' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1256702?labeling=true' target='_blank'>辞免同修国史奏状</a><span class='authorDate'>（1166年12月）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 南宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(28601, "南宋", "洪迈", "poem_title_1256702")'>洪迈</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1256702_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1256702'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1256702'>拜命稠沓，拊心震兢。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1256702_comment'></div>窃以史职至清，儒流所重。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1256702_comment'></div>祖功宗德，方资润色于无穷；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1256702_comment'></div>人祸天刑，实惧照临之在上。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1256702_comment'></div>顾以四朝之大典，萃于一介之鲰生，方辞撰述之除，更冒删修之任。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1256702_comment'></div>矧二名之宠，非侍从而不居；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1256702_comment'></div>乃两日之间，荷光灵之曲被。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1256702_comment'></div>倘稽牍免，立见器盈。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1256702_comment'></div>伏望皇帝陛下特寝新恩，俾仍旧贯，博选立言之士，来充抽室之官，庶使孱庸，获逃旷败。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1256702_comment'></div>所有恩命，臣未敢祗受。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1256702_comment'></div>伏候敕旨。</div><div id='poem_sentence_10_1256702_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1166&endYear=1166')">1166年</a>　是年冬，《圣政》书成，作《修圣政转官词》及《赐宰臣辞免提举圣政书成转官诏》。<div id='poem_1256651' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1256651' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1256651?labeling=true' target='_blank'>修圣政转官制</a><span class='authorDate'>（1166年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 南宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(28601, "南宋", "洪迈", "poem_title_1256651")'>洪迈</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1256651_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1256651'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1256651'>念五马浮江之后，光启中兴；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1256651_comment'></div>述六龙御天以来，式时猷训。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1256651_comment'></div></div><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_1256651'>荐于天而天是受，永言覆焘之恩；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1256651_comment'></div>问诸朝而朝不知，讵测形容之妙。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1256651_comment'></div></div><div id='poem_sentence_4_1256651_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1166&endYear=1166')">1166年</a><div id='poem_1256646' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1256646' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1256646?labeling=true' target='_blank'>赐宰臣辞免提举圣政书成转官诏</a><span class='authorDate'>（1166年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 南宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(28601, "南宋", "洪迈", "poem_title_1256646")'>洪迈</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1256646_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1256646'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1256646'>为天子父尊之至，永惟传序之恩；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1256646_comment'></div>问圣人德何以加，莫越重华之孝。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1256646_comment'></div></div><div id='poem_sentence_2_1256646_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1166&endYear=1166')">1166年</a>　是年，有《生查子》、《浣溪纱》词，赵磻老有和韵。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1167&endYear=1167')">1167年1月27日</a>　召对选德殿。高宗极论古今治乱事及祖宗法度，令迈作《选德殿记》。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1167&endYear=1167')">1167年2月13日</a>　洪迈奏两省毎日行遣录黄文书，不足以烦朝廷专出命者。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1167&endYear=1167')">1167年2月25日</a>　记中书门下省官壁题名。作品：中书门下省官壁记。<div id='poem_1256809' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1256809' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1256809?labeling=true' target='_blank'>中书门下省官壁记</a><span class='authorDate'>（乾道三年二月）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 南宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(28601, "南宋", "洪迈", "poem_title_1256809")'>洪迈</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1256809_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1256809'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1256809'>两省之官十有二，唐制也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1256809_comment'></div>今散骑常侍缺，繇谏大夫而下别为谏院，同门而异户。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1256809_comment'></div>唯给事中、中书舍人、左右起居实同省，其员亦十有二。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1256809_comment'></div>渡江以来，盖损三之一，然亦未尝备也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1256809_comment'></div>给、舍以法从为职，凡紫微、黄门之政，无论小大，实书之，实行之，其未韪者得以告而还之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1256809_comment'></div>两起居日侍殿上，备顾问，皆名一时清切要官。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1256809_comment'></div>然去来姓名不谨于掌故，四十年间，已泮散不可考。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1256809_comment'></div>迈兄弟前后四入省，举致意焉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1256809_comment'></div>迈去右史五年而复至，乃竟成之，独建炎年时为不整，叙或失其所来及所去官。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1256809_comment'></div>姑存之，合为百七十有五人，其重至三至者二十有五人。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1256809_comment'></div>今廊庙五公，皆从吾省干青云而直上，异时莫盛焉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1256809_comment'></div>权官不书，独记南阳公，所以尊宰相，重吾省也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1256809_comment'></div>题名成，又请浙东相公大隶表其上。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1256809_comment'></div>乾道三年二月二十五日记。</div><div id='poem_sentence_13_1256809_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1167&endYear=1167')">1167年3月7日</a>　宣召入殿侍讲。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1167&endYear=1167')">1167年3月25日</a>　与给事中王曮等上《同符贞观录》。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1167&endYear=1167')">1167年3月28日</a>　洪迈等奏修《哲宗宝训》成书。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1167&endYear=1167')">1167年5月1日</a>　主持编修《哲宗宝训》书成进上。并作《批执政辞经修哲宗宝训转官》。<div id='poem_1256645' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1256645' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1256645?labeling=true' target='_blank'>执政辞经修哲宗宝训转官批答</a><span class='authorDate'>（1167年5月1日）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 南宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(28601, "南宋", "洪迈", "poem_title_1256645")'>洪迈</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1256645_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1256645'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1256645'>念叠矩重规，当<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_0_1256645", 1256645, "Clauses/1/Comments/0")'>贤圣</span>之君七作；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1256645_comment'></div>而立经陈纪，在谟训之文百篇。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1256645_comment'></div></div><div id='poem_sentence_2_1256645_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1167&endYear=1167')">1167年5月11日</a>　迈奏请令靖康名臣孙觌撰述《钦宗实录》诸臣列传及一朝议论。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1167&endYear=1167')">1167年5月</a>　除起居郎。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1167&endYear=1167')">1167年6月11日</a>　乞禁戢巡尉迎送。作品：乞禁戢巡尉迎送劄子。<div id='poem_1256737' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1256737' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1256737?labeling=true' target='_blank'>乞禁戢巡尉迎送劄子</a><span class='authorDate'>（1167年6月11日）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 南宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(28601, "南宋", "洪迈", "poem_title_1256737")'>洪迈</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1256737_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1256737'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1256737'>臣窃惟巡尉之官，专以捕盗贼、督奸猾为职，未尝责其将迎上官，巡视传舍也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1256737_comment'></div>而间者以来，惟事趋走，漫不复以职事为意。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1256737_comment'></div>而最甚者，如都巡检使所部或连三州，或跨两路，凡监司守贰之去来，必候之于境上。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1256737_comment'></div>所带兵卒数十辈，无俸可借，则敛之众军以给。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1256737_comment'></div>所历道路数百里，无赀可赡，则取之村民以济。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1256737_comment'></div>若所除监司又或改命，往往空行空反，动涉一两月。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1256737_comment'></div>设部内不虞而有鼠窃狗偷之盗，当以何人捕之？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1256737_comment'></div>夫居此官者亦岂乐为奔走之役哉？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1256737_comment'></div>一或不至，则上官以为失礼，因缘捃摭，使不安位。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1256737_comment'></div>故相承为例，欲罢不能，非有以惩革之，实为未便。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1256737_comment'></div>臣愚欲望圣慈，行下诸路提刑司，约束所部巡尉，今后遇监司、知、通初到，许量带兵级出一程防护。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1256737_comment'></div>若只值出巡经历而在监司五十里内者，许其送迎。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1256737_comment'></div>过此以外，皆不得出。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1256737_comment'></div>如尚敢循习远去者，乞并受接之官差治其罪。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1256737_comment'></div>庶使各安职业，精意徼巡，不至虚费军力，且为民害。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1256737_comment'></div>如蒙俞允，乞敕下施行。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1256737_comment'></div>取进止。</div><div id='poem_sentence_16_1256737_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1167&endYear=1167')">1167年6月</a>　以权中书舍人兼实录院修撰。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1167&endYear=1167')">1167年7月6日</a>　除中书舍人兼侍读兼权直学士院。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1167&endYear=1167')">1167年7月22日</a>　落“权”字。有《谢除中书舍人表》。<div id='poem_1256686' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1256686' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1256686?labeling=true' target='_blank'>谢除中书舍人表</a><span class='authorDate'>（1167年7月22日）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 南宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(28601, "南宋", "洪迈", "poem_title_1256686")'>洪迈</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1256686_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1256686'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1256686'>记言左史，甫沐于序迁；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1256686_comment'></div>掌制中书，遽叨于真拜。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1256686_comment'></div>荷光灵之曲被，循涯涘以难胜<span class='inlineComment2'>（中谢。）</span>。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1256686_comment'></div>伏念臣行能亡以瘉人，愚憧而不逮事。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1256686_comment'></div>少年驰骛，妄有意于功名；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1256686_comment'></div>壮岁崎嵚，私自怜于力命。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1256686_comment'></div>未分山林之独往，甘从州郡之徒劳。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1256686_comment'></div>正违鸣玉之趋，忽点赐环之召。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1256686_comment'></div>径归故步，亟侍清光。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1256686_comment'></div>官资兼五职之华，翰墨极一时之选。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1256686_comment'></div>顾生成之特异，觉报称以至难。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1256686_comment'></div>可以言而言，造膝必期于展尽；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1256686_comment'></div>非所据而据，谋身敢择于便安！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1256686_comment'></div>深虞羁迹之疾颠，乃辱脩门之孟进。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1256686_comment'></div>矧是词臣之贵，实为世掌之荣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1256686_comment'></div>父子相承，四上鸾坡之直；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1256686_comment'></div>弟兄在望，三陪凤阁之游。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1256686_comment'></div>共夸遭遇之殊，窃有满盈之惧。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1256686_comment'></div>兹盖伏遇皇帝陛下重华协帝，下武继文。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1256686_comment'></div>笃实辉光而日新，躬行仁义；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_19_1256686_comment'></div>溥博渊泉而时出，独化陶钧。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_20_1256686_comment'></div>当循名责实之辰，欲砥节奉公之士。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_21_1256686_comment'></div>察其孤立，或效一长，使居侍从之班，仍在丝纶之地。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_22_1256686_comment'></div>臣敢不敬共官次，感诵天恩？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_23_1256686_comment'></div>巍巍其有成功，方际有为之会；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_24_1256686_comment'></div>断断而无他技，誓殚无隐之忠。</div><div id='poem_sentence_25_1256686_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1167&endYear=1167')">1167年闰7月</a>　刘共甫自潭帅除翰林学士，迈作答诏。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1167&endYear=1167')">1167年8月</a>　召对便殿。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1167&endYear=1167')">1167年10月</a>　占城入贡，答敕，引故事，乞用金花白藤纸写诏，与李焘有争执。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1167&endYear=1167')">1167年11月</a>　奏请修《钦宗实录》。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1167&endYear=1167')">1167年11月2日</a>　南郊礼成，迈当制撰赦文。作品：南郊赦文。<div id='poem_1256637' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1256637' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1256637?labeling=true' target='_blank'>南郊赦文</a><span class='authorDate'>（1167年11月2日）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 南宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(28601, "南宋", "洪迈", "poem_title_1256637")'>洪迈</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1256637_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1256637'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1256637'>皇天后土，监于成命之诗；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1256637_comment'></div>艺祖太宗，昭我思文之配。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1256637_comment'></div></div><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_1256637'>天地设位而圣人成能，既扑缊纷之况；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1256637_comment'></div>雷雨作解而君子赦过，式流汪濊之恩。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1256637_comment'></div></div><div id='poem_sentence_4_1256637_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1167&endYear=1167')">1167年11月9日</a>　叶颙以郊祀雷罢相，迈草制。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1167&endYear=1167')">1167年11月13日</a>　以雷发非时，诏台谏、侍从、两省官指陈阙失。陈俊卿劾奏洪迈“奸险谗佞，不宜在左右”。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1167&endYear=1167')">1167年12月3日</a>　诏令直前奏事。此后修注官遇常朝日有奏禀职事，依此。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1167&endYear=1167')">1167年12月11日</a>　请修《钦宗实录》展限一年。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1167&endYear=1167')">1167年12月18日</a>　序洪适《隶续》。作品：隶续序。<div id='poem_1256769' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1256769' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1256769?labeling=true' target='_blank'>隶续序</a><span class='authorDate'>（乾道三年十二月）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 南宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(28601, "南宋", "洪迈", "poem_title_1256769")'>洪迈</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1256769_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1256769'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1256769'>吾兄丞相番阳公安抚浙江东道，部郡七，治所临会稽，部县八，西接行在所，东际海，南拊百越之区，地大物众，槃槃一都会也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1256769_comment'></div>处之踰年，兵民两安，山颠水厓，如立庭户。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1256769_comment'></div>不能称过使客饰厨传，又不能蒙子公力作长安书，独于隶古之习根著胶固，手追心摹，今三十馀年。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1256769_comment'></div>得黄金百，如视涕唾，即获一汉刻，津津然盱衡击节，辍食罢寝，摩挲而谨读之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1256769_comment'></div>意世间所谓乐事，直无以右此者。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1256769_comment'></div>喟然叹曰：「天下奇宝也，吾颛乡而独美之为不仁」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1256769_comment'></div>空箧中，得所藏碑百八十有九，译其文，又述其所以然，为二十七卷，曰《隶释》。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1256769_comment'></div>书法不必同，人视之无如也，则皆毛举十数字刊诸石，曰《隶缵》。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1256769_comment'></div>其字同，其体异，参差不可齐，则倚声而汇之，曰《隶韵》。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1256769_comment'></div>龙龟爵麟，九尾之狐，琮璜璋圭，名物怪奇，凡见于扁颜者，各肖其象，曰《隶图》。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1256769_comment'></div>亦既释之而又得之，则列于廿七卷以往，曰《隶续》。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1256769_comment'></div>大氐皆祖东汉时，其高出西京，<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_11_1256769", 1256769, "Clauses/56/Comments/0")'>浸淫</span>以及魏晋者，率不能什一。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1256769_comment'></div>搜罗梱粹，盖不遗馀力矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1256769_comment'></div>自篆捷于汉而为隶，变于魏八分。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1256769_comment'></div>于晋、宋、隋、唐之间，以分视隶，由康瓠之与周鼎也，而唐人笃好之，汉法益亡。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1256769_comment'></div>杜子美之诗云：「仓颉鸟迹既茫昧，字体变化如浮云。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1256769_comment'></div>陈仓石鼓又已讹，大小二篆生八分」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1256769_comment'></div>又曰：「中郎石经后，八分盖蕉萃」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1256769_comment'></div>则泾渭杂揉，以分为隶，虽杜子美有所不能知。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1256769_comment'></div>吾兄一旦发千古之秘藏，悉主张是。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_19_1256769_comment'></div>使蔡中郎复生，见此数者，当复有得异书之叹。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_20_1256769_comment'></div>兄尝三上奏天子，乞身归，辄奉诏不许。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_21_1256769_comment'></div>傥留不已，惧其汗南山之竹云。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_22_1256769_comment'></div>乾道三年十二月十八日，弟左中奉大夫、守中书舍人、兼直学士院、兼同修国史、兼实录院修撰、兼侍讲迈书。</div><div id='poem_sentence_23_1256769_comment'></div></div><div class='poemNote' id='poem_note_1256769'><span class='label'>按：</span>《隶续》卷首，中华书局一九八三年影印本。<br /></div><div id='poem_note_1256769_comment'></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1167&endYear=1167')">1167年</a>　赵彦端自右司赴江东漕，迈送行，有《临江仙》词。作品：临江仙。<span class='inlineComment2'>（《嗣濮王加恩制》、《士衎加恩制》、《吴璘奖谕诏》、《吴挺兴州制》、《吴挺起复金州制》、《奖谕吴挺诏》、《岳阳军节度使韩公裔碑》等作，大约在是年前后所作。）</span><div id='poem_179705' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_179705' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/179705?labeling=true' target='_blank'>临江仙</a><span class='authorDate'>（1145年3月15日）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 南宋 · </span><a class='poemContent' id='poem_content_179705'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_179705'>绮席流欢欢正洽，高楼佳气重重。<div id='poem_sentence_0_179705_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_179705_comment'></div></div><br /><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_3_179705'>桂月十分春正半，广寒宫殿葱葱。<div id='poem_sentence_3_179705_comment'></div></div><div ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1185&endYear=1185')">1185年</a>　除提举佑神观，兼侍讲。有辞状及谢表。作品：辞免兼侍讲状。<div id='poem_1256698' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1256698' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1256698?labeling=true' target='_blank'>辞免兼侍讲状</a><span class='authorDate'>（1185年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 南宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(28601, "南宋", "洪迈", "poem_title_1256698")'>洪迈</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1256698_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1256698'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1256698'>臣闻命震悚，不知所云。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1256698_comment'></div>伏念臣一介书生，见识污下，仅能骈四俪六，缀缉华藻，以事区区应用之词章。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1256698_comment'></div>至于潜心圣经，窥发关键，如以蠡测海，莫知津涯。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1256698_comment'></div>而使之参劝讲之联，侍迩英之席，非所据焉，实为甚惧。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1256698_comment'></div>又况圣学渊妙，今古洞然，如日当天，幽隐毕照，虽使大雅宏达之士殚效尺寸，日陈乎前，犹增高泰山，何足云补？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1256698_comment'></div>顾臣等辈决非所堪。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1256698_comment'></div>伏望圣慈，曲垂英监，别择经谊高明可备顾问者，使充此选。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1256698_comment'></div>臣无任祈天恳激之至。</div><div id='poem_sentence_7_1256698_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1185&endYear=1185')">1185年</a><div id='poem_1256685' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1256685' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1256685?labeling=true' target='_blank'>谢兼侍讲表</a><span class='authorDate'>（1185年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 南宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(28601, "南宋", "洪迈", "poem_title_1256685")'>洪迈</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1256685_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1256685'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1256685'>经帷初启，宜延茂异之儒；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1256685_comment'></div>讲缀正清，乃及蔽蒙之士。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1256685_comment'></div>据非所称，荣不胜恩<span class='inlineComment2'>（中谢。）</span>。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1256685_comment'></div>切以王求多闻，虽资启沃朝夕之助；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1256685_comment'></div>天纵将圣，自有缉熙光明之功。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1256685_comment'></div>揆臣之愚，何若而可？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1256685_comment'></div>猥以传家之末技，尝有意于遗经。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1256685_comment'></div>措游、夏之一辞，岂知笔削？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1256685_comment'></div>束《春秋》之五传，空极钻研。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1256685_comment'></div>使居诵说之联，入奉清閒之燕。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1256685_comment'></div>内而省己，恧有腼颜。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1256685_comment'></div>兹盖伏遇皇帝陛下聪明宪天，浚哲稽古。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1256685_comment'></div>拨乱世而反诸正，既统一于圣真；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1256685_comment'></div>守经事而知其宜，欲汎观于物应。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1256685_comment'></div>故如臣等，亦寘选中。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1256685_comment'></div>臣敢不别嫌明微，章善瘅恶？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1256685_comment'></div>灿然兴文武之业，方观一统之成；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1256685_comment'></div>学者以帝王为师，式几千龄之遇。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1256685_comment'></div></div><div id='poem_sentence_18_1256685_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1185&endYear=1185')">1185年</a>　太府少卿张抑字子仪，以启贺迈，云：“珍台闲馆，冠皋伊之伦魁；广厦细旃，论唐虞之圣道。”<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1185&endYear=1185')">1185年3月26日</a>　车驾宿戒幸玉津园，迈进诗歌咏。作品：玉津喜晴诗。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1185&endYear=1185')">1185年4月4日</a>　迈扈从景灵宫，孝宗和《玉津喜晴诗》。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1185&endYear=1185')">1185年6月</a>　以敷文阁待制提举佑神观兼同修国史，有谢表及辞状。作品：谢侍讲兼修国史表。<div id='poem_1256689' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1256689' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1256689?labeling=true' target='_blank'>谢侍讲兼修国史表</a><span class='authorDate'>（1185年6月）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 南宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(28601, "南宋", "洪迈", "poem_title_1256689")'>洪迈</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1256689_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1256689'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1256689'>七闰去朝，久隔钧天之梦；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1256689_comment'></div>一朝得觐，重趋丹地之班。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1256689_comment'></div>仰戴鸿私，俯惭驽钝<span class='inlineComment2'>（中谢。）</span>。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1256689_comment'></div>伏念臣本无学，鲜克有功。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1256689_comment'></div>禁路持荷，蚤占荣于清贯；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1256689_comment'></div>大州剖竹，旋待罪于辅藩。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1256689_comment'></div>蔑报毫分，怅违颜咫。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1256689_comment'></div>敢谓玺封之收召，趣前宣席之对扬，禄以真祠，还其故步。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1256689_comment'></div>劝汉殿光禄之讲，安用腐儒？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1256689_comment'></div>纂周官石室之文，复为太史。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1256689_comment'></div>拜训辞之甚厚，知符任之益专。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1256689_comment'></div>自顾惷愚，将何答塞！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1256689_comment'></div>兹盖伏遇皇帝陛下道齐尧舜，仁奉祖宗。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1256689_comment'></div>下建武之诏书，正尔恢张于治具；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1256689_comment'></div>数正元之朝士，独怜流落之孤踪。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1256689_comment'></div>肆垂齿录之恩，俾卒汗青之业。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1256689_comment'></div>臣敢不旁搜远绍，广记备言？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1256689_comment'></div>窃窥圣学之光明，谨次旧闻之放失。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1256689_comment'></div>抱遗经而究终始，讵殚佔毕之勤？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1256689_comment'></div>藏名山而副京师，实有遭逢之幸。</div><div id='poem_sentence_19_1256689_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1185&endYear=1185')">1185年</a><div id='poem_1256700' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1256700' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1256700?labeling=true' target='_blank'>辞免兼修国史奏状</a><span class='authorDate'>（1185年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 南宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(28601, "南宋", "洪迈", "poem_title_1256700")'>洪迈</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1256700_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1256700'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1256700'>恩辉狎至，荣惧交中。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1256700_comment'></div>窃以史官之权，从昔所重。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1256700_comment'></div>自四朝大典开院以来几三十年，臣三预编摩，两叨修纂，初无才学识之三长，以裨笔削。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1256700_comment'></div>爰自去岁，蒙恩纪录，召从外郡，俾续抽金匮石室之书。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1256700_comment'></div>赖圣学发挥，窃窥至赜，期年于兹，行有汗青之望，庶得少逃罪悔，上答恩知。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1256700_comment'></div>今乃猥缘晋除，就升厥次，颛此重任，顾何以堪？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1256700_comment'></div>伏望圣慈矜存，姑令仍旧。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1256700_comment'></div>其兼侍讲一节，更不敢辄辞，所有兼修国史恩命，臣未敢祗受。</div><div id='poem_sentence_7_1256700_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1185&endYear=1185')">1185年7月9日</a>　奏《四朝正史》列传宜分类载述。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1185&endYear=1185')">1185年</a>　有劄子，以盗贼为虑。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1185&endYear=1185')">1185年9月10日</a>　中书舍人王信使金，迈有送诗。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1185&endYear=1185')">1185年</a>　王信将命出使，三馆之士饯于史退傅北园，沈虞卿出《兰亭序》示坐客，同观者凡十四人。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1185&endYear=1185')">1185年9月13日</a>　孝宗赐御书唐白居易诗二首。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1185&endYear=1185')">1185年10月8日</a>　请行课绩之法。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1185&endYear=1185')">1185年</a>　友人沈虞卿遣相士苏生来，王敬甫亦来。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1186&endYear=1186')">1186年1月5日</a>　以光尧太上庆寿，肆赦恩转一官，授通奉大夫。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1186&endYear=1186')">1186年</a>　光尧庆寿，覃恩免解，宗子在学者不预，迈遍谒侍从、台谏，各纳一劄子。迈以待制侍讲内宿，适蒙宣引，因出其纸以奏。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1186&endYear=1186')">1186年3月17日</a>　召对，孝宗恩宠有加。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1186&endYear=1186')">1186年3月26日</a>　进诗。<br /><a ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1186&endYear=1186')">1186年4月</a>　跋《范文正与尹师鲁二帖》。<div id='poem_1256794' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1256794' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1256794?labeling=true' target='_blank'>题范文正公与尹师鲁手启墨迹</a><span class='authorDate'>（淳熙十三年四月）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 南宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(28601, "南宋", "洪迈", "poem_title_1256794")'>洪迈</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1256794_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1256794'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1256794'>范公二帖，皆是师鲁谪汉东时书。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1256794_comment'></div>后一帖却当在前，或是自均过邓，托范公以死时问讯之书，与众云云之戒可见也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1256794_comment'></div>贤者困厄至此，人到于今伤之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1256794_comment'></div>藏之深，固之密，石可朽，名不灭，欧公铭文尽之矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1256794_comment'></div>淳熙丙午四月，洪迈书。</div><div id='poem_sentence_4_1256794_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1186&endYear=1186')">1186年4月</a>　除敷文阁直学士兼直学士院。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1186&endYear=1186')">1186年5月1日</a>　与同僚进读陆贽奏议终篇。乞宣付史馆，以彰不矜不伐执古御今之意。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1186&endYear=1186')">1186年5月6日</a>　诏转一官酬劳。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1186&endYear=1186')">1186年5月13日</a>　撰谢恩诗进上，诏宣付史馆。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1186&endYear=1186')">1186年8月26日</a>　知龙州王偁上《东都事略》百十三卷，洪迈时领修《四朝国史》，颇取资焉。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1186&endYear=1186')">1186年9月</a>　除翰林学士知制诰，兼修国史，依前正奉大夫。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1186&endYear=1186')">1186年9月29日</a>　迈奏乞取钦宗遗翰布之史馆。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1186&endYear=1186')">1186年9月</a>　周必大求祠，迈作二《不允诏》。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1186&endYear=1186')">1186年10月2日</a>　进钦宗宸翰石刻，付史馆。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1186&endYear=1186')">1186年10月9日</a>　奏《四朝史传》成书。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1186&endYear=1186')">1186年11月</a>　国史院上迈所主持编修《四朝国史·列传》一百三十五卷。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1186&endYear=1186')">1186年11月</a>　丞相王淮、梁克家进《玉牒》、《四朝史传》等书加恩，迈草制。作品：王丞相进玉牒加恩制。<div id='poem_1256648' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1256648' class='poemTitle ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1186&endYear=1186')">1186年</a>　张镃即席又有[谒金门]赏梅词，和迈韵。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1186&endYear=1186')">1186年</a>　有《赐安南国历日诏》。<br ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1187&endYear=1187')">1187年3月18日</a>　奏荐承议郎知龙州王偁、登仕郎龚敦颐，乞赐甄录。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1187&endYear=1187')">1187年3月22日</a>　驾幸玉津园，洪迈等群臣扈从，有摩崖题名。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1187&endYear=1187')">1187年4月4日</a>　召对清华殿，孝宗取宸翰一轴赐迈。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1187&endYear=1187')">1187年4月</a>　又晚对，孝宗谕以止痰法。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1187&endYear=1187')">1187年4月6日</a>　与尤袤等九人于群玉亭观《兰亭序》。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1187&endYear=1187')">1187年8月3日</a>　诏祭告得雨，迈草《批以旱得雨请御殿》。<div id='poem_1256647' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1256647' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1256647?labeling=true' target='_blank'>以旱得雨请御殿批答</a><span class='authorDate'>（1187年8月3日）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 南宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(28601, "南宋", "洪迈", "poem_title_1256647")'>洪迈</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1256647_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1256647'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1256647'>念七月之间则旱，咎徵已深；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1256647_comment'></div>虽三日已往为霖，忧端未贳。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1256647_comment'></div></div><div id='poem_sentence_2_1256647_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1187&endYear=1187')">1187年8月8日</a>　周必大过史院，迈出示所藏王摩诘山水。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1187&endYear=1187')">1187年8月24日</a>　作《重建金山佛殿记》。<div id='poem_1256815' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1256815' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1256815?labeling=true' target='_blank'>重建佛殿记</a><span class='authorDate'>（淳熙十四年八月）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 南宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(28601, "南宋", "洪迈", "poem_title_1256815")'>洪迈</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1256815_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1256815'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1256815'>江自岷山而下，历巴夔湘楚，包吞前沫，横漾浯流，沱潜澧沔眄金，巨川数千百，演迤横放，薄于朱方，极沛以大，然后东入于海，举天下之水莫盛此焉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1256815_comment'></div>金、焦两山，崒然天立，镇乎中流，皆有大兰若岧峣其上，古记谓紫金、浮玉者是矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1256815_comment'></div>浮玉处其左，如幽人逸士，岩栖谷隐，恐入林之不密，故航苇罕至，而僧居触事，随亦泯歇。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1256815_comment'></div>惟紫金超遥擅胜，不复与同，荡然开辟，八面应敌。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1256815_comment'></div>所谓江心一峰，水面千里，潭月双映，云天四垂，真能雄跨东南二百州，如宸章所表揭者。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1256815_comment'></div>千帆下来，万客鳞萃，鱼龙之所凭怙，人天之所宾悒，古今推胜，无得拟议。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1256815_comment'></div>寺旧名泽心，天禧中真宗皇帝感宵梦所抵，更为龙游，飞帛扁额，以贲方来，室庐峥嵘，概与境称。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1256815_comment'></div>遭罹魔劫，鞠为烬墟。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1256815_comment'></div>中兴以还，视力开葺。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1256815_comment'></div>军师刘宝奋营大殿，几成而厄于火。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1256815_comment'></div>明年，郡守韩及祖又嗣为之，筑于道谋，旋即蠹败。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1256815_comment'></div>淳熙四年，枢密沈公复出治，慨然叹曰：「吾行四方多矣，未有如此刹者，住山非本色人其可哉」！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1256815_comment'></div>乃卑礼厚帛，延金华蕴衷师于集山，俾主张是。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1256815_comment'></div>舍寂而居嚣，去安而即烦，人以为介介，师不屑也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1256815_comment'></div>遍行其疆，悲智歘起，自念己身逢此坏相，亟倒空钵囊，先众募舍。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1256815_comment'></div>前所未及，一切趋新。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1256815_comment'></div>展前资以安耆旧，抗塔院以壮瞻睹。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1256815_comment'></div>寿坊、经室、庖浴、厢萦，易翳为明，宽洁敞靓。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1256815_comment'></div>江滨故址隘而不舒，累石拓基，堤护榆杨，作屋二十四楹。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1256815_comment'></div>中建亭，命曰「烟雨奇观」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_19_1256815_comment'></div>游士戾止，洗心储清。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_20_1256815_comment'></div>又舍法施，为后人买田六十顷。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_21_1256815_comment'></div>唯雄殿尊居，役钜费侈，居之六年而后敢议。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_22_1256815_comment'></div>择廉谨僧入闽，即山伐木，如约浮海，归命鼋鼍而协谟，节定星而揆日，道充于内而迹彰于外，其声远扬，如谷应响。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_23_1256815_comment'></div>施者惟恐不克丰其献，匠者惟恐不克既其巧。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_24_1256815_comment'></div>度为崇五十有五尺，为广七十有四尺，糜钱六十万，阅四寒暑而成。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_25_1256815_comment'></div>廓如穹如，轮奂华奕。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_26_1256815_comment'></div>却顾城阙，根尘聿清，前瞻海潮，法音如在，吴头楚尾，莫之与京。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_27_1256815_comment'></div>功甫讫，师移锡钱塘灵隐，邦人愿有记，使来谒。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_28_1256815_comment'></div>当绍兴之季，戎马饮江，暴骨堆莽。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_29_1256815_comment'></div>是时长老净信，诱化童隶，收拾瘗藏。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_30_1256815_comment'></div>予再奉使，往来亲见，为之启于太上，被褒宠计僧徒二十人，则予于兹山疑若有宿因，故书而不辞。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_31_1256815_comment'></div>殿经始于癸卯之孟夏，成于乙巳之仲春，而记于丁未之秋八月实有二十四日癸巳云。</div><div id='poem_sentence_32_1256815_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1187&endYear=1187')">1187年8月</a>　尝入侍，孝宗称赞《容斋随笔》。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1187&endYear=1187')">1187年9月13日</a>　为陈铸作《城南堂记》。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1187&endYear=1187')">1187年10月8日</a>　草《太上遗诏》。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1187&endYear=1187')">1187年10月8日</a>　太上皇高宗赵构卒于德寿殿。孝宗未见群臣，首引翰林学士洪迈及萧燧。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1187&endYear=1187')">1187年10月11日</a>　言大行皇帝庙号当称“祖”，诏有司集议以闻。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1187&endYear=1187')">1187年10月</a>　光尧上宾，迈以学士充桥道顿递使。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1187&endYear=1187')">1187年10月12日</a>　表请孝宗还宫听政。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1187&endYear=1187')">1187年10月</a>　有《贺皇帝御殿表》。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1187&endYear=1187')">1187年10月14日</a>　请太上庙号“世祖”。诏有司讨论庙号仪制以闻。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1187&endYear=1187')">1187年10月22日</a>　尝入奏。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1187&endYear=1187')">1187年10月25日</a>　内引洪迈，奏事。留身预太子听政事。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1187&endYear=1187')">1187年10月25日</a>　召对，谕迈欲以皇太子参决，使条具合行事宜以进。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1187&endYear=1187')">1187年10月28日</a>　迈撰《告哀使国书》。孝宗复召迈议事。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1187&endYear=1187')">1187年11月1日</a>　内引洪迈，拟皇太子参决诏。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1187&endYear=1187')">1187年11月2日</a>　诏皇太子参决庶务。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1187&endYear=1187')">1187年11月11日</a>　集议太上谥号，用礼官所拟“高宗”，不用迈所请“世祖”。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1187&endYear=1187')">1187年11月24日</a>　洪迈入局，乞省罢排顿官十二员，只付见任官，仍不推赏。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1187&endYear=1187')">1187年11月28日</a>　迈奏或指不合首议称祖，乞居家待罪。批云：“议礼何嫌异同，可日下供职”。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1187&endYear=1187')">1187年11月29日</a>　内引宿直官洪迈谢称“祖”待罪事。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1187&endYear=1187')">1187年</a>　冬，孝宗召迈，与语用宦者甘升事。欲迈向王信转达旨意。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1187&endYear=1187')">1187年</a>　有《乞审察将副劄子》、《谢书御书孟子表》、《谢冬衣表》、《贺祠高禖表》、《戒谕中外百僚诏》。<div id='poem_1256738' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1256738' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1256738?labeling=true' target='_blank'>乞审察将副劄子</a><span class='authorDate'>（1187年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 南宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(28601, "南宋", "洪迈", "poem_title_1256738")'>洪迈</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1256738_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1256738'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1256738'>臣仰惟陛下天纵神武，励精政事，当国家閒暇之时，所以为久远之计者，未尝一日而辍。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1256738_comment'></div>故整军经武之备，尤切于圣心。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1256738_comment'></div>至于激励将士，则自用兵以来所未之有。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1256738_comment'></div>窃见比者以禁军疑射铁帘，收纵甚敏，旌殿步帅之能训习，即迁其官。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1256738_comment'></div>以建康统制官刘忠、赵皋武艺精绝，既赏二人，又升其帅郭钧以遥郡，其不称者则寘之閒官。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1256738_comment'></div>赏信罚明，辕门竞劝，继自今必无复有妄补偏裨如向来之弊者。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1256738_comment'></div>然臣于此窃有献焉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1256738_comment'></div>臣谓大军列屯，既已闻风争夺，其州郡主兵者上则有总管，次则有钤辖，下则有都监，名为兵官，然麾下不过厮役之卒数十辈，虽有将略，亦无所施。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1256738_comment'></div>今东南将兵多者五千人，少者三二千人。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1256738_comment'></div>其任职者唯正副将，而资历颇卑，寻常除授之间，不暇精择，岂无不才者滥吹其间？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1256738_comment'></div>脱有差委，惧不胜任。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1256738_comment'></div>臣愚欲乞圣慈，特降睿旨，凡诸路将副阙到半年之前，略仿路钤以上谢辞之制，令赴枢密院审察。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1256738_comment'></div>其曾随军者仍试以技艺，较其能否，其不足统众者改授他职。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1256738_comment'></div>庶几兵将之间，无小无大，皆可以训圣天子阃外使令，诚非小补。</div><div id='poem_sentence_13_1256738_comment'></div></div></div><div id='poem_1256692' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1256692' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1256692?labeling=true' target='_blank'>福州谢历日表</a><span class='authorDate'>（1187年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 南宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(28601, "南宋", "洪迈", "poem_title_1256692")'>洪迈</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1256692_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1256692'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1256692'>课自清台，虽朝廷之故事；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1256692_comment'></div>命于方国，盖天子之至恩。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1256692_comment'></div>拜赐为荣，窥文何幸！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1256692_comment'></div>切以期三百六旬有六日，事盖备于唐尧；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1256692_comment'></div>律八十一寸则一分，法益严于汉武。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1256692_comment'></div>考辅相裁成之道，戒析因夷隩之宜，皆聚此书，以前民用。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1256692_comment'></div>恭惟皇帝陛下乾坤合德，历数在躬，卜年万寿以无疆，纪号一成而不变。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1256692_comment'></div>神祇祖考，既安乐于太平；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1256692_comment'></div>岁月日时，又明章于庶證。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1256692_comment'></div>礼勿忘于告朔，圣愈谨于占天。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1256692_comment'></div>肆令宣化以承流，咸识履端而举正。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1256692_comment'></div>璿玑不忒，玉烛自调。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1256692_comment'></div>臣敢不奉以周旋，审其作辍？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1256692_comment'></div>联珠合璧，曾何造化之能知；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1256692_comment'></div>流火授衣，尚见艰难之所致。</div><div id='poem_sentence_14_1256692_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1188&endYear=1188')">1188年1月2日</a>　皇太子初决庶务于议事堂。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1188&endYear=1188')">1188年1月7日</a>　内引贺金国生辰使副辞于清华閤，迈作国书。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1188&endYear=1188')">1188年1月19日</a>　内引洪迈，奏已过百日，宜服黪服。又具劄子奏饶州天申节进银之外贡金三百两，乞一例蠲免。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1188&endYear=1188')">1188年2月</a>　入直，上令中使持《御製太上挽诗》五首草示之，且谕今须有所改定。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1188&endYear=1188')">1188年3月11日</a>　内引洪迈，奏吕、赵、张、韩配享，乞令侍从议，并批依奏。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1188&endYear=1188')">1188年3月11日</a>　又进劄子，乞请开院修纂《高宗实录》。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1188&endYear=1188')">1188年3月15日</a>　高庙攒宫，迈拟《指挥》。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1188&endYear=1188')">1188年3月15日</a>　高宗梓宫发引，迈作《警场导引鼓吹词》及撰《挽诗》五章。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1188&endYear=1188')">1188年3月17日</a>　永思礼成，以吕颐浩、赵鼎、韩世忠、张俊配享。秘书省少监杨万里等乞用张浚，侍从集议，宜如明诏。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1188&endYear=1188')">1188年3月19日</a>　高宗梓宫过钱清江北闸，洪迈奏“恐内人等登车暴露，但当减节闲之舟上”。批依。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1188&endYear=1188')">1188年3月22日</a>　高宗梓宫安葬永思陵，迈与周必大等皆馆于泰宁寺。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1188&endYear=1188')">1188年3月22日</a>　孝宗言及张俊复辟之功及张浚两败事等。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1188&endYear=1188')">1188年3月25日</a>　右拾遗许及之密报洪迈，以台谏欲祔庙后论列配享，迈亟入奏，引杨万里之言乞去。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1188&endYear=1188')">1188年3月28日</a>　下《赐洪迈不允诏》。遗迈思堂春十尊。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1188&endYear=1188')">1188年3月30日</a>　高宗灵驾赴攒宫，与周必大、伯圭、萧燧、宇文价皆陪位。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1188&endYear=1188')">1188年4月8日</a>　孝宗谓杨万里争配享，言过而不公。决定杨、洪两人皆除职与郡。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1188&endYear=1188')">1188年4月9日</a>　诏洪迈、杨万里并予郡。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1188&endYear=1188')">1188年4月25日</a>　孝宗谕大臣曰：“吕颐浩等四人配享，正合公论，杨万里乃谓洪迈专私，迈虽是轻率，万里未免浮薄。”<br /></div>
-----end



-----title
英德
-----detail
<div class='label1' id='bb98d83686a84f5a806aad92c9be2c2c_label'><a href='javascript: DetailSwitch("bb98d83686a84f5a806aad92c9be2c2c");'><span id='bb98d83686a84f5a806aad92c9be2c2c_link' class='switch'>—</span></a><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1147&endYear=1147')">1147年</a>，25岁</div><div id='bb98d83686a84f5a806aad92c9be2c2c' class='detail'><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1147&endYear=1147')">1147年</a>　侍父居英。在英州置田百亩自给。与僧希赐游南山，读东坡《何公桥》诗石刻。<br /></div><div class='label1' id='2d587b74ed78444ba03383400a15d69e_label'><a href='javascript: DetailSwitch("2d587b74ed78444ba03383400a15d69e");'><span id='2d587b74ed78444ba03383400a15d69e_link' class='switch'>—</span></a><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1147&endYear=1147')">1147年</a>，25岁</div><div id='2d587b74ed78444ba03383400a15d69e' class='detail'><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1147&endYear=1147')">1147年</a>　闻英州二节妇事，为作传。作品：二节妇传。<div id='poem_1256848' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1256848' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1256848?labeling=true' target='_blank'>英州南雄二节妇传</a><span class='authorDate'>（1147年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 南宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(28601, "南宋", "洪迈", "poem_title_1256848")'>洪迈</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1256848_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1256848'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1256848'>绍兴五年，英州观音山盗起，摽掠所过，乡村空其人。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1256848_comment'></div>至曲江村，有书生吴琪者用窜免，其妻谭氏不能俱，与邻妇人数辈为贼得。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1256848_comment'></div>谭在众有姿色，群盗争主之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1256848_comment'></div>或临以刃，欲强辱之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1256848_comment'></div>谭怒骂曰：「若贼也，今所行甚獚无道，官军瞬息至，血肉喂狗猪矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1256848_comment'></div>我良家女，岂若偶」！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1256848_comment'></div>贼意自失，然甚爱，冀尚可回诱，鞘其刃，啖以隽语。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1256848_comment'></div>谭辄痛骂，奋袂狻其腕，贼袖殷焉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1256848_comment'></div>度无可奈何，杀之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1256848_comment'></div>后官兵至，盗所向槩执者皆得还，曰：「使吴书生妻不骂贼，一辱之忍，今归弗死矣」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1256848_comment'></div>为吴生言其取死时状然。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1256848_comment'></div>同时有南雄李科妻谢氏，保昌故村人，陷于虔盗。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1256848_comment'></div>留盗中数日，有欲与之床笫谋，谢吐其面曰：「宁杀我，我不汝徇也」！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1256848_comment'></div>盗怒刭之而去。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1256848_comment'></div>后十有七年，予来岭南，有僧希赐、秀才黄文谟雅为予说如此，予叹息久之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1256848_comment'></div>洪子曰：自《周南》之诗熄，姆傅师保职废，为女妇者瞢不识彤管之为何物。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1256848_comment'></div>旷二三百年得一人，史氏必谨志之，曰烈女。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1256848_comment'></div>今夫谭、谢二氏出于越绝下邑荛人蓬藋之家耳，不熟衿缡帨鞶之戒，无珩璜琚瑀之节，习贯见闻又非有则范以自厉也，一旦横逆不挠，无所顾惜，视其死与牖下不异，视书史刘更生所记摩肩无少惭，可不为难得乎？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1256848_comment'></div>此予所以兴叹也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1256848_comment'></div>人之生东西南北，不常味人善于齿牙间者，不一能然也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_19_1256848_comment'></div>使予无南来，希赐、黄文谟不我告，则谭、谢之事，今虽在人间，极不过十数年歇矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_20_1256848_comment'></div>用是以占山林膏壤之士，修洁履蹈，没没不得传，同烟云变灭者，可胜道哉！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_21_1256848_comment'></div>此予所以又叹也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_22_1256848_comment'></div>言之无文，行之不远，若扬烈妇高，悯女虽贤，得李习之之文，是以名益彰。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_23_1256848_comment'></div>予识痹名隘，文不足有所起，则夫二妇人虽幸而得书，与不传等耳。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_24_1256848_comment'></div>此予所以又叹也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_25_1256848_comment'></div>作《英州南雄二节妇传》。</div><div id='poem_sentence_26_1256848_comment'></div></div></div><br /></div>
-----end



-----title
赣州
-----detail
<div class='label1' id='334b31ec4acb474d852080decad94fac_label'><a href='javascript: DetailSwitch("334b31ec4acb474d852080decad94fac");'><span id='334b31ec4acb474d852080decad94fac_link' class='switch'>—</span></a><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1147&endYear=1147')">1147年</a>，25岁</div><div id='334b31ec4acb474d852080decad94fac' class='detail'><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1147&endYear=1147')">1147年8月2日</a>　父皓南迁至虔州，迈与季弟从行。<br /></div><div class='label1' id='1c8cd4757f91415b84276bfe46466c6d_label'><a href='javascript: DetailSwitch("1c8cd4757f91415b84276bfe46466c6d");'><span id='1c8cd4757f91415b84276bfe46466c6d_link' class='switch'>—</span></a><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1170&endYear=1173')">1170-1173年</a>，48-51岁</div><div id='1c8cd4757f91415b84276bfe46466c6d' class='detail'><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1170&endYear=1170')">1170年</a>　起知赣州。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1170&endYear=1170')">1170年</a>　友人向巨源《葵斋杂稿》成，请迈为序。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1170&endYear=1170')">1170年</a>　洪遵以灵溪庄赡学，洪迈作学记。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1171&endYear=1171')">1171年</a>　在赣州任，是岁江浙大旱，江西饥馑，赣适中熟，迈令移粟济邻郡。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1171&endYear=1171')">1171年5月18日</a>　《夷坚丙志》二十卷成。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1171&endYear=1171')">1171年8月</a>　友人汪澈卒，迈作《铭》。作品：汪庄敏铭。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1171&endYear=1171')">1171年11月14日</a>　赣守曹观离任，迈有送序。作品：送曹赣州序。<div id='poem_1256750' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1256750' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1256750?labeling=true' target='_blank'>送曹赣州序</a><span class='authorDate'>（乾道七年十一月）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 南宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(28601, "南宋", "洪迈", "poem_title_1256750")'>洪迈</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1256750_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1256750'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1256750'>开封曹侯守赣三年有四月，乃得代去。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1256750_comment'></div>去之日，代者番阳洪迈出祖于十里津亭上，举酒挹之曰：曹大夫仕宦至二千石，古称人生五马贵，陛下垂意方内，为斯民宅牧，地无小，官无卑，其去其还，必赐延英对。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1256750_comment'></div>虽台寺要职更内外，非真守一郡不得入尚书为郎。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1256750_comment'></div>苟以是官至造膝，正合上心，其联清骛华，直探物笥中耳。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1256750_comment'></div>然郡国或荒寒不可治，积为长吏忧。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1256750_comment'></div>今年天惜雨，自湘沔西江放乎彭蠡之滨，盖数百城皆莫得善岁。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1256750_comment'></div>唯赣也独中熟，人人言侯治状昭卓可称道。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1256750_comment'></div>天用畀之嘉祥，章明其功，持归报天子，用以足占侯之策，富贵不待證龟蔡也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1256750_comment'></div>为我竟此爵谢曹大夫。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1256750_comment'></div>霜风鸣冬，万木僵立，黄鹤高遰，戛摩青云，鹪鹩啐啄空谷中，冀附翼而翔讵可得！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1256750_comment'></div>于是船鼓三通，仆夫趣整驾，侯去矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1256750_comment'></div>乾道七年十一月十四日序。</div><div id='poem_sentence_11_1256750_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1171&endYear=1171')">1171年11月29日</a><div id='poem_1256790' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1256790' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1256790?labeling=true' target='_blank'>跋苏颍滨诗帖</a><span class='authorDate'>（乾道七年十一月）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 南宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(28601, "南宋", "洪迈", "poem_title_1256790")'>洪迈</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1256790_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1256790'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1256790'>两苏公帖平生多见之，盖真赝相半也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1256790_comment'></div>从季所藏如渊明诗一纸，虽掷弃瓦砾，当自有神光发见。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1256790_comment'></div>乾道七年十一月廿九日，洪迈书。</div><div id='poem_sentence_2_1256790_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1171&endYear=1171')">1171年</a>　婺源令洪邦直新修县学，遣信请作《婺源县儒学记》。作品：婺源县儒学记。<span class='inlineComment2'>（是年前后，伯兄洪适有诗相寄。）</span><div id='poem_1256812' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1256812' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1256812?labeling=true' target='_blank'>婺源新学记<span class='inlineComment2'>（乾道九年闰正月）</span></a><span class='authorDate'>（1171年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 南宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(28601, "南宋", "洪迈", "poem_title_1256812")'>洪迈</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1256812_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1256812'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1256812'>江东俗本嚚于讼，歙浪受其名，婺源人重不幸，至席鼎汤最沸之目。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1256812_comment'></div>县人翰林汪公藻、吏部朱公松，用文章行谊表表独立，不忍视乡曲蒙恶，顾而之他邦，纷闵闵焉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1256812_comment'></div>诸生时相与言，学宫在西边九十五年，寖入于坏，地势暗昧，青衿不能群居，阴阳家流杂指山乡背为不韪，当徙而趋新，士大夫滋益多，淫谤宜革。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1256812_comment'></div>是时乾道岁戊子，令彭君烜曰：「嘻，吾责也，将安所易置乎」？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1256812_comment'></div>曰：「吉莫如城东驿」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1256812_comment'></div>君曰：「是在部使者，非吾实颛」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1256812_comment'></div>合诸生请之而俞，且至五十万钱侑费，倾县大喜。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1256812_comment'></div>儒生王允恭、李知己并捐其旁便近地，倡出钱粟。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1256812_comment'></div>诸公闻，欢趋之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1256812_comment'></div>即其冬，庙殿及藏书阁咸垂就矣，合郡守好恶异，疑县持以计特歛民，书揭邀愬章，至换他健吏。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1256812_comment'></div>耳目钩讦亡一词，始抟颊愧悔，听绪成之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1256812_comment'></div>然首议者倦矣，谢工遣徒，仆木撤瓦，丞尉亦惩艾祸，噤不复发口。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1256812_comment'></div>独殿阁栖棘篱中不敢毁，望之愀然。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1256812_comment'></div>又三年，后令洪君邦直至，为后守史侯言，侯矍然悼前，故曰：「二千石惟不兴学，县令揽众谋自办之，靳靳尼其成，安取此」！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1256812_comment'></div>即出郡钱六十万，使讫役。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1256812_comment'></div>既萎而苏，既偻而伸，民又益喜勇劝，视曩时倍数。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1256812_comment'></div>月顷，百室之宫成，靓深广盱，不啬于素，过者心开目明，毋间处者。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1256812_comment'></div>于是隽秀士滕生恪以降百有一人介令为容，遣信千八百里走赣川，合词告鄱阳洪迈曰：愿有以记。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1256812_comment'></div>予乡壤与斯邑接，令君又宗盟长，其得辞？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1256812_comment'></div>今之学若古之塾也，庠序之制，既以糟粕仅存，至于主敬以直内，主义以方外，致知格物之本，穷理尽性之要，正心诚意之传，绵绵延延，如线不绝。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_19_1256812_comment'></div>曾子且死，不忍一箦之姑息，举扶而易之；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_20_1256812_comment'></div>季路临大难，正冠结缨之暇，如在洙泗；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_21_1256812_comment'></div>工尹商阳，手弓而杀人，掩目止御，不忘有礼。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_22_1256812_comment'></div>死生之变，争战之急，亦大矣，而归趣如此，况乎从容进退、洒扫寝食之间哉？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_23_1256812_comment'></div>少成若天性，习惯如自然，古之人欤？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_24_1256812_comment'></div>其天资高明，后世虽不可跂及，向非学问，辅以谊士，有不能教民而驱使战，是谓弃民；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_25_1256812_comment'></div>不素养士而望其必然，斯为弃士。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_26_1256812_comment'></div>宜国家拳拳致力，立学遍海内，临之官师，而不容释也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_27_1256812_comment'></div>呜呼！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_28_1256812_comment'></div>事难兴而易败。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_29_1256812_comment'></div>今夫是役，有邑子开先，部使者畀其地，县大夫慭为之，而职教化者顾不可，功十八而画。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_30_1256812_comment'></div>历四年，阅两令，始克溃于成。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_31_1256812_comment'></div>故予诘曲登载，验其至难。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_32_1256812_comment'></div>后之君子朝夕游于斯，尚思先王之所以教，古人之所以行，朝廷所以留意，翰林、吏部烨然之光辉，祭酒之所以急，利其春辉，以既秋实，穷高极深，暴白成就，使远近称颂，曰婺源又有人。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_33_1256812_comment'></div>若是乃答令君本意，科第馀事耳。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_34_1256812_comment'></div>乾道九年闰正月二日，左太中大夫、充集英殿修撰、知赣州军州、提举学事、馀干县开国子、食邑五百户洪迈撰并书。</div><div id='poem_sentence_35_1256812_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1172&endYear=1172')">1172年</a>　是年，在赣州任。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1172&endYear=1172')">1172年2月</a>　奏赣州狱空。朝廷降诏奖谕。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1172&endYear=1172')">1172年5月</a>　以会稽本《夷坚乙志》别刻于赣，去五事，易二事，其他亦颇有改定处。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1172&endYear=1172')">1172年</a>　雩都县灌婴庙旁耕得古瓦，迈取作砚，铭之。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1172&endYear=1172')">1172年9月</a>　跋孝宗赐虞允文诗。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1172&endYear=1172')">1172年11月</a>　再奏赣州狱空。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1172&endYear=1172')">1172年12月9日</a>　作《徙赣县东尉治记》。<div id='poem_1256811' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1256811' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1256811?labeling=true' target='_blank'>徙赣县东尉治记</a><span class='authorDate'>（乾道八年十二月）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 南宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(28601, "南宋", "洪迈", "poem_title_1256811")'>洪迈</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1256811_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1256811'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1256811'>赣尉分东西，久皆治郡下，仍其方以居。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1256811_comment'></div>东部廨残于兵，寄而即西偏萧寺，历年所不能自还，与西俱西，地爽其实。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1256811_comment'></div>尉掾参军，短于才力，盖皆录录尘埃间，视景蚤莫，势不暇小有建立，指日得践更，逝如脱兔。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1256811_comment'></div>郡县之长吏固莫或知，知之亦莫或问，如是殆三十年。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1256811_comment'></div>予之来守也，事建东江飞梁。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1256811_comment'></div>邑长赵颜何始为予言，尉以东名官而强颜为西，赘位无小，于窥观不宜。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1256811_comment'></div>幸得徙归之，正名居方，畀桥为安，一役而两利集，计成便。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1256811_comment'></div>于是尉官缺，南康田橡捧檄来摄承，忘其身之羁，毕力关策，经行空旷地，度可容百室者。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1256811_comment'></div>即日得南距桥仅百步，愿民致喜，或持圃券以献。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1256811_comment'></div>古道傍出，尚约略可寻，政走雷冈径也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1256811_comment'></div>蓁秽积五纪，霅然雾开，天藏而神閟之定有数。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1256811_comment'></div>基具矣，安所得居。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1256811_comment'></div>郡有邸一区，其左物或冯焉，僦不售，撤以为之堂，又取野庐三楹以立厅事。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1256811_comment'></div>费无巨颣，皆我之自出，盖不伐一木而迄成。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1256811_comment'></div>吏士环居，整芘如翼，过者辍步驩叹。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1256811_comment'></div>老道士年八九十，日见蒇就，亦洒然以惊。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1256811_comment'></div>予曰人不难锐始，及必，玩假板嬴禄，逆旅尸厥官。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1256811_comment'></div>且赵令君秩过期，新令鼎来，民听怀向背；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1256811_comment'></div>真尉又扣镜，田不可留。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1256811_comment'></div>然皆曰即得斯役成，吾顾接浙去此。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_19_1256811_comment'></div>予既其实，味其言，赏之以酒而为事其事。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_20_1256811_comment'></div>且告之曰，国家方急材，二子往矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_21_1256811_comment'></div>乾道八年十有二月九日记。</div><div id='poem_sentence_22_1256811_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1172&endYear=1172')">1172年</a>　王资重建南雄州种玉亭，请迈作记。作品：种玉亭记。<div id='poem_1256826' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1256826' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1256826?labeling=true' target='_blank'>南雍州池亭记</a><span class='authorDate'>（1172年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 南宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(28601, "南宋", "洪迈", "poem_title_1256826")'>洪迈</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1256826_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1256826'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1256826'>观山者必于终南、二华、天台、赤城，观水者必于五湖、三江，适梁、魏、周、秦然后极通都大邑之盛，不登凌风之台、黄云之楼，却月露寒之观，不足以游目骋怀，竟瑰壮绝特之美，彼夸者之谈则然。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1256826_comment'></div>若是而充之，马必须蒲梢齧膝之骏，饮必中山桑落之酒，炰太官之羔，炊共城之稻，鲙秋风之鲈、槎头之鳊，郑、卫娥媌以为御，孟公、君卿以为客，冬室暖，夏室寒，朝经而夕纬之，中心萦绕，如车汰辀万，宁有足理？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1256826_comment'></div>今吾环堵之宫，把茅盖头，开数椽之窗，扫隙地五六尺，植竹数十个，田父过我，倾浊醪老瓦盆中，张两脚如箕，径醉辄睡，无人乎柴门之下，独昌翔其间，由我者吾，岂不大好？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1256826_comment'></div>夫是之谓随寓而安，则吾焉往而不为胜？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1256826_comment'></div>庾岭之南七十里，以雄名州，当孔道往来之门，候人者日缘续不绝。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1256826_comment'></div>守居不宽绰，又无高明爽垲之临以舒厥心。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1256826_comment'></div>主诺者幸满秩决去，何用知委蛇退食之可乐！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1256826_comment'></div>听事之东故有池，延袤且十亩，满中白芙蕖，千叶而实。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1256826_comment'></div>池心突然，亭亡而址存，不知几年数。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1256826_comment'></div>豫章王稚川至，颇有意复之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1256826_comment'></div>得废寺弃材，西向作屋，周以栏，廓然四澈，榜曰「种玉亭」，直北堤贯中，架梁以往。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1256826_comment'></div>又南向作屋，罗群山于雉堞之外，榜曰「挹翠亭」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1256826_comment'></div>池亭距黄堂不费步武，脱阛阓嚣尘，而山薮林壑之胜具。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1256826_comment'></div>天实开稚川，锐使为之，以为凌江上善第一妙境。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1256826_comment'></div>人人指岭表为瘴邑，讵知所谓随寓而安者，顾乃不啻足耶？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1256826_comment'></div>稚川佳公子，善属文，作郡有治理效，上官贤之，雄民不能淹使留，更数月当去。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1256826_comment'></div>其未去也，举杯中之渌，并栏长吟。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1256826_comment'></div>有信来，傥以示我。</div><div id='poem_sentence_17_1256826_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1173&endYear=1173')">1173年闰1月10日</a>　刘子和赴官赣州，周必大有诗相送，兼简洪迈，赠诗有“人留河内寇，帝念禁中颇”之句，迈次其韵。作品：周丈直院侍郎以诗送子和教授之官兼以见简且及夷坚丁志辄次其韵。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1173&endYear=1173')">1173年</a>　司马光曾孙伋出镇广州，道过赣州，迈获见司马光亲书《客位榜》。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1173&endYear=1173')">1173年2月7日</a>　奏赣州狱空。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1173&endYear=1173')">1173年</a>　冬至郊祀改元，迈有贺表。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1173&endYear=1173')">1173年</a>　是年，有《山堂学记》、《新桥记》及诗示周必大。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1173&endYear=1173')">1173年</a>　作《赣州学记》。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1173&endYear=1173')">1173年</a>　罢赣守，送者十六人，有诗。<br /></div>
-----end

韶关
