-----title
福州
-----detail
<div class='label1' id='fdb451d85a714b5992f9ac61a49651a8_label'><a href='javascript: DetailSwitch("fdb451d85a714b5992f9ac61a49651a8");'><span id='fdb451d85a714b5992f9ac61a49651a8_link' class='switch'>—</span></a><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1148&endYear=1150')">1148-1150年</a>，26-28岁</div><div id='fdb451d85a714b5992f9ac61a49651a8' class='detail'><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1148&endYear=1148')">1148年11月</a>　至福州，为教授。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1149&endYear=1149')">1149年1月</a>　作《福州教授壁记》。<div id='poem_1256805' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1256805' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1256805?labeling=true' target='_blank'>福州教授壁记<span class='inlineComment2'>（绍兴十九年正月）</span></a><span class='authorDate'>（1149年1月）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 南宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(28601, "南宋", "洪迈", "poem_title_1256805")'>洪迈</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1256805_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1256805'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1256805'>自庆历诏书，郡国大抵悉有学，而立官教授则由熙宁始。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1256805_comment'></div>然服岭以南，草山小州若被边初郡，或自诡偪仄，或生长兵间，虽与闻德音，或谦让未遑也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1256805_comment'></div>至崇宁、大观，乃极盛。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1256805_comment'></div>凡版在职方者，必建学如中州。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1256805_comment'></div>教授虽秩卑，吏部勿敢豫，必宰相自推择，而大郡多至四三员，文风张施，古无有也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1256805_comment'></div>陛下宅天命盖十有六载，立太学，置博士，悉还太平之治，而郡国立学除吏，复一切如先朝时。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1256805_comment'></div>福于东南最大，为督府，自平时最多士，故领袖学官者员多，类以进士高第得左官铮铮搢绅间者为之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1256805_comment'></div>绍兴十八年十一月癸巳，鄱阳洪迈至。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1256805_comment'></div>十二月辛酉，建安刘祥至。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1256805_comment'></div>迈捷取径路得一第，刘君以《易》书合上意，顾得之皆非所谓高进士选者。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1256805_comment'></div>惧不称时，相与言曰：「我曹特幸耳，若又饫其家而饥其徒，弗学之问不可」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1256805_comment'></div>乃旦旦坐直庐，稍挈纲维，苴补破坏。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1256805_comment'></div>凡泉谷之在民未入者，上诸二千石，悉索之，移长度于计台，取振其所乏，廥廪颇益实。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1256805_comment'></div>峨冠束带，朝莫必谨，毋敢不谒而归。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1256805_comment'></div>既略定，有士前曰：「自吾学张官至今若干人，名数具在，倘仍弗纪录，惧其年多而莫知也，愿石而刻之」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1256805_comment'></div>予曰：「诚然」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1256805_comment'></div>吏以文书来，顷而籍至，则某人某人，皆在不遗，于是志诸壁，而由夫林君迪始。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1256805_comment'></div>十九年正月十四日记<sup class='reference inlineComment2'>⑴</sup>。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1256805_comment'></div></div><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_18_1256805'>或：《国朝二百家名贤文粹》作「咸」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1256805_comment'></div>又「让」作「逊」。</div><div id='poem_sentence_19_1256805_comment'></div></div><div class='poemNote' id='poem_note_1256805'><div class='inline1'><div id='poem_sentence_17_1256805_0'>⑴ 《古今事文类聚》外集卷一三。又见《国朝二百家名贤文粹》卷一二八，《洪文敏公集》卷六。</div></div></div><div id='poem_note_1256805_comment'></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1149&endYear=1149')">1149年</a>　因春补诸生，邀友人叶晦叔同考校，有唱酬。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1149&endYear=1149')">1149年</a>　撰公家谢表、祈晴雨文及圣节乐语。作品：谢历日表。<div id='poem_1256690' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1256690' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1256690?labeling=true' target='_blank'>谢历日表</a><span class='authorDate'>（1149年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 南宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(28601, "南宋", "洪迈", "poem_title_1256690")'>洪迈</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1256690_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1256690'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1256690'>真主当阳，载谨占天之义；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1256690_comment'></div>畴人观象，一新底日之文。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1256690_comment'></div>方中诏之分颁，均外台而重拜<span class='inlineComment2'>（中谢。）</span>。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1256690_comment'></div>恭惟皇帝陛下尧身为度，舜历在躬。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1256690_comment'></div>知天其有五材，守而勿失；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1256690_comment'></div>对时而育万物，动则有成。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1256690_comment'></div>尝思利用以厚生，不怠履端而举正。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1256690_comment'></div>坦然明白，奉以周旋。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1256690_comment'></div>臣敢不祗诵成书，虔遵至意？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1256690_comment'></div>七月流火，益知王业之艰难；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1256690_comment'></div>五星连珠，莫测圣功之辅相。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1256690_comment'></div></div><div id='poem_sentence_11_1256690_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1149&endYear=1149')">1149年</a>　有《代福建提举茶事谢上表》<div id='poem_1256679' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1256679' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1256679?labeling=true' target='_blank'>代福建提举茶事谢上表<span class='inlineComment2'>（复兼常平）</span></a><span class='authorDate'>（1149年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 南宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(28601, "南宋", "洪迈", "poem_title_1256679")'>洪迈</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1256679_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1256679'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1256679'>总浪舶于三吴，讫微善状；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1256679_comment'></div>按云艘于百越，复冒除书。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1256679_comment'></div>揆日问涂，挟辰诣部<span class='inlineComment2'>（中谢）</span>。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1256679_comment'></div>窃以汉规先具，开边籴以均输；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1256679_comment'></div>唐务富藏，藉关征而赡本。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1256679_comment'></div>虽有便民之志，颇乖实廪之宜。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1256679_comment'></div>纷更旋夺于廷臣，捐瘠或随于军用。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1256679_comment'></div>迨中世徙场而榷茗，致诸蕃塌地以名钱。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1256679_comment'></div>大抵虚文，蔑闻见效。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1256679_comment'></div>伟圣明之立制，张职守以建官。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1256679_comment'></div>吏偶失于三思，事寖成于一切。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1256679_comment'></div>维时改作，尽复旧章。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1256679_comment'></div>自非通敏之流，曷副班宣之责？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1256679_comment'></div>如臣者猥蒙世赏，辱在周行。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1256679_comment'></div>无材能阀阅之劳，固宜尺退；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1256679_comment'></div>习功利分铢之事，岂有寸长？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1256679_comment'></div>曾是使华，荐沾恩纪。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1256679_comment'></div>兹盖伏遇皇帝陛下，体天刚健，措国清宁。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1256679_comment'></div>总六服以收贤，明德远矣；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1256679_comment'></div>访万几而询政，使人器之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_19_1256679_comment'></div>遂令朝著之微，亦玷輶轩之寄。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_20_1256679_comment'></div>臣敢不裒多益寡，散滞取赢？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_21_1256679_comment'></div>一身而二任之加，勉祗承于上意；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_22_1256679_comment'></div>三登遗九年之食，庶还定于王民。</div><div id='poem_sentence_23_1256679_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1149&endYear=1149')">1149年</a>　有《代陆提举漳州谢上表》<div id='poem_1256684' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1256684' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1256684?labeling=true' target='_blank'>代陆提举漳州谢上表</a><span class='authorDate'>（1149年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 南宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(28601, "南宋", "洪迈", "poem_title_1256684")'>洪迈</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1256684_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1256684'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1256684'>乘轺东广，初无华远之功；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1256684_comment'></div>分屏南州，更受牧人之寄。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1256684_comment'></div>即趋官署，祗布诏条<span class='inlineComment2'>（中谢。）</span>。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1256684_comment'></div>伏念臣一介微生，七闽琐隶。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1256684_comment'></div>抱关击柝，居自分于尘埃；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1256684_comment'></div>揽辔登车，忽滥蒙于推择。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1256684_comment'></div>偶逭官刑之逮，敢期天宠之加！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1256684_comment'></div>惟是漳江，素称道院。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1256684_comment'></div>圣贤相遇，坐收无侮之威；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1256684_comment'></div>草野虽愚，亦识有生之乐。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1256684_comment'></div>名为郡守，不异家居。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1256684_comment'></div>辄叨符竹之荣，仍托乡闾之便。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1256684_comment'></div>曾何侥倖，为是遭逢！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1256684_comment'></div>兹盖伏遇皇帝陛下日月合明，乾坤同量。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1256684_comment'></div>任贤勿贰，立太师兹惟三公；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1256684_comment'></div>恭己无为，履至尊而制六合。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1256684_comment'></div>迭选循良之吏，奉行宽大之书。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1256684_comment'></div>臣顾以衰残，莫胜委付。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1256684_comment'></div>安庶民而忘叹息，勉躬导于明恩；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1256684_comment'></div>敬盛德而赋中和，更力裒于善类。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_19_1256684_comment'></div></div><div id='poem_sentence_20_1256684_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1149&endYear=1149')">1149年</a>　访何大圭，讨论天文。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1149&endYear=1149')">1149年</a>　于吕虚己、僧智恢处分别见邵武上官校书诗一册、吴僧法具诗稿一纸。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1149&endYear=1149')">1149年</a>　于《道藏》见《周易举正》一书而传之。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1150&endYear=1150')">1150年</a>　以郡博士被檄考试临漳。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1150&endYear=1150')">1150年</a>　自福倅满归，叶晦叔有诗送别。<br /></div>
-----end



-----title
广州
-----detail
<div class='label1' id='1eb673be96f0479d9dd17c4a0ec3aa93_label'><a href='javascript: DetailSwitch("1eb673be96f0479d9dd17c4a0ec3aa93");'><span id='1eb673be96f0479d9dd17c4a0ec3aa93_link' class='switch'>—</span></a><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1154&endYear=1155')">1154-1155年</a>，32-33岁</div><div id='1eb673be96f0479d9dd17c4a0ec3aa93' class='detail'><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1154&endYear=1154')">1154年</a>　黄公度高要倅期满，帅方滋置酒，令迈作乐语。迈时摄帅司机宜。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1154&endYear=1154')">1154年</a>　有诗赋素馨，有“遐陬不遇赏拔之叹”，友人黄公度和之。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1155&endYear=1155')">1155年4月20日</a>　作《重修广州都盐仓记》。<div id='poem_1256806' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1256806' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1256806?labeling=true' target='_blank'>重修广州都盐仓记<span class='inlineComment2'>（绍兴二十五年四月）</span></a><span class='authorDate'>（1155年4月20日）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 南宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(28601, "南宋", "洪迈", "poem_title_1256806")'>洪迈</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1256806_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1256806'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1256806'>客从东方来，道南粤，顾瞻其山川，乐甚，为解辔少留。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1256806_comment'></div>时时游父老间，颇得闻粤中贤大夫事。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1256806_comment'></div>始则毛举枚具一二数，不悉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1256806_comment'></div>客隘而面之曰：「丈人休矣，盍置此而新其说乎」？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1256806_comment'></div>一人茫然长思，食顷，乃言曰：「客果欲知之耶，则吾部使者陆公真其人。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1256806_comment'></div>自朝廷合常平茶盐之政，相更五六官，因仍为容，豢蠹弗剔，鄢引岁月，储敝无地。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1256806_comment'></div>而公寻端摘绪，昼暮訾省，利出害去，逌然一新。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1256806_comment'></div>顾吾能老而已，不暇细语客，姑告客以都盐仓之故。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1256806_comment'></div>岭南鹾卤为市，与他道百，而吾州南肘大海，厥土广潟，牢盆取赢，又百他郡。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1256806_comment'></div>异时不官以临，不廥以贮，指庳宇数列借为仓称鬻。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1256806_comment'></div>盐狎至，或露积不墉，不泜于涂泥则回入主吏，稽商蹛财，上下一息。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1256806_comment'></div>公能出笑谈于期年，峙屋二百，修廊缦回，檐角骞舞，重栏杰栋，演迤嵽臬，而吾一民不与知。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1256806_comment'></div>岁计甲乙，旧为缗钱五十万，大抵不能滞。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1256806_comment'></div>今直数月主办，方求益县官，至上百万未止。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1256806_comment'></div>使得如汉仓庾氏世公子孙，吾侪小人，衣食而羡于盐足矣」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1256806_comment'></div>客曰：「父老而不前闻，昔公为莆阳，以忠厚长者近民，咏歌不可足，至溢为嘉麦、灵芝、爵玉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1256806_comment'></div>邑之三瑞，固已绘诸天朝，特书史官，持以试南宫士，荦荦然惊人。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1256806_comment'></div>惠敛兹土，如万分一。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1256806_comment'></div>方将都通藩，取介位，雁行天子从官，振前之光明。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1256806_comment'></div>诏书且下不久，父老虽惜，亦安得常常而见之？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_19_1256806_comment'></div>及今成计，买石诵烈，寄后日亡穷思，其可也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_20_1256806_comment'></div>客故倦游，尚能从笔研事，父老亦有意乎」？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_21_1256806_comment'></div>皆再拜伛谢曰：「幸甚！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_22_1256806_comment'></div>愿卒如上客教」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_23_1256806_comment'></div>公名涣，字允济，长乐人。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_24_1256806_comment'></div>客，番阳洪迈也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_25_1256806_comment'></div>绍兴二十五年四月二十日记。</div><div id='poem_sentence_26_1256806_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1155&endYear=1155')">1155年</a><div id='poem_1256830' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1256830' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1256830?labeling=true' target='_blank'>修天庆观三清殿记</a><span class='authorDate'>（1155年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 南宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(28601, "南宋", "洪迈", "poem_title_1256830")'>洪迈</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1256830_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1256830'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1256830'>通天下郡国有观宇，天庆最盛；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1256830_comment'></div>合天地百神至于上帝，三清其最尊。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1256830_comment'></div>以最盛奉最尊，故宜仙都珠庭，清穆闲敞，称所以揭虔妥灵之意。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1256830_comment'></div>广州观在郡西北隅，宫室规模，阘茸不壮。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1256830_comment'></div>所谓三清殿尤压迮莝陋，殆中人居不如。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1256830_comment'></div>东行西詹，观睨郁悒。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1256830_comment'></div>讳才惜力，何人肯一引手！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1256830_comment'></div>黄冠栖栖，无策可出，高圆主张，理若有待。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1256830_comment'></div>使持节常平茶盐事陆公涣始至，以令谒圣祖庭下，经行前除，延目毕览，心以为不然。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1256830_comment'></div>既而瞿然曰：「上天尊神在是观，祈祷吾君，官于斯宜毋敢不领责，更新之图必我也」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1256830_comment'></div>即以公家钱节而储之，又益以私钱，度为百五十万，简吏廉可使者相其役。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1256830_comment'></div>期年而殿成，睟容端章，黼坐俨赫，金史玉童，拱立擎侍，瓜华香火之案，榱题牖楯之节，户不改席，光辉烛人，恍如乘焱车羽轮而上觌紫皇于琼宫，不知犹吾南海也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1256830_comment'></div>功甫讫，公擢藩临漳，有日东去。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1256830_comment'></div>于是道士陈行坚帅邦之秀民二十有六人来，合辞言曰，愿有所记。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1256830_comment'></div>天子万年，介尔景福，公之于吾君也；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1256830_comment'></div>俾尔昌而炽，俾尔寿而富，吾民之于公也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1256830_comment'></div>迈既书其事，且又系之以诗，其辞曰：</div><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_16_1256830'>天池北阯，粤岭东麓。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1256830_comment'></div>银宫<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_17_1256830", 1256830, "Clauses/63/Comments/0")'>旟旟</span>，瑶殿谡谡。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1256830_comment'></div>陛纳九齿，阊披四目。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1256830_comment'></div>楯角储清，檐牙袤缛。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_19_1256830_comment'></div>雕牖𧮳閕，镂楹熠煜。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_20_1256830_comment'></div>元尊端拱，泰上秉录。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_21_1256830_comment'></div>绣黼<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_22_1256830", 1256830, "Clauses/73/Comments/0")'>周张</span>，神光<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_22_1256830", 1256830, "Clauses/74/Comments/0")'>晬穆</span>。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_22_1256830_comment'></div>宝帐流黄，温屏结绿。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_23_1256830_comment'></div>翠凤千旗，紫电溜褥。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_24_1256830_comment'></div>星伯振鹭，仙翁立鹄。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_25_1256830_comment'></div>昌明侍几，眉连捧纛。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_26_1256830_comment'></div>月节下堕，曦轮傍烛。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_27_1256830_comment'></div>涷雨清尘，矞云散縠。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_28_1256830_comment'></div>钓籁虚徐，流铃陆续。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_29_1256830_comment'></div>童初渟瀯，岣嵝蓄缩。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_30_1256830_comment'></div>岳君有衡，海帝惟倏。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_31_1256830_comment'></div>中边何卫，时节朝宿。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_32_1256830_comment'></div>飓母沦威，疟妃谢毒。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_33_1256830_comment'></div>丹崖罢徼，赤子累福。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_34_1256830_comment'></div>亿龄圣寿，万世永箓。</div><div id='poem_sentence_35_1256830_comment'></div></div></div><br /></div>
-----end



-----title
宜春
-----detail

ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1157&endYear=1157')">1157年9月</a>　还自衡岳，道宜春，买舟东下。永嘉方景南置酒秀川馆饯之。黄景达、向巨源、许季韶皆与坐中联句作诗，有《秀川馆联句》。<div id='poem_179647' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_179647' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/179647?labeling=true' target='_blank'>秀川馆联句</a><span class='authorDate'>（1157年9月）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 南宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(28601, "南宋", "洪迈", "poem_title_179647")'>洪迈</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_179647_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_179647'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_179647'>江声床摇寒，山色窗拗绿<span class='inlineComment2'>（方）</span>。<div id='poem_sentence_0_179647_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_179647'>归舟著沙边，客梦绕乡曲<span class='inlineComment2'>（洪）</span>。<div id='poem_sentence_1_179647_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_179647'>簪盍豁秋悲，筵开从夜卜<span class='inlineComment2'>（黄）</span>。<div id='poem_sentence_2_179647_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_3_179647'>黄花散疏篱，苍竹围破屋<span class='inlineComment2'>（向）</span>。<div id='poem_sentence_3_179647_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_4_179647'>诗豪争击铜，谈剧屡消烛<span class='inlineComment2'>（许）</span>。<div id='poem_sentence_4_179647_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_5_179647'>借君五言城，洗我万斛愁<span class='inlineComment2'>（方）</span>。<div id='poem_sentence_5_179647_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_6_179647'>主人意无穷，客子去敢速<span class='inlineComment2'>（洪）</span>。<div id='poem_sentence_6_179647_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_7_179647'>杯宽怯鲸吞，词涩愧貂续<span class='inlineComment2'>（黄）</span>。<div id='poem_sentence_7_179647_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_8_179647'>注瓦亦倾银，联珠仍缀玉<span class='inlineComment2'>（向）</span>。<div id='poem_sentence_8_179647_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_9_179647'>天迥月明洲，霜清风陨木<span class='inlineComment2'>（许）</span>。<div id='poem_sentence_9_179647_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_10_179647'>飞齐水击鹏，挥退日斜鵩<span class='inlineComment2'>（方）</span>。<div id='poem_sentence_10_179647_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_11_179647'>臭味漆投胶，芬芳兰间菊<span class='inlineComment2'>（洪）</span>。<div id='poem_sentence_11_179647_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_12_179647'>味甘一脔尝，话胜十年读<span class='inlineComment2'>（黄）</span>。<div id='poem_sentence_12_179647_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_13_179647'>未用赋骊驹，方看举鸿鹄<span class='inlineComment2'>（向）</span>。<div id='poem_sentence_13_179647_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_14_179647'>行当岁九迁，勿惮昼三宿<span class='inlineComment2'>（许）</span>。<div id='poem_sentence_14_179647_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_15_179647'>妙语子蝉嫣，孤踪吾鹿独<span class='inlineComment2'>（方）</span>。<div id='poem_sentence_15_179647_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_16_179647'>一老上星辰，三君进凫鹜<span class='inlineComment2'>（洪）</span>。<div id='poem_sentence_16_179647_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_17_179647'>平生仰高山，此夕沾剩馥<span class='inlineComment2'>（黄）</span>。<div id='poem_sentence_17_179647_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_18_179647'>飞龙十九章，金马三千牍<span class='inlineComment2'>（向）</span>。<div id='poem_sentence_18_179647_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_19_179647'>傥非论石渠，定是雠天禄<span class='inlineComment2'>（许）</span>。<div id='poem_sentence_19_179647_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_20_179647'>笔健翻狂澜，辩雄喷飞瀑<span class='inlineComment2'>（方）</span>。<div id='poem_sentence_20_179647_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_21_179647'>抄传疲小胥，侍立倦更仆<span class='inlineComment2'>（洪）</span>。<div id='poem_sentence_21_179647_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_22_179647'>力举六鳌连，肘运千兔秃<span class='inlineComment2'>（方）</span>。<div id='poem_sentence_22_179647_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_23_179647'>庖厨洗玉盘，萍豆鄙金谷<span class='inlineComment2'>（向）</span>。<div id='poem_sentence_23_179647_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_24_179647'>岂无麟脯羞，亦有熊蹯熟<span class='inlineComment2'>（方）</span>。<div 南雄

-----title

-----title
建瓯
-----detail
<div class='label1' id='364e81637cd144b9ba712304e44296ba_label'><a href='javascript: DetailSwitch("364e81637cd144b9ba712304e44296ba");'><span id='364e81637cd144b9ba712304e44296ba_link' class='switch'>—</span></a><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1177&endYear=1180')">1177-1180年</a>，55-58岁</div><div id='364e81637cd144b9ba712304e44296ba' class='detail'><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1177&endYear=1177')">1177年</a>　是年，起知建宁，有谢表。作品：谢知建宁府表。<span class='inlineComment2'>（考迈以乾道四年六月去朝，十年后当在淳熙四年，故知迈知建宁府当在是年。《钱谱》系于淳熙二年，误。）</span><div id='poem_1256681' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1256681' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1256681?labeling=true' target='_blank'>谢知建宁府表</a><span class='authorDate'>（1177年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 南宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(28601, "南宋", "洪迈", "poem_title_1256681")'>洪迈</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1256681_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1256681'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1256681'>香火奉祠，所祈申命；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1256681_comment'></div>丝纶假宠，更俾治民。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1256681_comment'></div>戴恩施之非常，极糜捐而莫报<span class='inlineComment2'>（中谢。）</span>。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1256681_comment'></div>伏念臣天资戆拙，人品妄庸。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1256681_comment'></div>䌷石室之书，久惭清贯；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1256681_comment'></div>污玉堂之直，深负隆知。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1256681_comment'></div>一去京华，十周岁纪。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1256681_comment'></div>敢意诏除之下，犹居推择之中！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1256681_comment'></div>兹盖伏遇皇帝陛下游意泰和，玩心至理。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1256681_comment'></div>方搢笏垂绅之盛，岂谓乏才？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1256681_comment'></div>顾遗簪敝履之微，亦容待罪。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1256681_comment'></div>致令冗散，获殿潜藩。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1256681_comment'></div>臣尚尔怀章，未遑进谢。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1256681_comment'></div>备汉庭之笔橐，敢忘安世之忠？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1256681_comment'></div>存魏阙于江湖，更剧子牟之恋。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1256681_comment'></div></div><div id='poem_sentence_15_1256681_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1177&endYear=1177')">1177年</a>　作《泛舟游武夷九曲池》诗。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1178&endYear=1178')">1178年</a><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1179&endYear=1179')">1179年4月7日</a>　跋米元暉《潇湘图》。作品：潇湘图跋。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1179&endYear=1179')">1179年</a>　是秋，明堂大礼恩泽，改奏一岁儿。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1180&endYear=1180')">1180年2月21日</a>　作《芜湖县令厅壁记》。<div id='poem_1256814' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1256814' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1256814?labeling=true' target='_blank'>芜湖县令厅壁记</a><span class='authorDate'>（淳熙七年二月）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 南宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(28601, "南宋", "洪迈", "poem_title_1256814")'>洪迈</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1256814_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1256814'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1256814'>郡县之官难莫难于令，令不可为也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1256814_comment'></div>泉粟所入，繄两税是赖，郡裁十一二予之，或名存寔亡。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1256814_comment'></div>借曰充数，薄责征须，不少遗力。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1256814_comment'></div>偪于弱，不敢不共命，至贾市争分铢，侠取巧掇，仆救过，与法为午，而无俚之画出焉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1256814_comment'></div>法目如猬毛，举头畏触。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1256814_comment'></div>不良子险健成讼，左狙右掠，蔓游其词，以聋上官，计一行令束手矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1256814_comment'></div>昧旦坐堂上，追胥在庭，睢盱嚣呶，諠不可晓。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1256814_comment'></div>将甲乙扣其胫，惧及善人，循循而舍诸，又纳侮。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1256814_comment'></div>故佞偷宽猛均足以蹈罪，令不可为如此。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1256814_comment'></div>用是人莫肯为令，非吏部考籍而畀之，通万国无一焉可也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1256814_comment'></div>芜湖在春秋曰鸠兹，盖吴楚必争地。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1256814_comment'></div>入东晋、宋、齐，建牧立州，实为南豫，台家常选宗王名将握节往控临。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1256814_comment'></div>今虽不能邦，犹名姑孰壮县。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1256814_comment'></div>用壮为累，郡百役以要之，栩栩然而来，贸贸然而去，项领常相望也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1256814_comment'></div>挈此校彼，其视他令中为又难。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1256814_comment'></div>吴人朱似菽召以故辅臣孙捐其门，凡少年时已锐与寒畯角，推排受县。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1256814_comment'></div>自诡为此来，勇者尚其决，獧者储其笑，爱之者丛然以为忧。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1256814_comment'></div>菽召若不闻，曰吾知为百里宰而已。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1256814_comment'></div>处之期年，民吏相忘，乃若尹赏之在粟邑，东舟西舫出其涂，篙工榜人皆略能诵说其梗槩。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1256814_comment'></div>于是与予书，言：「我已伐石置厅壁，将刻前长官名氏，盍为我识之」？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_19_1256814_comment'></div>予与菽召游四十年，向所谓丛然以忧者，盖其一也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_20_1256814_comment'></div>今若此，故喜而书之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_21_1256814_comment'></div>淳熙七年二月二十有一日记。</div><div id='poem_sentence_22_1256814_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1180&endYear=1180')">1180年7月</a>　刻《夷坚》甲、乙二志于建安。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1180&endYear=1180')">1180年</a>　是秋，迈罢知建宁。<br /></div>
-----end



-----title
乐平
-----detail
<div class='label1' id='6d4eaa01eba7439c9470d827332248ad_label'><a href='javascript: DetailSwitch("6d4eaa01eba7439c9470d827332248ad");'><span id='6d4eaa01eba7439c9470d827332248ad_link' class='switch'>—</span></a><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1180&endYear=1180')">1180年</a>，58岁</div><div id='6d4eaa01eba7439c9470d827332248ad' class='detail'><span style='margin: 0 0.5em; color: gray;'>▪</span>教稚儿诵唐人绝句，取诸家遗集得五七言五千四百篇，手书为六帙。<br /><span style='margin: 0 0.5em; color: gray;'>▪</span>是岁，《容斋随笔》成，序之。<br /></div><div class='label1' id='52e9f5de80f84eeba23068f1a75e70f3_label'><a href='javascript: DetailSwitch("52e9f5de80f84eeba23068f1a75e70f3");'><span id='52e9f5de80f84eeba23068f1a75e70f3_link' class='switch'>—</span></a><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1181&endYear=1183')">1181-1183年</a>，59-61岁</div><div id='52e9f5de80f84eeba23068f1a75e70f3' class='detail'><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1181&endYear=1181')">1181年</a>　司马汉章作山雨楼，迈为之记。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1181&endYear=1181')">1181年</a>　辛弃疾席间和迈《满江红》。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1181&endYear=1181')">1181年</a>　辛弃疾带湖新居落成，迈为作《稼轩记》。<div id='poem_1256822' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1256822' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1256822?labeling=true' target='_blank'>稼轩记</a><span class='authorDate'>（1181年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 南宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(28601, "南宋", "洪迈", "poem_title_1256822")'>洪迈</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1256822_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1256822'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1256822'>国家行在武林，广信最密迩畿辅，东舟西车，蜂午错出。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1256822_comment'></div>处势便近，士大夫乐寄焉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1256822_comment'></div>环城外中买宅且百数，基局不能宽，亦曰避燥湿寒暑而已耳。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1256822_comment'></div>郡治之北可里所，故有旷土存，三面傅城，前枕澄湖，如宝带。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1256822_comment'></div>其从千有二百三十尺，其衡八百有三十尺，截然砥平，可庐以居。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1256822_comment'></div>而前乎相攸者，皆莫识其处。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1256822_comment'></div>天作地藏，择然后予。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1256822_comment'></div>济南辛侯幼安最后至，一旦独得之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1256822_comment'></div>既筑室百楹，度财占地什四，乃荒左偏以立圃，稻田泱泱，居然衍十弓。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1256822_comment'></div>意它日释位而归，必躬耕于是，故凭高作屋下临之，是为「稼轩」，而命田边立亭曰「植杖」，若将真秉耒耨之为者。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1256822_comment'></div>东冈西阜，北墅南麓，以青径欸竹，以锦路行海棠，集山有楼，婆娑有堂，信步有亭，涤研有渚，皆约略位置，规岁月绪成之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1256822_comment'></div>而主人初未之识也，绘图畀予曰：「吾甚爱吾轩，为我记」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1256822_comment'></div>予谓侯本以中州隽人，抱忠仗义，章显闻于南邦。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1256822_comment'></div>齐虏巧负国，赤手领五十骑缚取于五万众中，如挟毚兔。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1256822_comment'></div>束马衔枚，由关西奏淮，至通昼夜不粒食，壮声英槩，懦士为之兴起。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1256822_comment'></div>圣天子一见三叹息，用是简深知，入登九卿，出节使二道，四立连率，莫府顷赖。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1256822_comment'></div>氐寇作自潭，薄于江西，两地惊震，谈笑埽空之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1256822_comment'></div>使遭事会之来，挈中原，还职方，氏彼周公瑾、安石事业，侯盖饶为之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1256822_comment'></div>此志未偿，顾自诡迹，放浪林泉，从老农学稼，无亦大不可欤！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1256822_comment'></div>若予者，伥伥一世间，不能为人轩轾，乃当夫须袯襫醉眠牛背，与荛童牧孺肩相摩。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_19_1256822_comment'></div>幸未黎老时，及见侯展大功名，锦衣来归，竟厦屋潭潭之乐，将荷笠棹舟，风乎玉溪之上，因圉隶内谒，曰是尝有力于稼轩者。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_20_1256822_comment'></div>侯当辍食迎门，曲席而坐，握手一笑，拂壁间石细读之，庶不为生客。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_21_1256822_comment'></div>侯名弃疾，今以右文殿脩撰再安抚江南西路云。</div><div id='poem_sentence_22_1256822_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1181&endYear=1181')">1181年</a>　张子颜创环波亭，迈有记。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1182&endYear=1182')">1182年</a>　《夷坚戊志》成。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1183&endYear=1183')">1183年</a>　是年，在鄱阳乡里。<br /></div>
-----end



-----title
南昌
-----detail
<div class='label1' id='51d38afde0b247cd9f85a5e0b959a008_label'><a href='javascript: DetailSwitch("51d38afde0b247cd9f85a5e0b959a008");'><span id='51d38afde0b247cd9f85a5e0b959a008_link' class='switch'>—</span></a><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1181&endYear=1181')">1181年</a>，59岁</div><div id='51d38afde0b247cd9f85a5e0b959a008' class='detail'><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1181&endYear=1181')">1181年</a>　是年春，有南昌之行，伯兄洪适有词惜别，友人辛弃疾、赵善括等有和篇。<br /></div><div class='label1' id='ed6cdafbd27b4d4f9ce845297747c099_label'><a href='javascript: DetailSwitch("ed6cdafbd27b4d4f9ce845297747c099");'><span id='ed6cdafbd27b4d4f9ce845297747c099_link' class='switch'>—</span></a><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1190&endYear=1196')">1190-1196年</a>，68-74岁</div><div id='ed6cdafbd27b4d4f9ce845297747c099' class='detail'><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1190&endYear=1190')">1190年12月</a>　除提举隆兴府玉隆万寿宫，以集英殿修撰王信代。从会稽西归。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1191&endYear=1191')">1191年</a>　论子时立春。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1191&endYear=1191')">1191年3月16日</a>　序张纲《华阳集》。作品：华阳集序。<div id='poem_1256778' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1256778' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1256778?labeling=true' target='_blank'>华阳集序<span class='inlineComment2'>（绍熙二年三月）</span></a><span class='authorDate'>（1191年3月16日）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 南宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(28601, "南宋", "洪迈", "poem_title_1256778")'>洪迈</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1256778_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1256778'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1256778'>《华阳集》四十卷，故参知政事、资政殿学士章简张公所著也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1256778_comment'></div>始大观、政和间，庠序宏盛，汇四方俊造于京师。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1256778_comment'></div>公起朱方孤生，持经术骧奋，声高一时，儒先仄足敛衽。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1256778_comment'></div>比三冠伦，遂策崇政，名为第一。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1256778_comment'></div>天子当扆挹叹，有旨隮用矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1256778_comment'></div>老蔡方颛国，挽使听己，倡富贵有命之说，连拄之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1256778_comment'></div>且雅憎王黼为邪，勿忍识其面。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1256778_comment'></div>擢才学馆郎官，坎𡒄过十稔，澹然无嗟悔意，独玩心于内，不肯顷刻辍为文章。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1256778_comment'></div>每一落纸，都人即日传播，至汗漫栋宇。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1256778_comment'></div>建炎庚戌，家乡厄敌兵，箧积贮藏，六丁下取略尽，煨燔所存，仅逮百一。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1256778_comment'></div>既桧相得志，齮龁知名士恶子组织人语言买进梯祸，公在睥中，又为之阁笔袖手。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1256778_comment'></div>秦亡公亦老，故历岁久，著录不能多。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1256778_comment'></div>薨之明年，嗣子户部郎中坚蒐拾论次，合八百五十九篇，将刊镂垂世，未克而没。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1256778_comment'></div>后二十三年，嗣孙池州使君釜乃出捐家赀，板寘郡学。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1256778_comment'></div>迈首得其书，伏读之，大抵制词严而缛，表疏卷卷主敬。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1256778_comment'></div>虽莫齿退休，未尝以一篇倩人代作。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1256778_comment'></div>而讲筵故事十九章，剀切明白，如《仁宗得君人之道》、《舜不穷其民》、《光武开心见诚》《、唐太宗察上封者之奸》、《宪宗御下有术》、《文宗不能正陈夷行唯阿之罪》，皆反复致志，因事纳忠，非若等辈区区备课程而已。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1256778_comment'></div>池州以书索序，顾晚出辽绝，欲谢不敢，念昔者辱与户部游，而伯氏文惠公奉使淮东时，筑亭结楼于官舍，公为赋两诗，「酒盏摇江，波吞翠璧」之句，至今讽咏在口，辄藉以自怨，然甚惭。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1256778_comment'></div>公自称曰华阳老人，集用是以名。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1256778_comment'></div>绍熙二年三月十六日序。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_19_1256778_comment'></div>焕章阁学士、宣奉大夫、提举隆兴府玉隆万寿宫、魏郡公洪迈撰。</div><div id='poem_sentence_20_1256778_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1191&endYear=1191')">1191年</a>　归鄱阳。向所种松蔚然成林，皆有干霄之势，有两园适居东西扁，西为西园，东为东园。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1191&endYear=1191')">1191年11月9日</a>　遣饶卒温青往信州，使兼程而进。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1191&endYear=1191')">1191年11月23日</a>　《万首唐人绝句》刻毕。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1191&endYear=1191')">1191年</a>　以宣奉当磨勘，又该覃霈。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1192&endYear=1192')">1192年3月</a>　上表进所编《万首唐人绝句》。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1192&endYear=1192')">1192年3月10日</a>　《容斋续笔》成，序之。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1192&endYear=1192')">1192年</a>　七十寿辰，辛弃疾有词相庆。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1192&endYear=1192')">1192年</a>　撰《能仁禅寺塔记》。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1192&endYear=1192')">1192年</a>　撰周麟之墓志，效坡公《富碑》之体。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1193&endYear=1193')">1193年1月</a>　为乡人李文中撰墓铭。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1193&endYear=1193')">1193年3月1日</a>　重华宫祗应耿柟到饶州宣谕，寿皇誉迈所编《唐诗绝句》曰：“选择甚精，备见博洽”。有赐甚厚。作谢上表。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1193&endYear=1193')">1193年3月1日</a>　又有《别奏劄子》，乞请摭圣谕中“博洽”两字，建博洽堂。<div id='poem_1256706' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1256706' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1256706?labeling=true' target='_blank'>进万首唐人绝句别奏劄子</a><span class='authorDate'>（1193年3月1日）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 南宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(28601, "南宋", "洪迈", "poem_title_1256706")'>洪迈</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1256706_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1256706'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1256706'>臣逖远威颜，忽焉六载。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1256706_comment'></div>念以么么之质，被蒙眷知，度越辈流，可为希世之遇，钧天梦断，无复可寻。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1256706_comment'></div>罢越还家，杜门屏迹，自去春投进唐诗，一伸奏牍之后，不敢妄以孤远姓名复尘渊几。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1256706_comment'></div>诚不自意，恩从天来，颛降使车，颁之珍赐，玉音褒谕，金宝烂然，荣光非常，道路骇瞩，盖自鄱阳有郡以来所未之见。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1256706_comment'></div>陛下脱屣北宫，遗物离人而立，于独予以驭，幸寥寥弗闻。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1256706_comment'></div>臣独何人，邈在千里之外，乃拜殊渥？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1256706_comment'></div>焚香望阙，尽室欢呼，捧玩之馀，感极以泣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1256706_comment'></div>已具表称谢外，复此手劄，少摅蝼蚁之诚。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1256706_comment'></div>臣窃不自揆，再有昧死之请。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1256706_comment'></div>向者蒙赐「野处」二大字，既已摹勒作碑，揭于小园，往来观瞻，无不稽首。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1256706_comment'></div>今祗戴恩华，巍巍卓异，思欲有以夸示无极，辄摭圣谕中「博洽」两字，建为一堂，妄意长夏之始；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1256706_comment'></div>殿阁馀凉，游戏翰墨之间。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1256706_comment'></div>敢乞怜臣区区之愚，贲以「博洽堂」三字，受言藏之，使子子孙孙朝暮瞻仰。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1256706_comment'></div>臣年过七十，无复他荣，痴庸有求，罪当万死。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1256706_comment'></div>伏惟圣慈曲垂宽贷。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1256706_comment'></div>引望黼扆，无翼以翔，不胜感恩恋德陨越激切之至。</div><div id='poem_sentence_15_1256706_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1193&endYear=1193')">1193年3月1日</a>　又有《奏耿柟不受书送劄子》。<div id='poem_1256707' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1256707' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1256707?labeling=true' target='_blank'>奏耿楠不受书送劄子</a><span class='authorDate'>（1193年3月1日）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 南宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(28601, "南宋", "洪迈", "poem_title_1256707")'>洪迈</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1256707_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1256707'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1256707'>臣兹勤使者远至，荣耀非常。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1256707_comment'></div>在于故事，当有薄礼，欲以银百两充书送，楮币百千犒从人，而耿楠再三退却，以为圣旨不许收接。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1256707_comment'></div>无以展区区下悃，臣不胜惶惧感戴之极，须至奏闻者。</div><div id='poem_sentence_2_1256707_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1193&endYear=1193')">1193年3月1日</a>　又有《谢南内奏状》，答谢圣恩。<div id='poem_1256708' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1256708' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1256708?labeling=true' target='_blank'>谢南内奏状</a><span class='authorDate'>（1193年3月1日）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 南宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(28601, "南宋", "洪迈", "poem_title_1256708")'>洪迈</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1256708_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1256708'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1256708'>右，臣伏蒙至尊寿皇圣帝圣恩，特降专使秉义郎、重华宫祗应耿楠，以三月一日至饶州，赍霍汝弼等白劄子，传圣旨宣谕，以臣向所进《唐诗绝句》，赐臣茶一百夸，清馥香一十贴，薰香二十贴，金器一百两，臣已即时出州城迎拜，还家望阙祗受讫。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1256708_comment'></div>上件异数，出自圣恩，臣无任感天荷圣激切屏营之至，谨录奏谢以闻。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1256708_comment'></div>谨奏。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1256708_comment'></div>绍熙四年三月日，焕章阁学士、宣奉大夫、提举隆兴府玉隆万寿宫、魏郡开国公、食邑二千五百户、食实封二百户臣洪迈状奏。</div><div id='poem_sentence_3_1256708_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1193&endYear=1193')">1193年</a>　为友人汪仲嘉撰《友恭堂记》。<div id='poem_1256829' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1256829' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1256829?labeling=true' target='_blank'>友恭堂记<span class='inlineComment2'>（绍熙四年八月）</span></a><span class='authorDate'>（1193年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 南宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(28601, "南宋", "洪迈", "poem_title_1256829")'>洪迈</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1256829_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1256829'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1256829'>友恭堂者，鄞江汪氏所立也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1256829_comment'></div>汪望于歙，宗家几十室而九，至于处鄞则由正奉公始大。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1256829_comment'></div>公用文学行谊表儒先，数随计偕，讫弗售。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1256829_comment'></div>晚以经授井邑，从之游户外屦满。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1256829_comment'></div>丰滀不施，天实开二子，联翩奋白屋，策高第。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1256829_comment'></div>念平生辛苦，每约老去归休，必同居，践昔贤风雨对床之乐，盖豫名其堂。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1256829_comment'></div>已而双立朝，讲读诸王邸。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1256829_comment'></div>高宗履位，少君以旧学擢郎天官，不幸早世。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1256829_comment'></div>长君独翱翔宦途，握乡部使者节，隮贰太府，称一代名卿。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1256829_comment'></div>用未渠究，不能媚合时宰，袖手家食历年多，遂得偿夙心，考卜西湖之上。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1256829_comment'></div>四子十孙，奉先志冞笃。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1256829_comment'></div>仲子尚书公入从出藩，单俸稍所赢，益屋且百间。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1256829_comment'></div>纠集群从，春秋伏腊，敬荣整爱，中外怡怡简简，迨女妇妾仆无一啧言。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1256829_comment'></div>家风翕清，四远羡唶，跂瞻斯堂，若挹蓬峤。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1256829_comment'></div>谓予托契同年，命之记。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1256829_comment'></div>顾年衰笔顿，思与愿横，而伻来自东，绪请至五六，终墨墨不可，乃即其实而书之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1256829_comment'></div>呜呼，人非父母不生活，由父母而降，亲莫兄弟如也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1256829_comment'></div>天生羽翼，分樊墙而尔汝之得乎！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1256829_comment'></div>弟弗念天显，不恭厥兄，兄不念鞠子哀，弗友于弟，圣人之戒如此。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1256829_comment'></div>田氏骨肉仓卒分，青天白日摧紫荆，上穹之应如此。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_19_1256829_comment'></div>彼颛己顾妻子，废忘天伦，直禽犊而冠耳。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_20_1256829_comment'></div>然则朝于是，夕于是，父基而子肯堂，为世准的，其有功于名教为何如哉！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_21_1256829_comment'></div>欧阳公美海陵许氏孝弟著于三世，以为凡过其园者，望其松竹，登其台榭，思其宗族，自一家而刑一乡，由一乡而推之无远迩，予谓斯堂则然。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_22_1256829_comment'></div>予与尚书公知闻阅岁四十九，投分为最厚，每一相逢，叹其日进乎道，特棋弈一事如寸弯强弓，与初时不少异，亦见其居心无竞，益足以章其盛德云。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_23_1256829_comment'></div>公名大猷，字仲嘉，未老即谢事，恩及诸房，今直敷文阁学士，而太府公赠少师。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_24_1256829_comment'></div>绍熙四年八月廿二日，焕章阁学士、宣奉大夫、提举隆兴府玉隆万寿宫、魏郡开国公、食邑二千五百户、食实封贰伯户鄱阳洪迈记。</div><div id='poem_sentence_25_1256829_comment'></div></div><div class='poemNote' id='poem_note_1256829'><span class='label'>按：</span>《四明续志》卷一一，咸丰四年刊本。<br /></div><div id='poem_note_1256829_comment'></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1193&endYear=1193')">1193年</a>　冬，有客从中都来，持所抄《班朝录》一编相示。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1193&endYear=1193')">1193年</a>　《夷坚辛志》二十卷成。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1193&endYear=1193')">1193年</a>　《夷坚壬志》二十卷成。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1194&endYear=1194')">1194年</a>　清明，饯别朱晞颜于野处。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1194&endYear=1194')">1194年</a>　夏，《夷坚癸志》成。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1194&endYear=1194')">1194年6月1日</a>　《夷坚支甲》成，序之。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1194&endYear=1194')">1194年7月</a>　宁宗即位，明堂礼成加恩。赵汝愚为右相。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1194&endYear=1194')">1194年9月</a>　杨简迁国子博士，迈有送行诗。作品：送杨简迁国子博士。<div id='poem_179666' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_179666' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/179666?labeling=true' target='_blank'>送杨简迁国子博士</a><span class='authorDate'>（1194年9月）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 南宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(28601, "南宋", "洪迈", "poem_title_179666")'>洪迈</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_179666_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_179666'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_179666'>杨君解墨绶，去作国子师。<div id='poem_sentence_0_179666_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_179666'>邑人十万户，遮道婴儿啼。<div id='poem_sentence_1_179666_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_179666'>曩岁天旱苦，赤地无馀遗。<div id='poem_sentence_2_179666_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_3_179666'>饥殍千百辈，上山争采薇。<div id='poem_sentence_3_179666_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_4_179666'>采薇有时尽，讵能救长饥。<div id='poem_sentence_4_179666_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_5_179666'>慨然顾自任，舍我将告谁。<div id='poem_sentence_5_179666_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_6_179666'>昧爽出厅事，日暮忘旋归。<div id='poem_sentence_6_179666_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_7_179666'>大家贮陈粟，出粜不敢迟。<div id='poem_sentence_7_179666_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_8_179666'>偷儿纷狗鼠，锄治如平时。<div id='poem_sentence_8_179666_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_9_179666'>一意摩手抚，如子得母慈。<div id='poem_sentence_9_179666_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_10_179666'>明年麰麦登，比屋无流移。<div id='poem_sentence_10_179666_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_11_179666'>史牒载循吏，于今亲见之。<div id='poem_sentence_11_179666_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_12_179666'>我亦受一廛，惜哉轻语离。<div id='poem_sentence_12_179666_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_13_179666'>桥山未迄役，酌饯疏酒卮。<div id='poem_sentence_13_179666_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_14_179666'>聊述路人颂，持作送君诗<span class='inlineComment2'>（《鄱阳县志》卷一九）</span>。<div id='poem_sentence_14_179666_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_15_179666'></div><div id='poem_sentence_15_179666_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1194&endYear=1194')">1194年</a>　作《上天竺寺讲碑》。<div id='poem_1256849' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1256849' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1256849?labeling=true' target='_blank'>上天竺讲寺碑</a><span class='authorDate'>（1194年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 南宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(28601, "南宋", "洪迈", "poem_title_1256849")'>洪迈</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1256849_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1256849'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1256849'>华藏世界，毗卢觉海，万亿河沙，诸佛菩萨，均以大慈能仁阐豁悲愿为出世导师，而随念融摄，从闻思修，使末劫有生，持戴瞻仰，如在其上者，惟观音大士为然。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1256849_comment'></div>自给孤灵山，胜身赡部，兜率、毗卢之宫，补怛、洛伽之谷，无量无垠，魔区鬼窟，未有不灵赫示化，畅宣正机，而放大光明，觉有缘众，接物利人，因病施药，直若家至户到者，惟钱塘天竺为然。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1256849_comment'></div>故其肇始于道翊师，示梦于钱忠懿，显祠于咸平，浮像于天圣，易十方于妙臻，还旧贯于元净，尘尘刹刹，久而愈昭。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1256849_comment'></div>于是有灵感美名之锡，当时宝光示现，浚发兆祥，绚烂隮升，上澈霄汉，湛然虚明，普照四天。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1256849_comment'></div>知制诰吕夏卿、龙图阁学士沈文通、宝文阁待制陈轩纪载于前，可覆视也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1256849_comment'></div>遭靖康孽火，鞠为灰烬。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1256849_comment'></div>蒿目浅智，意其复初为难。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1256849_comment'></div>人天护承，否极必泰。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1256849_comment'></div>大驾南巡，狩临是邦，绍开中兴，宁济方夏。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1256849_comment'></div>虽英谟雄烈，士业得以凭藉；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1256849_comment'></div>然窈冥沕穆，非菩萨焉依？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1256849_comment'></div>凡请雨谒晴，不嫌于屡，故六七十载，昭事愈饬。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1256849_comment'></div>传序三圣，年增岁加，锡銮和铃，荐往法驾。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1256849_comment'></div>捐内帑金币，俾建经、钟二楼，会法安僧之堂、罗汉之阁、水陆之宇，视所应为，次第崇立。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1256849_comment'></div>孝宗创于西北隅，启十六观，赐之玉缶觚彝，珠宫金相，宝冠缨络，价值数十万缗，亲制赞文，特书两扁，终之以法输宝藏。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1256849_comment'></div>圣安太上亦揭贲云章。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1256849_comment'></div>今皇帝又申永作天台教寺之旨，凡禅律贤首，慈恩异宗，毋得窥觎更易，然后学者知所蒙赖。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1256849_comment'></div>是教也，本于智者建化，以妙为宗，以如为体，以法华三昧为极致，以安养国土为依归，以止观为修證之要。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1256849_comment'></div>荡一切尘，以空为观；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1256849_comment'></div>立一切法，以假而观；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_19_1256849_comment'></div>究一切法性，以中而观。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_20_1256849_comment'></div>以五时八教判释如来，一代训典，讫于无生真谛，超最上乘。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_21_1256849_comment'></div>教海渊深，义天高远，业空缘废，理胜惑亡，等于太虚，无恶不断。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_22_1256849_comment'></div>厥令水精之域，圆满清净。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_23_1256849_comment'></div>其门庭烨如，其堂殿穹如，其观阁迥如，其厢庑邃如，群居以智导迷，人知选佛之场矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_24_1256849_comment'></div>先后住持者，曰惟日、曰若讷、曰师觉、曰妙圭，皆擢录教门，实称僧中龙象。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_25_1256849_comment'></div>圭遣信求记不置，既书之，而又系偈言。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_26_1256849_comment'></div>其词曰：</div><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_27_1256849'>北山镇钱塘，三竺分鼎峙。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_27_1256849_comment'></div>西峰居上头，气与下中异。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_28_1256849_comment'></div>南无观世音，的以何年至？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_29_1256849_comment'></div>至今无作相，在此犹在彼。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_30_1256849_comment'></div>虽自西徂东，而实未尝动。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_31_1256849_comment'></div>法门元不二，一一成菩提。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_32_1256849_comment'></div>应生无住心，了不滞空有。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_33_1256849_comment'></div>以我清净眼，普鉴阿耨尘。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_34_1256849_comment'></div>白日当空虚，岂复留纤翳？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_35_1256849_comment'></div>皇居尺有咫，天近圣泽弥。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_36_1256849_comment'></div>多罗莲花台，不与昔时似。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_37_1256849_comment'></div>高皇屈万乘，孝祖亲制文。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_38_1256849_comment'></div>玉觚宝瓶彝，冠珞粲珠琲。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_39_1256849_comment'></div>价值百千万，庄严不遗力。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_40_1256849_comment'></div>谁言佛土遥，小叩则小应。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_41_1256849_comment'></div>炎天六七月，要雨雨随注。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_42_1256849_comment'></div>乃至请晴霁，应念便护感。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_43_1256849_comment'></div>左右十六观，摄彼散乱心。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_44_1256849_comment'></div>天台妙教宗，永永传真谛。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_45_1256849_comment'></div>荡荡水精域，化乐侔天宫。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_46_1256849_comment'></div>太上及今皇，瞻敬更无极。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_47_1256849_comment'></div>咨汝白足士，思报君佛恩。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_48_1256849_comment'></div>善修成法身，一證一切證。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_49_1256849_comment'></div>譬如航巨海，龙骧驾高樯。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_50_1256849_comment'></div>无风送吹嘘，难拟彻彼岸。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_51_1256849_comment'></div>珍宝秘幽谷，虎豹严卫守。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_52_1256849_comment'></div>无人为我先，可到不可致。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_53_1256849_comment'></div>菩萨具方便，总持观十方。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_54_1256849_comment'></div>为巍大道场，誓愿遍应物。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_55_1256849_comment'></div>紫金光结聚，若非烟非云。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_56_1256849_comment'></div>阐宏慈悲心，为汝众生父。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_57_1256849_comment'></div>念今圣天子，与佛俱有缘。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_58_1256849_comment'></div>拈花世尊前，咸透第一义。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_59_1256849_comment'></div>求阐无尽藏，护国井福民。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_60_1256849_comment'></div>刹那弹指间，闻见悉成佛。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_61_1256849_comment'></div>惟日暨讷觉，于今妙圭师。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_62_1256849_comment'></div>稽首大士前，洗我绮语业。</div><div id='poem_sentence_63_1256849_comment'></div></div><div class='poemNote' id='poem_note_1256849'><span class='label'>按：</span>《杭州上天竺讲寺志》卷九，武林掌故丛编本。<br /></div><div id='poem_note_1256849_comment'></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1194&endYear=1194')">1194年</a>　友人王信囿山园成，属迈作《囿山园记》。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1195&endYear=1195')">1195年2月28日</a>　《夷坚支乙》成，序之。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1195&endYear=1195')">1195年2月</a>　作《李康时墓铭》。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1195&endYear=1195')">1195年9月</a>　朱子渊赴桂，经鄱阳，致石柏两屏于迈，有唱和诗。作品：和子渊石柏诗。<div id='poem_179600' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_179600' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/179600?labeling=true' target='_blank'>和朱子渊石柏诗</a><span class='authorDate'>（1195年9月）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 南宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(28601, "南宋", "洪迈", "poem_title_179600")'>洪迈</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'>七言律诗</div></div><div id='poem_title_179600_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_179600'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_179600'>海底灵根石效奇，山经地志不曾知。<div id='poem_sentence_0_179600_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_179600'>凝红幻出珠千颗，染紫装成玉一枝。<div id='poem_sentence_1_179600_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_179600'>鹤骨龙姿随质见，鸾栖凤宿与香宜。<div id='poem_sentence_2_179600_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_3_179600'>元戎高唱真难和，愧我年来笔力衰<span class='inlineComment2'>（《夷坚志·支景》卷二）</span>。<div id='poem_sentence_3_179600_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_4_179600'></div><div id='poem_sentence_4_179600_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1195&endYear=1195')">1195年9月15日</a>　作《高州石屏记》。<div id='poem_1256838' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1256838' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1256838?labeling=true' target='_blank'>高州石屏记</a><span class='authorDate'>（1195年9月15日）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 南宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(28601, "南宋", "洪迈", "poem_title_1256838")'>洪迈</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1256838_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1256838'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1256838'>高州茂名县，本唐潘州也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1256838_comment'></div>县界有黄尖岭，父老言昔有仙人姓潘，居此鍊丹，近十数年来，工人入山凿石，乃得树木屏于石中。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1256838_comment'></div>盖仙所遗丹剂堕地融结者，一层复一层，殆可揭取，但枝叶端正者百无一二。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1256838_comment'></div>民黄氏擅此山，外人欲采伐，则先以盐䌽与之，然后入山祀土神毕，徐徐施工。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1256838_comment'></div>朱子渊为桂帅，致两屏遗予。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1256838_comment'></div>老干扶疏，上挟云气，下临广漠，混然天成，略无斧凿一迹。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1256838_comment'></div>非若祁阳所产，藉人力磨治，故痕腭高下，失其自然也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1256838_comment'></div>又云海函万族，无所不有。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1256838_comment'></div>范石湖《虞衡志》尝载石柏，今方得一株，自海底石块上生，根株盘错，枝叶如画，其色紫，其根白，其质皆石也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1256838_comment'></div>天阴雨时，必有水珠在叶上枝间，亦有柏子，皆石脂凝结而成。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1256838_comment'></div>子渊赋诗云：「海物难穷造化奇，后凋惟有岁寒知。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1256838_comment'></div>谁将修月黄金斧，斲就凌霜紫玉枝。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1256838_comment'></div>直干渠容尘点涴，灵根偏与石相宜。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1256838_comment'></div>天然不假栽培力，肯逐春风盛与衰」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1256838_comment'></div>予和之云：「海底灵根石效奇，山经地志不曾知。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1256838_comment'></div>凝酥幻出珠千颗，染紫装成玉一枝。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1256838_comment'></div>鹤骨龙姿随质见，鸾栖凤宿与香宜。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1256838_comment'></div>元戎高唱真难和，愧我年来笔力衰」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1256838_comment'></div>又有石梅、石松，则未之见也。</div><div id='poem_sentence_18_1256838_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1195&endYear=1195')">1195年10月13日</a>　《夷坚支景》成，序之。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1195&endYear=1195')">1195年</a>　年过七十，法当致仕。以宁宗新立，未即请休，仍守玉隆。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1196&endYear=1196')">1196年3月19日</a>　《夷坚支丁》成，序之。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1196&endYear=1196')">1196年6月30日</a>　《容斋三笔》成，序之。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1196&endYear=1196')">1196年7月5日</a>　《夷坚支戊》成，序之。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1196&endYear=1196')">1196年10月14日</a>　序《黄御史集》。作品：黄御史集序。<div id='poem_1256780' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1256780' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1256780?labeling=true' target='_blank'>黄御史集序<span class='inlineComment2'>（庆元二年十月）</span></a><span class='authorDate'>（1196年10月14日）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 南宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(28601, "南宋", "洪迈", "poem_title_1256780")'>洪迈</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1256780_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1256780'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1256780'>词章关乎气运，于唐尤验云。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1256780_comment'></div>唐兴三百年，气运升降，其间而诗文因之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1256780_comment'></div>自晋阳举义，开馆宫西，以延文学，竟用词赋取士。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1256780_comment'></div>士以操觚显者无虑数百家，大都始沿江左<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_3_1256780", 1256780, "Clauses/10/Comments/0")'>颓习</span>，竞于絺绘，耽披靡而乏气骨。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1256780_comment'></div>伯玉奋然洗刷，沈、宋、燕、许，辈出振响。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1256780_comment'></div>以至贞元、长庆，经术大明，修古弥众。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1256780_comment'></div>于时墨儒<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_6_1256780", 1256780, "Clauses/19/Comments/0")'>词匠</span>所为诗若文，咸<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_6_1256780", 1256780, "Clauses/20/Comments/0")'>矩矱</span>自然，不以彫饰为工，相与<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_6_1256780", 1256780, "Clauses/22/Comments/0")'>赞翊</span>道真，赓飏鸿化。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1256780_comment'></div>斯为锵锵尔雅，故文盛于韩、柳、皇甫。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1256780_comment'></div>而其衰也，为孙樵，为刘蜕，为沈、颜。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1256780_comment'></div>诗盛于李、杜、刘、白，而其衰也，为郑谷，为罗隐，为杜荀鹤。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1256780_comment'></div>御史生最晚而独不然，其文赡蔚有典则，策扶教化，其诗清淳丰润，若与人对语，和气郁郁，有贞元、长庆风槩。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1256780_comment'></div>《祭陈林先辈》诸文，悲怆激越，交情之深，不以昼夜死生乱离契阔为间断。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1256780_comment'></div>《马嵬》、《馆娃》、《景阳》、《水殿》诸赋，<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_12_1256780", 1256780, "Clauses/47/Comments/0")'>雄新</span>隽永，使人读之废卷太息，如身生是时，目摄其故。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1256780_comment'></div>为文若是，其亦可贵已。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1256780_comment'></div>方登科时，适昭宗之季年，犹覆试殿廷，再中选然后得官。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1256780_comment'></div>未几而朱梁移国，因归闽不复西，故不志合于世。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1256780_comment'></div>夫讵知八九叶之后，得贤耳孙而平生作为文章遂获表见者！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1256780_comment'></div>邵州将锓板于郡斋，遣信谒序。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1256780_comment'></div>御史之从兄曰校书君璞者，名见集中，有《闽川名士传》及《雾居子》，予曩时尝叙之矣，故不辞而书。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1256780_comment'></div>御史讳滔，字文江，繇四门博士至里行、监察。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_19_1256780_comment'></div>考功讳公度，邵州名沃。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_20_1256780_comment'></div>庆元二年十月十四日，焕章阁学士、宣奉大夫、提举隆兴府玉隆万寿宫、魏郡公鄱阳洪迈序。</div><div id='poem_sentence_21_1256780_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1196&endYear=1196')">1196年10月15日</a>　序友人黄公度《莆阳知稼翁集》。作品：莆阳知稼翁集序。<div id='poem_1256781' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1256781' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1256781?labeling=true' target='_blank'>知稼翁集序<span class='inlineComment2'>（庆元二年十月）</span></a><span class='authorDate'>（1196年10月15日）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 南宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(28601, "南宋", "洪迈", "poem_title_1256781")'>洪迈</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1256781_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1256781'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1256781'>高宗一马化龙，讫于巽位，自丁未至壬午三十六年间，策进士数千计，擢居大龙甲者十有一人。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1256781_comment'></div>科名巍峨，副以属望，视富贵岐辙若长风挂席，一息万里。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1256781_comment'></div>于是文靖梁公至宰相，景明陈公冠枢极，位尚书者三，汪圣锡、刘文孺、王宣子也，它侍从者五，李顺之、张子韶、赵庄叔、张安国、王龟龄也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1256781_comment'></div>惟莆田黄公师宪名声最卓卓，而财至尚书郎，寿不满半百。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1256781_comment'></div>梦幻覆手，天歼此良，大车云徂，出门折轴，人到于今伤之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1256781_comment'></div>爰初登第，以行卷忤秦相，君旋为赵忠简公礼接，益衔之弗舍，坎𡒄摧揠，无复有为天下惜人材之意。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1256781_comment'></div>一旦遇主，则死及之，呜呼！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1256781_comment'></div>公既以词赋压英躔，故于诗尤精，大氐铿锵蹈厉，发越沈郁，精深而不浮于巧，平澹而不近俗，与强名作诗者直相千万。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1256781_comment'></div>风樯阵马，不足呈其勇；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1256781_comment'></div>犀渠鹤膝，不足侔其珍。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1256781_comment'></div>悲秋之句曰：「迢迢别浦帆双去，漠漠平芜天四垂。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1256781_comment'></div>雨意欲晴山鸟乐，寒声初到井梧知」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1256781_comment'></div>吾不知谪仙、少陵以还，大历十才子尚能窥其藩否？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1256781_comment'></div>公既没，其嗣子邵州君沃收拾手泽，汇次为十有一卷，诗居大半焉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1256781_comment'></div>它文悉从肺府，源深流长。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1256781_comment'></div>迨乐府词章，宛转清丽，读者咀嚼于齿颊间而不能已。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1256781_comment'></div>惟其不沽于用，身不到銮坡凤阁中铺扬太平之闳休，其所表暴如是而已。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1256781_comment'></div>魏国陈丞相既序其首，而邵州又欲予赘语于后。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1256781_comment'></div>忆四十年前与公从容于番禺药洲之上，予作《素馨赋》，公盖戏而反之，异于不相知闻者，兹不宜辞。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1256781_comment'></div>若平生事业，则有参知政事龚公、吏部尚书林公之铭在。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_19_1256781_comment'></div>庆元二年十月庚申，焕章阁学士、宣奉大夫、提举隆兴府玉隆万寿宫、魏郡公鄱阳洪迈序。</div><div id='poem_sentence_20_1256781_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1196&endYear=1196')">1196年10月</a>　序黄滔所辑《泉山秀句集》。作品：泉山秀句集序。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1196&endYear=1196')">1196年10月</a>　序《闽川名士传》、《雾居子》。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1196&endYear=1196')">1196年11月</a>　《夷坚支己》成，序之。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1196&endYear=1196')">1196年12月8日</a>　友人王信卒，迈作墓志铭。作品：王信墓志铭。<div id='poem_1256851' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1256851' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1256851?labeling=true' target='_blank'>孺人陈氏墓志铭</a><span class='authorDate'>（1196年12月8日）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 南宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(28601, "南宋", "洪迈", "poem_title_1256851")'>洪迈</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1256851_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1256851'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1256851'>休宁于新安为县，于县有滕溪，于溪之人有陈氏，男尽为名人，女尽嫁策策知名士。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1256851_comment'></div>故同里程承事君讳畎，娶于陈，得今夫人。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1256851_comment'></div>夫人处士与之女也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1256851_comment'></div>自其幼时，实能起孝敬，事父母。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1256851_comment'></div>嫁，移诸舅姑。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1256851_comment'></div>舅没，姑亦老，夫人季于众妇，独身忠养之，调停节适，委曲至到。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1256851_comment'></div>二姒良以为弗如，姑亦曰季宜我程氏。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1256851_comment'></div>春多祠，正月率朔迨晦，夫人与鸡俱兴，湘濯亨孰必躬亲乃荐宾。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1256851_comment'></div>延师资整训诸子，拊卑承尊，礼法周备。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1256851_comment'></div>东西家时节相往还，人人意满去，无一退言有负己者。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1256851_comment'></div>异时用，缓急叩门，称力为之尽，不以前故芥蒂，于是闺门之称震，远近如一辞。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1256851_comment'></div>承事君申申安安，内得奇助，见其子大昌名进士，底闻成家。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1256851_comment'></div>承事君即世，夫人教馀子愈益力。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1256851_comment'></div>中女择对未决，大昌官太学，得婺士杨大法于诸生中，归以女，曰：「婿如是，何必嫁官人」？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1256851_comment'></div>未几杨优入舍选，将对策大廷，即除官，闻者證夫人贤有识。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1256851_comment'></div>大昌由学省入佐著作秘书，至驾部郎，直皇子庆王讲，夫人享恩封，安舆就养。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1256851_comment'></div>母汪在乡里年考高，辄再岁一归宁。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1256851_comment'></div>他日归，驾部拜乞留。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1256851_comment'></div>留少须臾而汪以病告，载星徂南，胗絮汤饵，浃日而永诀。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1256851_comment'></div>爵踊鹥弥，如孺儿之初去乳保，曰：「吾不蚤侍母，今舍我，吾生复何憀」？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_19_1256851_comment'></div>时春秋六十有二矣，法不致毁，竟以病。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_20_1256851_comment'></div>病且笃，子妇蕲食肉辅病，牢不可。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_21_1256851_comment'></div>气息惙然，逮于不能，病遂以卒，隆兴之元年十一月二十有六日也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_22_1256851_comment'></div>凡六男子，驾部君最长，次淑昌，全昌，世昌，道昌，其最少曰文昌，亦以材为博士弟子。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_23_1256851_comment'></div>大女适朱庸，季适吴辉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_24_1256851_comment'></div>夫人氏之丧，驾部谒急，府王釐尚方珍锡以赙，为观瞻者荣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_25_1256851_comment'></div>驾部吁哀痛中，卜宅兆未得。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_26_1256851_comment'></div>去年之秋，异人感于宵梦，褐衣长髯，自云皇父氏，来告曰：「有竁直艮，在朱之原，山川翚翔，后其炽蕃，而庀而役，冬当获旃」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_27_1256851_comment'></div>觉而谇于墓师物其地，地与梦协，将以祥之明日大葬。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_28_1256851_comment'></div>驾部君哀未尽，能自割以礼，使来请铭曰：「吾母亡矣，而有不亡者寿，能寿吾母者子也」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_29_1256851_comment'></div>予与君知闻十五年，久同僚于三馆，为甚厚，铭何说以辞？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_30_1256851_comment'></div>其词曰：</div><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_31_1256851'>孝敬其身之，本诸赜也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_31_1256851_comment'></div>乡闾我仪之，善斯则也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_32_1256851_comment'></div>有子实昌之，天报格也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_33_1256851_comment'></div>耄龄不崇之，寿胡啬也！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_34_1256851_comment'></div>卜宅谁朕之？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_35_1256851_comment'></div>神告啧也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_36_1256851_comment'></div>矢诗以飏之，诏于㗲也。</div><div id='poem_sentence_37_1256851_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1196&endYear=1196')">1196年</a>　《夷坚支庚》成，序之。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1196&endYear=1196')">1196年</a>　冬，长子携家寓居福州大中寺，以俟解印。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1196&endYear=1196')">1196年</a>　侄孙偲在长兴得张天觉与章子厚之子致平帖墨本，记之《随笔》。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1196&endYear=1196')">1196年</a>　邵州守黄沃叔启买得一钮汉寿亭侯印，为作《辨跋》。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1196&endYear=1196')">1196年</a>　为吏部侍郎万元亨作《南园记》。<br /></div>
-----end



-----title
金华
-----detail
<div class='label1' id='07ea4ae365b348ce8cc3900853faf7ee_label'><a href='javascript: DetailSwitch("07ea4ae365b348ce8cc3900853faf7ee");'><span id='07ea4ae365b348ce8cc3900853faf7ee_link' href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1184&endYear=1184')">1184年</a>　春，起知婺州，周必大有《回婺州洪舍人迈启》。<br /><a href="javascript: /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1184&endYear=1184')">1184年4月</a>　迈在婺州尝治巡检馆客全璧一事。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1184&endYear=1184')">1184年</a>　夏，奏奖金华县丞江士龙。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1184&endYear=1184')">1184年11月3日</a>　请蠲中都储仓积欠米。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1184&endYear=1184')">1184年</a>　婺州八咏楼，在唐为观，洪迈请锡嘉字，赐额宝婺。<br /><a href="javascript: id='poem_179706' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_179706' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/179706?labeling=true' target='_blank'>满江红 立夏前一日借坡公韵</a><span -----title
镇江

-----title
当涂

<div class='label1' id='22ecd48a415443358f2646f7ffe389f8_label'><a href='javascript: DetailSwitch("22ecd48a415443358f2646f7ffe389f8");'><span id='22ecd48a415443358f2646f7ffe389f8_link'
