href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1188&endYear=1188')">1188年9月17日</a>　改除知太平州。有《谢除知太平州表》、《当涂谢执政书》。作品：谢除知太平州表。当涂谢执政书。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1188&endYear=1188')">1188年10月23日</a>　跋《西塞渔社图》。作品：西塞渔社图跋。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1188&endYear=1188')">1188年12月</a>　孝宗书“野处”二字赐迈。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1188&endYear=1188')">1188年</a>　有《见闻事实》。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1189&endYear=1189')">1189年</a>　春，作《洞斋记》。<div id='poem_1256835' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1256835' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1256835?labeling=true' target='_blank'>洞斋记</a><span class='authorDate'>（1189年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 南宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(28601, "南宋", "洪迈", "poem_title_1256835")'>洪迈</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1256835_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1256835'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1256835'>姑熟郡治东偏有屋三间，衡三十尺，从丈九，暧昧苟简，不与风日接。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1256835_comment'></div>前守张几仲小为致葺，访后圃竹亭净香废扁表出之，而种竹百个。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1256835_comment'></div>既其实，于今三年，竟亦不能佳也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1256835_comment'></div>屋日朽，竹日悴。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1256835_comment'></div>正面棚苇深且低，巧为鄣翳，翻书燕坐，未晡时已思秉烛。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1256835_comment'></div>脱阴雨，愦愦无所见，用繄为累。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1256835_comment'></div>故虽跬步堂奥，而至则倦厌，或不暇御茗碗辄起。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1256835_comment'></div>予惜焉，即日革前楹屋而瓦之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1256835_comment'></div>凡室中之故，若牖若壁，尽撤弃弗用。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1256835_comment'></div>为八窗四户，槛其旁以高召明，延晨曦而纳凉飔。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1256835_comment'></div>穿门庭右，客至可通车马，地不改辟而轩豁献状。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1256835_comment'></div>顾旧名不称，使复初，而命此曰「洞斋」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1256835_comment'></div>世指神仙所宅曰洞府，山川之胜处曰洞天、洞渊，高门绮疏邃而廊者曰洞房、洞户，是皆不可拟。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1256835_comment'></div>至此中空洞无物，足容君辈数百人。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1256835_comment'></div>如周伯仁之肆言，吾又不敢。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1256835_comment'></div>今之目吾斋，特有取于「四达皇皇明白洞彻」之意云。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1256835_comment'></div>就赋诗曰：</div><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_16_1256835'>佳眠起清坐，目送孤飞云。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1256835_comment'></div>婆娑此室中，浥浥炉烟芬。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1256835_comment'></div>鬓边霜千丈，羞说翰墨勋。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1256835_comment'></div>桃李春未了，明妆罗缟裙。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_19_1256835_comment'></div>庭竹虽不多，照屏友墨君。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_20_1256835_comment'></div>俗尘斲已尽，底用成风斤。</div><div id='poem_sentence_21_1256835_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1189&endYear=1189')">1189年闰5月</a>　以久旱祷雨于广德之张王庙，得雨，撰《灵济应祷记》。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1189&endYear=1189')">1189年</a>　夏，范朝散秩满归朝，迈送有诗。作品：送通判范朝散秩满归朝。<div id='poem_179606' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_179606' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/179606?labeling=true' target='_blank'>送通判范朝散秩满造朝<span style='margin: 0 0.5em'> 其一 </span></a><span class='authorDate'>（1189年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 南宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(28601, "南宋", "洪迈", "poem_title_179606")'>洪迈</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'>五言律诗</div></div><div id='poem_title_179606_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_179606'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_179606'>打鼓发姑孰，送君朝帝乡。<div id='poem_sentence_0_179606_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_179606'>风流夸半刺，耆旧忆襄阳。<div id='poem_sentence_1_179606_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_179606'>别酒不成醉，征途能底忙。<div id='poem_sentence_2_179606_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_3_179606'>只应旗脚转，趁此麦天凉。<div id='poem_sentence_3_179606_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_4_179606'></div><div id='poem_sentence_4_179606_comment'></div></div></div><div id='poem_179607' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_179607' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/179607?labeling=true' target='_blank'><span style='margin: 0 0.5em'> 其二 </span></a><span class='authorDate'>（1189年）</span><br /><div class='titleIndent'>五言律诗</div></div><div id='poem_title_179607_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_179607'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_179607'>我欲菟裘老，推排强典州。<div id='poem_sentence_0_179607_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_179607'>同官有才俊，坐啸得遨游。<div id='poem_sentence_1_179607_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_179607'>便作烟霄去，知难郡县留。<div id='poem_sentence_2_179607_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_3_179607'>画船看不见，江水自东流<span class='inlineComment2'>（同上书卷一二）</span>。<div id='poem_sentence_3_179607_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_4_179607'></div><div id='poem_sentence_4_179607_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1189&endYear=1189')">1189年8月</a>　州生异麻，数本同干，作《瑞麻赞》，刻于石。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1189&endYear=1189')">1189年12月</a>　得东坡诗文十篇真迹，刻石郡斋。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1189&endYear=1189')">1189年</a>　太平郡圃建午桥庄，有记。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1189&endYear=1189')">1189年</a>　秘阁修撰平江郡守赵彦操即六经阁旧址建御书阁，驰书当涂，请迈识本末，因撰平江府学《御书阁记》。<div id='poem_1256832' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1256832' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1256832?labeling=true' target='_blank'>御书阁记</a><span class='authorDate'>（1189年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 南宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(28601, "南宋", "洪迈", "poem_title_1256832")'>洪迈</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1256832_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1256832'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1256832'>若稽古高宗皇帝，实天生德，既以聪明圣武，戡济多难，垂中兴亿年之基。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1256832_comment'></div>洎保大定功，投戈息马于世纷万殊，泊乎无一嗜玩，唯翰墨梱域，天纵神与，特致志颛心，不舍食息。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1256832_comment'></div>渊妙沉著，顾韦诞、钟繇。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1256832_comment'></div>所擅正书中取威定霸，高处视古无上，帝中第一，殆隘么不足言，羲、献、诸庾，固已望洋歛避，矧唐欧、虞、褚、薛辈，直可舆台命也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1256832_comment'></div>《诗》、《书》、《易》《、春秋》、《孝经》、《论语》、孟轲氏，凡几书，书凡几帙，帙凡几字，一一肆笔而成。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1256832_comment'></div>翥凤翔鸾，震荡辉赫，端正严重，肃如神明。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1256832_comment'></div>当是时，每终一经，辄诏玉册官摹刻，编以石本，侈锡方夏光天之内，盖郡载其书。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1256832_comment'></div>昔人谓万世之下一遇大圣而知其解者，是为旦暮之遇，况乎亲见帝王以为之师，恩斯勤斯，士宜如何报也？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1256832_comment'></div>妥奉当在頖宫，苏为吴盛府，故有六经阁，燬于兵。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1256832_comment'></div>绍兴中，守臣宝文阁学士王㬇始改建学，室宇宏备，夸雄他邦，阁独未克立，而庋置石经于大成殿。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1256832_comment'></div>仍俭就寡，瓜华芗火之敬弗答弗涓，揆于祗瞻，殊甚不称。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1256832_comment'></div>寥寥向四纪，郡博士领诸生数有请，二千石亦数留意，然画不坚定，会其凡辄中止，更数十政，讫莫之能为。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1256832_comment'></div>淳熙十四年，秘阁修撰赵彦操至，平易中和，敏絜莅业，用善政得民。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1256832_comment'></div>苏比比多事，且去天咫尺，南北问途者衔舟接轴。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1256832_comment'></div>冗丛厥身，居东道主，第知承迎过客，趣了停传为先务，朴遬马上，戴星而入，民瘼不暇问，尚安以教化劝功为哉？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1256832_comment'></div>彦操才旬月久，非能滋民使多，浚财使丰，辟土使广，而千里一旦廊廊如仙晨道院，于是以一阁之任自予。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1256832_comment'></div>即旧址度为三楹两翼，三其檐为高六十尺，为广七十有五尺。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1256832_comment'></div>材木以壮买，瓦石以硕市，工以募来，发公帑赢储千万给费，相以餐钱二十之一，毫釐之须，于我何取！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1256832_comment'></div>虑卜于素，五县乃不知。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1256832_comment'></div>去年秋七月壬戌命日，今年春二月丁卯成。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_19_1256832_comment'></div>一区之宫，若飞从天外，行人骇观，凝立如植。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_20_1256832_comment'></div>彦操写其制以告当涂守迈，使识本末。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_21_1256832_comment'></div>臣恭维西箱清穆敞閒之处，至尊寿皇圣帝奉先追孝，方勒崇焕章，建官列职，燕迪宸奎之昭回，上模紫清，一时臣子，宜有以效尺寸。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_22_1256832_comment'></div>彦操羽仪宗支，尝典正京邑，参侍从，兹息偃辅藩，首能扩尊君亲上，然后兴学之谊，鸠此巨役，章天显休，佥谓当刊表乐石，以志不朽。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_23_1256832_comment'></div>其词曰：</div><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_24_1256832'>故吴所都，上直斗牛。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_24_1256832_comment'></div>今为畿辅，气压百州。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_25_1256832_comment'></div>沉沉学宫，鼎以杰阁。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_26_1256832_comment'></div>烂其天光，照我海岳。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_27_1256832_comment'></div>倬哉高皇，肆笔成书。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_28_1256832_comment'></div>石经百卷，方国是储。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_29_1256832_comment'></div>岧峣干云，翚若有造。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_30_1256832_comment'></div>谁其尸之？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_31_1256832_comment'></div>臣曰彦操。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_32_1256832_comment'></div>洞庭之山，具区五湖。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_33_1256832_comment'></div>龙螭万数，右翼左趋。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_34_1256832_comment'></div>惟尔有神，实主张是。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_35_1256832_comment'></div>时即来朝，敬千万祀。</div><div id='poem_sentence_36_1256832_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1189&endYear=1189')">1189年</a>　《夷坚庚志》二十卷成。<br /></div>
-----end



-----title
绍兴
-----detail
<div class='label1' id='849df3af841d4d598b0ef4d2c722a77d_label'><a href='javascript: DetailSwitch("849df3af841d4d598b0ef4d2c722a77d");'><span id='849df3af841d4d598b0ef4d2c722a77d_link' class='switch'>—</span></a><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1190&endYear=1190')">1190年</a>，68岁</div><div id='849df3af841d4d598b0ef4d2c722a77d' class='detail'><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1190&endYear=1190')">1190年2月</a>　进焕章阁学士，依前宣奉大夫知绍兴府，有《知绍兴府谢上表》。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1190&endYear=1190')">1190年</a>　自当涂徙会稽，过阙奏事，言新政宜以“十渐”为戒。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1190&endYear=1190')">1190年</a>　及到官，建棣萼堂于府廨，以伯兄洪适尝守越取纶告中语名之。又建晚对阁。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1190&endYear=1190')">1190年</a>　定均敷和买之法上之，即《会稽和买事宜录》，诏依所措置推行。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1190&endYear=1190')">1190年11月8日</a>　刻《万首唐人绝句》于蓬莱阁，序之。<br /></div>
-----end
